            "content": "<h2><b>In-App Purchase内购</b><br/></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d2661f00a43e4b2aefe4c793064abe68_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"296\" data-rawheight=\"597\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"296\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;296&#39; height=&#39;597&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"296\" data-rawheight=\"597\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"296\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d2661f00a43e4b2aefe4c793064abe68_b.png\"/></figure>In-App Purchase enables people to\nsecurely pay for digital products through a custom store contained within your\napp. Apps often use In-App Purchase to let people add premium features,\nsubscribe to recurring content, and purchase virtual items, such as a new level\nor a weapon in a game.</p><p>app内购使人们能够通过app内的自定义商店安全地支付数字产品。 APP通常使用内购让人们添加高级功能，订阅定期内容，以及购买虚拟物品，比如游戏中的新级别或武器。</p><p><strong>TIP</strong>It’s\nimportant to understand the difference between In-App Purchase and Apple Pay.\nUse In-App Purchase to sell virtual goods, such as premium content for your\napp, and subscriptions for digital content. Use Apple Pay to sell physical\ngoods such as groceries, clothing, and appliances. Also use Apple Pay for\nservices such as club memberships, hotel reservations, and tickets for events.\nSee <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/technologies/apple-pay/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple\nPay</a>.</p><p>TIPIt了解应用内购和Apple Pay之间的区别非常重要。 用app内购销售虚拟商品，如app的优质内容和数字内容的订阅。 用Apple Pay出售杂货，服装和家电等实物商品。 还可以用Apple Pay为俱乐部会员，酒店预订和活动门票等服务。 请参阅Apple Pay。</p><p><strong>Design an integrated shopping\nexperience.</strong> People\nshouldn’t think they’ve entered a different app when they use your store.\nPresent products and handle transactions in a way that feels at home in your\napp.</p><p>设计一体化的购物体验。 人们不应该认为他们在使用您的商店时进入了不同的app。 在APP中展示产品并且用宾至如归的方式处理交易体验。</p><p><strong>Use simple, succinct product names\nand descriptions.</strong> It’s best\nwhen people can scan a set of products quickly and find the ones they’re\ninterested in. Use plain, direct language and titles that don’t truncate or\nwrap.</p><p>使用简单简洁的产品名称和描述。最好人们能快速浏览产品并找到他们感兴趣的东西。用不会被截短或遮挡的直白的语言和标题</p><p><strong>Use\nthe default confirmation alert.</strong> When someone initiates an in-app purchase, the system displays a\nconfirmation alert to avoid accidental purchases. Don’t attempt to modify this\nalert.</p><p>用默认的确认警报。当某人启动了一个内购，系统就显示一个确认警报以避免意外购买。不要试图修改该警告。</p><p>Note\nthat In-App Purchase collects payment for products you’ve registered with the\nApp Store, but your app must implement any functionality needed to actually\npresent a store, unlock features, or download content. For business guidelines\nand implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/in-app-purchase/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">In-App\nPurchase for Developers</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/NetworkingInternet/Conceptual/StoreKitGuide/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">In-App\nPurchase Programming Guide</a>. For detailed information about\nwhat you can and can’t sell in your app, as well as In-App Purchase usage\nrequirements and restrictions, see your<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/terms/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Developer Program license\nagreement</a>.</p><p>请注意，应用内购买会收集您在App Store注册的产品的付款，但您的应用必须实现实际展示商店，解锁功能或下载内容所需的任何功能。商业指南和使用详情请查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/in-app-purchase/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">In-App Purchase for Developers</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/NetworkingInternet/Conceptual/StoreKitGuide/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">In-App\nPurchase Programming Guide</a>】，APP中可以以及不可以售卖物品的详情，以及内购使用要求和限制，请查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/terms/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Developer Program license\nagreement</a>.】</p><h2><b>Live Photos</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-96e86307cc1355bddcbad702659a4c6e_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"266\" data-rawheight=\"276\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"266\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;266&#39; height=&#39;276&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"266\" data-rawheight=\"276\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"266\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-96e86307cc1355bddcbad702659a4c6e_b.png\"/></figure><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a25673f32589de03f0662b341ed19ca6_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"269\" data-rawheight=\"276\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"269\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;269&#39; height=&#39;276&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"269\" data-rawheight=\"276\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"269\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-a25673f32589de03f0662b341ed19ca6_b.png\"/></figure>Live Photos capture favorite memories\nin a sound- and motion-rich interactive experience that adds vitality to traditional\nstill photos. With this feature enabled, the Camera app captures additional\ncontent—including audio and extra frames before and after the photo is taken.\nSimply press a Live Photo to see it spring to life.</p><p>Live Photos 用声音动作并茂的交互抓住珍爱的记忆，为传统的静态照片增条活力。开启这个功能之后，照相机app拍摄包含音频和照片拍摄前后几帧的附加内容。只要点按Live\nPhoto就能看到它又鲜活起来。</p><p><b>Display\nLive Photos as traditional photos in environments that don’t support Live\nPhotos.</b> Don’t attempt to replicate the Live Photos\nexperience provided in a supported environment. Instead, show a traditional,\nstill representation of the photo.</p><p>在不支持Live Photos的环境中，将Live Photo显示为传统照片。不要尝试复制受支持环境中提供的Live Photos体验。相反，显示传统的静态照片。</p><p><b>Make Live Photos easily distinguishable from still\nphotos.</b> The\nbest way to identify a Live Photo is through a hint of movement. Note that\nthere are no built-in Live Photo motion effects, like the one that occurs as\nyou swipe through photos in the full-screen browser of Photos app. Any motion\neffects like this must be custom designed and implemented. In cases where movement\nisn’t possible, show a system-provided badge above the photo. This badge can be\ndisplayed as an overlay with a shadow or as a solid color without a shadow. A\nbadge variant is also available for situations where a Live Photo appears as a\ntraditional photo. Never include a playback button that could be interpreted as\na video playback button.</p><p>使Live\nPhotos与静态照片轻松区分。 识别Live Photos的最佳方式是通过移动提示。 请注意，没有内置的实时照片动作效果，例如当您在照片应用的全屏浏览器中滑动照片时出现的效果。 任何像这样的运动效果必须自定义设计和实施。 如果无法移动，请在照片上方显示系统提供的徽章。 此徽章可以显示为带阴影的叠加层，也可以是不带阴影的纯色。 如果Live Photos作为传统照片显示，也可以使用徽章变体。 切勿包含可解释为视频播放按钮的播放按钮。</p><p><b>Keep badge placement consistent.</b> If\nyou show a badge, put it in the same location on every photo. Typically, a\nbadge looks best in a corner of a photo.</p><p>徽章位置要一致。如果您要显示徽章，将它放在每张照片的同一位置。通常来说，徽章在照片的角上看起来最好。</p><p><b>Apply adjustments to all frames.</b> If\nyour app lets people apply effects or adjustments to a Live Photo, make sure\nthose changes are applied to the entire photo. If you don’t support this, give\npeople the option of converting it to a still photo.</p><p>为所有帧使用调整。如果app让人们对Live Photo使用效果或者调整，确保这些修改被用在了整个照片上。如果不支持这个功能，给人们转成静态照片的选项。</p><p><b>Keep Live Photo content intact.</b> It’s\nimportant for people to experience Live Photos in a consistent way that uses\nthe same visual treatment and interaction model across all apps. Don’t\ndisassemble a Live Photo and present its frames or audio separately.</p><p>保持Live\nPhoto内容完整。对人们来说，在所有app中使用一样的视觉待遇和交互模式，用一致的方式体验Live\nPhotos，是很重要的。不要分解Live\nPhoto并分别显示画面和音频。</p><p><b>Implement a great photo sharing experience.</b> If\nyour app supports photo sharing, let users preview the entire contents of Live\nPhotos before deciding to share. Always offer the option to share Live Photos\nas traditional photos.</p><p>实现优秀的照片分享体验。如果app支持照片分享，让用户在决定分享之前预览Live Photos的所有内容。总是提供将Live Photos作为传统照片分享的选项。</p><p><b>Clearly indicate when a Live Photo is downloading and\nwhen the photo is playable.</b> Show a progress indicator during the\ndownload process and provide some indication when the download is complete.</p><p>当一张Live\nPhoto正在下载或可播放时，要明确提示。在下载期间显示进程指示符，在下载完成时提供一些提示。</p><p>Live\nPhoto support is available in iOS 9.1 and later. </p><h2><b>ResearchKit</b></h2><p>A research app lets people everywhere\nparticipate in important medical research studies. The ResearchKit framework\nprovides predesigned screens and transitions that make it easy to design and\nbuild an engaging custom research app. For implementation guidelines and other\ninformation, see<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//researchkit.org/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">researchkit.org</a>.</p><p>研究app使人们无处不在地参与重要的医学研究。\nResearchKit框架提供了预先设计的页面和转换，使其易于设计和构建一个引人入胜的定制研究应用程序。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//researchkit.org/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">researchkit.org</a>.】</p><p>These guidelines are\nfor informational purposes only and do not constitute legal advice. Contact an\nattorney to obtain advice with respect to the development of a research app and\nany applicable laws.</p><p>这些指南仅供参考，不构成法律意见。 联系律师，以获得有关研究app开发和任何适用法律的建议。</p><h3>Creating the Onboarding Experience</h3><p>When opening a research app for the\nfirst time, people encounter a series of screens that introduce them to the\nstudy, determine their eligibility to participate, request permission to\nproceed with the study, and, when appropriate, grant access to personal data.\nThese screens aren’t typically revisited once they’ve been completed, so\nclarity is essential.</p><p>当第一次打开研究app时，人们会遇到一系列页面，介绍他们参加研究，确定他们是否合格参与，请求许可继续研究，并在适当时授予访问个人数据。 这些页面通常在完成后通常不会重新访问，因此清晰度至关重要。</p><p><strong>Always display the onboarding\nscreens in the correct order.</strong></p><p><strong>总是用正确顺序显示引导页面</strong></p><h4><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f016e1ccc86d23566e7c62f612426a6d_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"72\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f016e1ccc86d23566e7c62f612426a6d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;553&#39; height=&#39;72&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"72\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f016e1ccc86d23566e7c62f612426a6d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-f016e1ccc86d23566e7c62f612426a6d_b.png\"/></figure>1.\nIntroduction介绍</h4><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a7d0ce9aa596832f573baa538e5485e4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"272\" data-rawheight=\"540\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"272\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;272&#39; height=&#39;540&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"272\" data-rawheight=\"540\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"272\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a7d0ce9aa596832f573baa538e5485e4_b.png\"/></figure>Provide an introduction that\ninforms and provides a call to action.</strong> Clearly describe the subject and purpose of your study. Also\nallow existing participants to quickly log in and continue an in-progress\nstudy.</p><p>提供通知并呼吁采取行动的介绍。 清楚地描述您的研究主题和目的。 也允许现有参与者快速登录并继续进行中的研究。</p><h4>2. Determine Eligibility确定资格    </h4><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bd64bdd4d20b5e33645091624e22da80_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"272\" data-rawheight=\"540\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"272\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;272&#39; height=&#39;540&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"272\" data-rawheight=\"540\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"272\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bd64bdd4d20b5e33645091624e22da80_b.png\"/></figure>Determine eligibility\nas soon as possible.</strong> People\ndon’t need to move on to the consent section if they’re not eligible for the\nstudy. Only present eligibility requirements that are necessary for your study.\nUse simple, straightforward language that describes the requirements, and make\nit easy to enter information.</p><p>尽快确定资格。如果人们对于人们不符合参与研究的资质，他们就不必继续到同意区域了。只在对于研究来说有必要时才显示资格要求。使用简单直接的语言描述要求，并使其易于输入信息。</p><h4>3. Get Informed Consent获得知情同意书</h4><p><strong>Make sure participants\nunderstand your study before you get their consent.</strong> ResearchKit helps you make the consent process concise and\nfriendly, while still allowing you to incorporate into the consent any legal\nrequirements or requirements set by an institutional review board or ethics\nreview board. Make sure that your app complies with the applicable App Store\nGuidelines, including the consent requirements. Typically, the consent section\nexplains how the study works, ensures that participants understand the study\nand their responsibilities, and gets the participant’s consent.</p><p>在获得参与者的同意书之前，确保他们理解您的研究。ResearchKit帮助您使同意过程简洁友好，同时允许您将任何法律要求或机构审查委员会或道德审查委员会设定的要求纳入同意书。确保APP遵守包含同意书要求的APP Store指南，通常来说，痛与区域解释研究如何进行，确保参与者理解研究以及他们的责任，并且获得参与者的同意。</p><p><strong> Break a long consent form into easily\ndigestible sections.</strong> Each\nsection can cover one aspect of the study, such as data gathering, data use,\npotential benefits, possible risks, time commitment, how to withdraw, and so\non. For each section, use simple, straightforward language to provide a\nhigh-level overview. If necessary, provide a more detailed explanation of the\nsection that participants can read by tapping a Learn More button. Participants\nshould be able to view the entire consent form before they agree to\nparticipate.</p><p>将冗长的同意书形式打散为简单易懂的几个区域。每个区域可以包含研究的某一方面，例如数据收集，数据使用，潜在利益，可能的风险，时间承诺，如何退出，诸如此类。对每一个区域，用简单直白的语言提供高度概括。必要的话，提供更详细解释区域，参与者可以通过点击Learn\nMore按钮阅读。参与者应该能在同意参与之前查看整个同意书。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-99c7ab926df22f1535bfdc719eae445d_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"226\" data-rawheight=\"454\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"226\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;226&#39; height=&#39;454&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"226\" data-rawheight=\"454\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"226\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-99c7ab926df22f1535bfdc719eae445d_b.png\"/></figure>If it makes sense, provide a quiz that tests the participant’s\nunderstanding.</b> You might do this for questions the participant\nwould otherwise be asked when obtaining consent in person.</p><p>如果有意义的话，提供测试参与者理解能力的小测试。您可能为了 获取同意书时参与者可能被亲自问到的问题来做这件事。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3c0b43052ba1947be3875b1267df7e5d_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"229\" data-rawheight=\"454\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"229\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;229&#39; height=&#39;454&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"229\" data-rawheight=\"454\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"229\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3c0b43052ba1947be3875b1267df7e5d_b.png\"/></figure><b>Get\nthe participant’s consent and, if appropriate, some contact information.</b> After agreeing to join the study, participants receive a\nconfirmation dialog, which should be followed by screens in which they provide\ntheir signature and contact details. Most research apps email participants a\nPDF version of the consent form for their records.</p><p>如果合适的话，获取参与者的同意书和一些联络信息。在同意参与研究之后，参与者收到一个确认对话，在他们提供签名和合同详情之后。大多数研究app会给参与者用邮件发PDF版本的同意书以供保存。</p><h4><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c3a914b54b6e1fa2238d284c1bc156c5_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"180\" data-rawheight=\"363\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"180\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;180&#39; height=&#39;363&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"180\" data-rawheight=\"363\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"180\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c3a914b54b6e1fa2238d284c1bc156c5_b.png\"/></figure>4. Request Permission to Access Data要求获取数据的许可</h4><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d515a4af8640a0679b38ec40f49d35b9_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"229\" data-rawheight=\"466\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"229\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;229&#39; height=&#39;466&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"229\" data-rawheight=\"466\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"229\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-d515a4af8640a0679b38ec40f49d35b9_b.png\"/></figure>Get permission to\naccess the participant’s device or data, and to send notifications.</strong> Clearly explain why your research app needs access to location,\nHealth, or other data, and don’t request access to data that isn’t critical to\nyour study. If your app requires it, also ask for permission to send\nnotifications to the participant’s device.</p><p>得到获取参与者设备或者信息以及发送通知的许可。解释清楚为什么研究app需要获取位置，健康APP或者其他数据，不要要求获取对您的研究不重要的数据。如果app需要，也要请求向参与者设备发送通知的许可。 </p><h3>Conducting Research进行研究</h3><p>To get input from participants, your\nstudy might use surveys, active tasks, or a combination of both. Depending on\nthe architecture of your study, participants may interact with each section\nmultiple times or only once.</p><p>为了从参与者那里获取输入，您的研究可能使用调研，活动任务或者两者结合。取决于研究的结构，参与者可能和每个区域多次交互或者只互动一次。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6807e083713528255f84b3f88f81af49_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"294\" data-rawheight=\"594\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"294\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;294&#39; height=&#39;594&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"294\" data-rawheight=\"594\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"294\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6807e083713528255f84b3f88f81af49_b.png\"/></figure>Create surveys that keep participants focused and\nengaged.</b> ResearchKit\nprovides many customizable screens you can use in your surveys, and makes it\neasy to present questions that require different types of answers, such as true\nor false, multiple choice, dates and times, sliding scales, and open-ended text\nentry. As you use ResearchKit screens to design a survey, follow these\nguidelines to provide a great experience:</p><p>创建让参与者集中注意力、吸引人的调研。ResearchKit提供很多自定义屏，您可以把他们用在调研中，并且让它易于表现要求多种回答的问题，比如是非题，多项选择，日期和时间，滑动刻度以及开放式文本输入。当您用ResearchKit屏设计调研时，遵循这些指南以提供优秀体验。</p><p>·       \nTell participants how many questions there\nare and about how long the survey will take.</p><p>·       \n告诉参与者有多少个问题以及调研要花多少时间。</p><p>·       \nUse one screen per question.</p><p>·       \n每个问题用一屏</p><p>·       \nShow participants their progress in the\nsurvey.</p><p>·       \n显示参与者的调研进程</p><p>·       \nKeep the survey as short as possible. Several\nshort surveys tend to work better than one long survey.</p><p>·       \n让调研尽量短。几个短调研可能比一个冗长的调研效果好。</p><p>·       \nFor questions that require some additional\nexplanation, use the standard font for the question and a slightly smaller font\nfor the explanatory text.</p><p>·       \n对于需要额外解释的问题，对问题使用标准字体，对解释文字用稍小一点的字体。</p><p>·       \nTell participants when the survey is\ncomplete.</p><p>·       \n当调研完成时告诉参与者。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-dff97ba1be35f34f384eea64f45f89aa_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"202\" data-rawheight=\"412\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"202\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;202&#39; height=&#39;412&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"202\" data-rawheight=\"412\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"202\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-dff97ba1be35f34f384eea64f45f89aa_b.png\"/></figure>Make active tasks easy\nto understand.</strong> An active\ntask requires the participant to engage in an activity, such as speaking into\nthe microphone, tapping fingers on the screen, walking, or performing a memory\ntest. Follow these guidelines to encourage participants to perform an active\ntask and give them the best chance of success:</p><p>让活动任务易于理解。活动任务需要参与者参与到活动中，比如对麦克风说话，在屏幕上点击，走动或者实行一个记忆力测试。遵循以下指南来鼓励参与者实行一个活动任务并给他们最好的成功机会？？？</p><p>·       \nDescribe how to perform the task using clear, simple language.</p><p>·       \n用清楚简单的语言来描述如何实施任务。</p><p>·       \nExplain any requirements, such as if the task must be performed\nat a particular time or under specific circumstances.</p><p>·       \n解释清楚要求，比如如果这个任务必须在特定时间或者在特定情境下实施。</p><p>·       \nMake sure participants can tell when the task is complete.</p><p>·       \n确认参与者能知道什么时候任务完成。</p><h3>Managing Personal Information and Providing Encouragement管理个人信息以及提供鼓励</h3><p>ResearchKit offers a profile screen you\ncan use to let participants manage personal information while they’re in your research\napp. It’s also a good idea to design a custom screen that motivates people and\ngives them a way to track progress in the study. Ideally, both screens should\nbe accessible at any time in your app.</p><p>ResearchKit提供一个档案屏，您可以用它来让参与者在您的研究app中管理个人信息。设计自定义屏来激励人们，给他们一个追踪研究进程的方法也是一个好主意。理想状况下，在您的app中这两屏应该能随时访问。。</p><p><b>Use a\nprofile to help participants manage personal data related to your study.</b> A profile screen can let people edit data that might change during\nthe course of the study—such as weight or sleep habits—and remind them of\nupcoming activities. A profile screen can also provide an easy way to leave a\nstudy and view important information, such as the consent document and privacy\npolicy.</p><p>使用档案帮助参与者管理与您的研究相关的个人数据。 档案屏能让人们编辑在研究过程中可能改变的数据，例如体重或睡眠习惯，并提醒他们即将到来的活动。 档案屏还可以提供一个简单的方式来离开研究和查看重要信息，如同意文档和隐私政策。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ee48f51c331057c00797595a5b02fc2c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"231\" data-rawheight=\"468\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"231\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;231&#39; height=&#39;468&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"231\" data-rawheight=\"468\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"231\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ee48f51c331057c00797595a5b02fc2c_b.png\"/></figure>Use a dashboard to show progress and motivate participants to continue.</b> If appropriate for your study, use a dashboard to provide\nencouraging feedback, such as daily progress, weekly assessments, results from\nspecific activities, and even results that compare the participant’s results\nwith aggregated results from others in the study.</p><p>用图表显示进程并且激励参与者继续。如果对您的研究合适的话，用图表来提供鼓舞人心的反馈，比如每天进程，每周测评，特定活动的结果，甚至是将参与者的结果与其他在研究中的参与者的局和结果相比较的结果。</p><h2><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-33aac9a6624a1902325e41dd6e8ab689_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"222\" data-rawheight=\"448\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"222\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;222&#39; height=&#39;448&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"222\" data-rawheight=\"448\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"222\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-33aac9a6624a1902325e41dd6e8ab689_b.png\"/></figure>Social Media社交媒体</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a5f28d8ffaf6c49948c9b918fc703f7b_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"288\" data-rawheight=\"594\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"288\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;288&#39; height=&#39;594&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"288\" data-rawheight=\"594\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"288\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a5f28d8ffaf6c49948c9b918fc703f7b_b.png\"/></figure>People expect to have quick access to\ntheir favorite social media accounts, regardless of the current context. iOS\nmakes it easy to integrate social media interactions into your app, including\nsharing content and displaying an activity feed.</p><p>人们期待能快速访问他们喜爱的社交媒体账户，无论当前情境是什么。iOS让在app中集成社交媒体互动变得更容易了，包括分享内容和显示活动反馈。</p><p><strong>Don&#39;t ask people to sign in.</strong> iOS employs a single sign-on model for accessing social media\naccounts, so you can get authorization to access an account without requiring\nauthentication. If the user isn’t signed into an account, you can display a\nsystem-provided interface that allows them to do so.</p><p>不要要求用户登录。iOS采用单点登录模式访问社交媒体帐户，因此您可以获得访问帐户的授权，而无需身份验证。 如果用户未登录到帐户，则可以显示系统提供的界面，让他们这样做。</p><p><strong>Make sharing easy.</strong> Many people enable share extensions that make it easy to post\ncontent from anywhere to their favorite social media services. These extensions\nare accessed by tapping a sharing button, usually in a toolbar, to display a\nlist of available services. Selecting a service then displays a composition\nview. Whenever possible, prepopulate this view with content before presenting\nit for editing. For example, a photo app could attach the active photo, a\ntravel app could add the current location, or a cooking app could insert a URL\nfor a favorite recipe.</p><p>让分享更容易。很多人开启分享扩展，这让从任何地方发布内容至他们喜爱的社交媒体服务很容易。通过点击分享按钮，通常在工具条上，可以获取这些扩展，来显示一些列可用服务。选择一项服务，然后显示合成视图。可能的话，在显示出编辑界面之前用内容预填充这个视图。例如，一个照片app可以附上动态照片，一个旅游app可以添加当前位置，或者一个烹饪app能插入一个收藏菜谱的URL。</p><p>For information about implementing\nsocial media interactions in your app, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/social\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Social</a>. To\nlearn about designing share extensions other apps can use to post content to\nyour social media service, see<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/sharing-and-actions\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Sharing and Actions</a>.</p><p>有关在您的应用中实施社交媒体互动的信息，请参阅【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/social\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Social</a>】。 要了解如何设计分享额外资讯，您可以使用其他应用程式将内容张贴到社交媒体服务，请参阅【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/sharing-and-actions\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Sharing and Actions</a>】。</p><h2><b>Wallet</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-be6ae08da5653a6ed1fb68eb2d343c82_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"294\" data-rawheight=\"603\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"294\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;294&#39; height=&#39;603&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"294\" data-rawheight=\"603\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"294\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-be6ae08da5653a6ed1fb68eb2d343c82_b.png\"/></figure>People use the Wallet app to view and\nmanage passes—digital representations of information that is otherwise printed\non small pieces of paper or plastic and kept in a physical wallet. Passes are\nused to take action in the real world, such as to board a plane, enter a venue,\nor receive a discount. Wallet also stores credit, debit, and store cards used\nby Apple Pay.</p><p>人们用Wallet app来查看和管理凭证——数码显示的，否则会印刷在一小片纸或塑料并被保存在物理钱包中的信息。凭证被用于真实世界的活动，比如登机，进入场地，或者或的折扣。Wallet也存储信用卡，借记卡，并存储用于Apple Pay的卡。</p><p>The PassKit framework makes it easy for\napps to access, create, distribute, and update passes. This framework\nimplements several templates, each of which defines the layout and fields for a\nspecific style of pass.</p><p>PassKit框架让app更容易访问，创建，发送和更新凭证。这个框架使用几个模板，每个模板为特定种类的凭证定义布局和区域。</p><p><b>Style</b></p><p><b>Uses</b></p><p><strong>Boarding pass</strong><strong>交通凭证</strong></p><p>火车票，飞机登机牌，以及其他种类的交通凭证。每个凭证对应一个特定</p><p>起点和重点的单程旅行。</p><p><strong>Coupons</strong><strong>券</strong></p><p>优惠券，特价以及其他打折。</p><p><strong>Event tickets</strong><strong>事件票</strong></p><p><br/>进入音乐会，电影，戏剧，运动赛事，或者其他事件。通常来说</p><p>每个凭证对应一个特定事件，但是您也可以为几个事件用一个凭证</p><p>比如季票。</p><p><strong>Store cards</strong><strong>商店卡</strong></p><p>商店贵宾卡，打折卡，点券卡，礼品卡。如果账户关联的商店卡有</p><p>余额，凭证通常显示当前余额。</p><p><strong>Generic pass</strong><strong>通用凭证</strong></p><p>任何其他类型的凭证，比如健身卡或者存包存大衣的凭证</p><p><strong>Design a pass that looks great on\nall devices.</strong> Be\nmindful that passes appear differently on different devices. For example, strip\nand thumbnail images aren’t displayed on Apple Watch. Don’t put essential\ninformation in elements that might be unavailable on certain devices. Note\nthat, even if you don’t create a watch-specific app, people can add your passes\nto their Apple Watch.</p><p>设计在所有设备上都看起来很棒的凭证。注意凭证在不同设备上看起来不一样。例如，条形图和缩略图不会显示在Apple\nWatch上。 不要将基本信息放在某些设备上可能无法使用的元素中。 请注意，即使您不创建手表专用app，人们可以将您的凭证添加到他们的Apple\nWatch。</p><p><strong>To the extent possible, avoid\nreproducing existing physical passes.</strong> Wallet matches the general design aesthetic of iOS to build\ntrust and familiarity. Instead of replicating the appearance of a physical\nitem, take this opportunity to design a clean, simple pass that follows the\nform and function of Wallet.</p><p>尽可能避免再现现有的物理凭证。 Wallet符合iOS的通用设计美学，建立信任和熟悉。 不要复制物理物品的外观，请借此机会设计一个遵循Wallet形式和功能的简洁凭证。</p><p><strong>Avoid using a plain white\nbackground.</strong> A pass\nlooks best when its background is a vivid, solid color or an image with strong,\nvibrant colors. As you design the background, make sure it doesn’t interfere\nwith the readability of the content.</p><p>避免使用纯白背景。当凭证背景是鲜艳的实心填充或者颜色强烈跳跃的图片时看起来最棒。当您设计背景时，确保背景不会干扰内容的可读性。</p><p><strong>Use pass fields to display text.</strong> Each pass style defines fields that give your pass a consistent\nlook and work with accessibility features. Avoid embedding text in images\nbecause not all images are displayed on all devices. Avoid using custom fonts\nthat make text difficult to read.</p><p>用凭证区域来显示文本。每个凭证样式定义的字段，使您的凭证一致的外观和使用辅助功能。 避免在图片中嵌入文字，因为并非所有图片都显示在所有设备上。 避免使用让文本难以阅读的自定义字体。</p><p><strong>Avoid using device-specific\nlanguage.</strong> You can’t\npredict the device people will use to view your pass, so don’t include language\nthat might not make sense on a particular device. For example, text that tells\npeople to “slide to view” content doesn’t make sense when it appears on Apple\nWatch.</p><p>避免使用特定于设备的语言。 您无法预测用户要查看凭证的设备，因此请勿包含在特定设备上可能没有意义的语言。 例如，告诉人们“滑动查看”内容的文本在Apple Watch上显示时没有意义。</p><p><strong>Be selective about the information\non the front of a pass.</strong> People\nexpect to glance at a pass and quickly get the information they need, so the\nfront of a pass should be uncluttered and easy to read. If there’s additional\ninformation you think people might need, put it on the back of the pass. Just\nbe aware that passes on Apple Watch don&#39;t include a back view.</p><p>仔细挑选凭证正面的信息。 人们期望看到一个凭证就能快速获得他们需要的信息，所以凭证正面应该整洁，容易阅读。 如果您认为人们可能需要额外的信息，把它放在凭证的背面。 只要注意，Apple Watch上的凭证不包括背面视图。</p><p><strong>Use the logo text field for your\ncompany name.</strong> Text in\nthis field is rendered in a consistent font on all passes. To avoid clashing\nwith other passes in Wallet, consider entering text here instead of using a\ncustom font.</p><p>为您的公司名称使用logo文本字段。 此字段中的文本在所有凭证中以一致的字体呈现。 为避免与Wallet中的其他凭证发生冲突，请考虑在此输入文字，而不要使用自定义字体。</p><p><strong>Update passes when appropriate.</strong> Even though physical passes don’t typically change, digital\npasses can be updated to reflect real-world events. An airline boarding pass,\nfor example, could be updated to reflect flight delays.</p><p>适当时更新凭证。 即使物理凭证通常不会改变，但是数字凭证是可以更新以反映真实世界的事件。 例如，航空公司登机牌可以更新以反映航班延误。</p><p><strong>Use a rectangular barcode when\npossible.</strong> A square\nbarcode creates empty gutters on both sides and can vertically crowd the fields\nabove and below it. Because of the layout of a pass, a rectangular barcode—such\nas a PDF417-style barcode—typically looks better.</p><p>尽可能使用矩形条形码。 正方形条形码在两侧创建空槽，并可以垂直地包围其上方和下方的字段。 由于凭证的布局，矩形条形码（例如PDF417样式的条形码）通常看起来更好。</p><p><strong>Optimize images for performance.</strong> People often receive passes via email or Safari. To make\ndownloads as fast as possible, use the smallest image files that still look\ngreat.</p><p>优化图像的性能。 人们经常通过电子邮件或Safari接收凭证。 为了尽可能快地下载，使用看起来很好的最小的图像文件。</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/PassKit_PG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Wallet Developer\nGuide</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/passkit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">PassKit</a>.</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/PassKit_PG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Wallet Developer\nGuide</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/passkit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">PassKit</a>.】</p><p>People use the Wallet app to view and\nmanage passes—digital representations of information that is otherwise printed\non small pieces of paper or plastic and kept in a physical wallet. Passes are\nused to take action in the real world, such as to board a plane, enter a venue,\nor receive a discount. Wallet also stores credit, debit, and store cards used\nby Apple Pay.</p><p>人们用Wallet app来查看和管理凭证——数码显示的，否则会印刷在一小片纸或塑料并被保存在物理钱包中的信息。凭证被用于真实世界的活动，比如登机，进入场地，或者或的折扣。Wallet也存储信用卡，借记卡，并存储用于Apple Pay的卡。</p><p>The PassKit framework makes it easy for\napps to access, create, distribute, and update passes. This framework\nimplements several templates, each of which defines the layout and fields for a\nspecific style of pass.</p><p>PassKit框架让app更容易访问，创建，发送和更新凭证。这个框架使用几个模板，每个模板为特定种类的凭证定义布局和区域。</p><p><b>Style</b></p><p><b>Uses</b></p><p><strong>Boarding pass</strong><strong>交通凭证</strong></p><p>火车票，飞机登机牌，以及其他种类的交通凭证。每个凭证对应一个特定</p><p>起点和重点的单程旅行。</p><p><strong>Coupons</strong><strong>券</strong></p><p>优惠券，特价以及其他打折。</p><p><strong>Event tickets</strong><strong>事件票</strong></p><p><br/>进入音乐会，电影，戏剧，运动赛事，或者其他事件。通常来说</p><p>每个凭证对应一个特定事件，但是您也可以为几个事件用一个凭证</p><p>比如季票。</p><p><strong>Store cards</strong><strong>商店卡</strong></p><p>商店贵宾卡，打折卡，点券卡，礼品卡。如果账户关联的商店卡有</p><p>余额，凭证通常显示当前余额。</p><p><strong>Generic pass</strong><strong>通用凭证</strong></p><p>任何其他类型的凭证，比如健身卡或者存包存大衣的凭证</p><p><strong>Design a pass that looks great on\nall devices.</strong> Be\nmindful that passes appear differently on different devices. For example, strip\nand thumbnail images aren’t displayed on Apple Watch. Don’t put essential\ninformation in elements that might be unavailable on certain devices. Note\nthat, even if you don’t create a watch-specific app, people can add your passes\nto their Apple Watch.</p><p>设计在所有设备上都看起来很棒的凭证。注意凭证在不同设备上看起来不一样。例如，条形图和缩略图不会显示在Apple\nWatch上。 不要将基本信息放在某些设备上可能无法使用的元素中。 请注意，即使您不创建手表专用app，人们可以将您的凭证添加到他们的Apple\nWatch。</p><p><strong>To the extent possible, avoid\nreproducing existing physical passes.</strong> Wallet matches the general design aesthetic of iOS to build\ntrust and familiarity. Instead of replicating the appearance of a physical\nitem, take this opportunity to design a clean, simple pass that follows the\nform and function of Wallet.</p><p>尽可能避免再现现有的物理凭证。 Wallet符合iOS的通用设计美学，建立信任和熟悉。 不要复制物理物品的外观，请借此机会设计一个遵循Wallet形式和功能的简洁凭证。</p><p><strong>Avoid using a plain white\nbackground.</strong> A pass\nlooks best when its background is a vivid, solid color or an image with strong,\nvibrant colors. As you design the background, make sure it doesn’t interfere\nwith the readability of the content.</p><p>避免使用纯白背景。当凭证背景是鲜艳的实心填充或者颜色强烈跳跃的图片时看起来最棒。当您设计背景时，确保背景不会干扰内容的可读性。</p><p><strong>Use pass fields to display text.</strong> Each pass style defines fields that give your pass a consistent\nlook and work with accessibility features. Avoid embedding text in images\nbecause not all images are displayed on all devices. Avoid using custom fonts\nthat make text difficult to read.</p><p>用凭证区域来显示文本。每个凭证样式定义的字段，使您的凭证一致的外观和使用辅助功能。 避免在图片中嵌入文字，因为并非所有图片都显示在所有设备上。 避免使用让文本难以阅读的自定义字体。</p><p><strong>Avoid using device-specific\nlanguage.</strong> You can’t\npredict the device people will use to view your pass, so don’t include language\nthat might not make sense on a particular device. For example, text that tells\npeople to “slide to view” content doesn’t make sense when it appears on Apple\nWatch.</p><p>避免使用特定于设备的语言。 您无法预测用户要查看凭证的设备，因此请勿包含在特定设备上可能没有意义的语言。 例如，告诉人们“滑动查看”内容的文本在Apple Watch上显示时没有意义。</p><p><strong>Be selective about the information\non the front of a pass.</strong> People\nexpect to glance at a pass and quickly get the information they need, so the\nfront of a pass should be uncluttered and easy to read. If there’s additional\ninformation you think people might need, put it on the back of the pass. Just\nbe aware that passes on Apple Watch don&#39;t include a back view.</p><p>仔细挑选凭证正面的信息。 人们期望看到一个凭证就能快速获得他们需要的信息，所以凭证正面应该整洁，容易阅读。 如果您认为人们可能需要额外的信息，把它放在凭证的背面。 只要注意，Apple Watch上的凭证不包括背面视图。</p><p><strong>Use the logo text field for your\ncompany name.</strong> Text in\nthis field is rendered in a consistent font on all passes. To avoid clashing\nwith other passes in Wallet, consider entering text here instead of using a\ncustom font.</p><p>为您的公司名称使用logo文本字段。 此字段中的文本在所有凭证中以一致的字体呈现。 为避免与Wallet中的其他凭证发生冲突，请考虑在此输入文字，而不要使用自定义字体。</p><p><strong>Update passes when appropriate.</strong> Even though physical passes don’t typically change, digital\npasses can be updated to reflect real-world events. An airline boarding pass,\nfor example, could be updated to reflect flight delays.</p><p>适当时更新凭证。 即使物理凭证通常不会改变，但是数字凭证是可以更新以反映真实世界的事件。 例如，航空公司登机牌可以更新以反映航班延误。</p><p><strong>Use a rectangular barcode when\npossible.</strong> A square\nbarcode creates empty gutters on both sides and can vertically crowd the fields\nabove and below it. Because of the layout of a pass, a rectangular barcode—such\nas a PDF417-style barcode—typically looks better.</p><p>尽可能使用矩形条形码。 正方形条形码在两侧创建空槽，并可以垂直地包围其上方和下方的字段。 由于凭证的布局，矩形条形码（例如PDF417样式的条形码）通常看起来更好。</p><p><strong>Optimize images for performance.</strong> People often receive passes via email or Safari. To make\ndownloads as fast as possible, use the smallest image files that still look\ngreat.</p><p>优化图像的性能。 人们经常通过电子邮件或Safari接收凭证。 为了尽可能快地下载，使用看起来很好的最小的图像文件。</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/PassKit_PG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Wallet Developer\nGuide</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/passkit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">PassKit</a>.</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/PassKit_PG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Wallet Developer\nGuide</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/passkit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">PassKit</a>.】</p>",
