            "title": "iOS10人机界面指南：技术（一）", 
            "content": "<h2><b>Apple Pay</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-aa4ecd4a5b9d19d189b6ed47fe6d9d9d_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"297\" data-rawheight=\"601\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"297\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;297&#39; height=&#39;601&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"297\" data-rawheight=\"601\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"297\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-aa4ecd4a5b9d19d189b6ed47fe6d9d9d_b.png\"/></figure>Apple Pay is a secure, private,\nhassle-free way to make payments for physical goods and services within iOS and\nwatchOS apps, and on websites. People use Touch ID to quickly and easily\nauthorize payments and provide shipping and contact information, using\ncredentials that are securely stored on the device.</p><p>Apple Pay是一种安全，私人，不麻烦的，在iOS和watchOSapp以及网站上支付实体商品和服务方式。人们使用Touch ID快速轻松地授权付款，并使用安全存储在设备上的凭据提供运输和联系信息。</p><p>The Apple Pay process is clear,\nstreamlined, and unobtrusive. Apps and websites indicate when they accept Apple\nPay. During checkout, a payment sheet shows the credit or debit card, purchase\namount (including tax and fees), and possibly shipping options and contact\ninformation. Users make any necessary adjustments to this information and then\nuse Touch ID to authorize payment and complete the purchase.</p><p>Apple Pay流程清晰，简洁，不引人注目。app和网站指示他们何时接受Apple Pay。在结帐时，付款单显示信用卡或借记卡，购买金额（包括税金和费用），以及可能的运输选项和联系信息。用户对此信息进行必要的调整，然后使用Touch ID授权付款并完成购买。</p><p>For design guidance that&#39;s specific to\nwebsites, see<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/apple-pay/web-human-interface-guidelines/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Pay on the Web\nHuman Interface Guidelines</a>.</p><p>网页设计指南详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/apple-pay/web-human-interface-guidelines/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Pay on the Web\nHuman Interface Guidelines</a>.】</p><p><strong>TIP</strong>It’s\nimportant to understand the difference between Apple Pay and In-App Purchase.\nUse Apple Pay in apps and on websites to sell physical goods such as groceries,\nclothing, and appliances, and for services such as club memberships, hotel\nreservations, and tickets for events. Use In-App Purchase in apps to sell\nvirtual goods, such as premium content for your app, and subscriptions for\ndigital content. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/technologies/in-app-purchase/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">In-App\nPurchase</a>.</p><p>了解Apple Pay和内购之间的区别很重要。在app和网站上使用Apple Pay销售杂货，服装和电器等实体商品，以及俱乐部会员资格，酒店预订和活动门票等服务。在app中使用内购功能贩售虚拟商品，例如app的优质内容和数字内容的订阅。详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/technologies/in-app-purchase/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">In-App\nPurchase</a>.】</p><h3>Present Apple Pay as a Payment Option</h3><p>将Apple Pay作为付款方式</p><p>Use the following elements if your app\nor website accepts Apple Pay.</p><p>如果app或网站支持apple pay，请使用如下元素。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3edd965eb1ed5006ecccfe508235d57b_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"290\" data-rawheight=\"41\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"290\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;290&#39; height=&#39;41&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"290\" data-rawheight=\"41\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"290\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3edd965eb1ed5006ecccfe508235d57b_b.png\"/></figure>Apple\nPay or Buy with Apple Pay button.</b> Use one of these\nbuttons in your app wherever payment is made, such as on a product detail page\nor shopping cart page, to display the payment sheet and let people complete the\ncheckout process.</p><p>在app中需要支付的地方使用其中一个button，例如商品详情页面或者购物车页面，来显示付款单并让人们完成结账流程。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b2ec5f655b110f96cc9f2e2deb4f9c4c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"223\" data-rawheight=\"38\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"223\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;223&#39; height=&#39;38&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"223\" data-rawheight=\"38\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"223\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b2ec5f655b110f96cc9f2e2deb4f9c4c_b.png\"/></figure>Apple\nPay mark.</b> Use this graphic to communicate that Apple Pay is\nan available payment option when showing other payment options in a similar\nmanner. You can also use plain text to indicate that Apple Pay is a payment\noption.</p><p>当其他支付选项用类似形式显示时，用这张图片表达Apple Pay也是一个可用的支付选项。您也可以用纯文本表示Apple Pay是支付选项。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-994ffd54e22c12e5800f2b848ec96b68_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"143\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"143\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;143&#39; height=&#39;39&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"143\" data-rawheight=\"39\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"143\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-994ffd54e22c12e5800f2b848ec96b68_b.png\"/></figure>Set\nup Apple Pay button.</b> Show this button when the\ndevice supports Apple Pay, but Apple Pay hasn’t been set up yet. Use this\nbutton to take people directly to the Wallet app, so they can add a card.</p><p>当设备支持Apple Pay但还没设置好时，显示这个按钮。用这个按钮将人们直接带到Wallet app，这样他们就能添加一张卡了。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a197313915fe8e0152f7e82c046a4987_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"142\" data-rawheight=\"38\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"142\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;142&#39; height=&#39;38&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"142\" data-rawheight=\"38\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"142\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-a197313915fe8e0152f7e82c046a4987_b.png\"/></figure>Pay\nwith Apple Pay button.</b> Card issuers can use this\nbutton to let people bring up their card when making a purchase in a physical\nstore.</p><p>发卡商可以用这个按钮让人们在实体店购物时带上他们的卡。</p><p><strong>Offer Apple Pay on all devices\nthat support it.</strong> If the\ndevice supports Apple Pay but Apple Pay hasn&#39;t been set up yet, present the Set\nup Apple Pay button. If the device doesn’t support Apple Pay, don’t offer Apple\nPay as a payment option.</p><p>在所有支持Apple Pay的设备上提供这项服务。如果设备支持Apple Pay，但是还没设置，那就显示Set up\nApple Pay。如果设备不支持Apple Pay，那就不要将Apple Pay作为一个支付选项。</p><p><strong>Make Apple Pay buttons the same\nsize or larger than other payment buttons.</strong> Always display the Apple Pay button prominently, so people can\nfind it easily.</p><p>让Apple Pay按钮和其他支付按钮一样大或者大一点。一直突出显示Apple Pay按钮，这样人们就很容易发现它。</p><p><strong>Don’t disable or hide an Apple Pay\nbutton.</strong> If an\nApple Pay button can’t be used, such as because a product size or color hasn’t\nbeen selected, gracefully point out the problem after the button is tapped.</p><p>不要让Apple pay按钮失效或者隐藏它。如果Apple Pay按钮不能用了，比如因为产品尺寸或者颜色不能选择，那就在按钮被点击之后优雅地指出问题所在。</p><p><strong>Use the Apple Pay mark only to\ncommunicate that Apple Pay is accepted.</strong> The mark doesn’t facilitate payment. Never use it as a button or\nposition it as a button.</p><p>使用Apple Pay标志只表达支持Apple Pay。这个标志不能用于支付。永远不要用它作为按钮或者将它定位为按钮。</p><p>For specific guidance regarding the use\nof Apple Pay buttons and the Apple Pay mark, including sizing requirements, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/apple-pay/Apple-Pay-Identity-Guidelines.pdf\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Pay Identity\nGuidelines</a>. For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/ApplePay_Guide/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Pay Programming\nGuide</a>.</p><p>详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/apple-pay/Apple-Pay-Identity-Guidelines.pdf\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Pay Identity\nGuidelines</a>.  <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/ApplePay_Guide/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Pay\nProgramming Guide</a>.】</p><h3>Streamline the Checkout Process精简结账流程</h3><p>People appreciate using Apple Pay to\nmake purchases quickly and easily, so the payment sheet should let people\npromptly authorize payment and complete the transaction.</p><p>人们喜欢用Apple Pay来让购买更容易更迅速，所以付款单应该让人们及时授权支付并且完成交易。</p><p><strong>Make Apple Pay the\ndefault payment option when possible.</strong> If Apple Pay is enabled, assume the person wants to use it when\nmaking a purchase. Consider presenting the Apple Pay button as the first\npayment option, displaying it larger than other options, or using a line to\nvisually separate it from other choices. </p><p>尽可能让Apple Pay成为默认支付选项。如果启用Apple Pay，则假定该人在购物时想要使用它。考虑将Apple Pay按钮显示为第一个付款选项，将其显示为大于其他选项，或用线将其与其他选项在视觉上分开。</p><p><strong>Accelerate purchases with Apple\nPay buttons on product detail pages and with express checkout.</strong> In addition to a shopping cart, consider putting Apple Pay\nbuttons on product detail pages so people can quickly purchase individual\nitems. Where a shopping cart is used to purchase multiple items with the same\nshipping options, consider providing an express checkout feature that shows the\npayment sheet immediately.</p><p>在产品详情页上用Apple Pay按钮加快购物速度，并快速结帐。除了购物车，考虑将Apple Pay按钮放在产品详情页上，以便人们可以快速购买单个项目。如果购物车用于购买具有相同送货选项的多个商品，请考虑提供一个立即显示付款表的快速结帐功能。</p><p><strong>Don&#39;t interrupt checkout after the\nApple Pay button is tapped.</strong> When a\nuser taps the Apple Pay button, they should immediately see the payment sheet.\nDisplaying alerts or views that force people to take additional steps after\ndeciding to complete their purchase adds friction and frustration to the\nprocess. Gather the information you need before people reach the Apple Pay\nbutton. For example, let people choose options, such as color and size, on a\nproduct detail page. On a checkout page, use highlighting or an alert to\nidentify missing information before showing the payment sheet.</p><p>在轻按Apple Pay按钮后不要中断结帐。当用户点击Apple Pay按钮时，他们应该立即看到付款单。显示迫使人们在决定完成购买后采取额外步骤的警告或视图，会增加过程的摩擦和沮丧。在人们访问Apple Pay按钮之前收集所需的信息。例如，让用户在产品详细信息页面上选择颜色和尺寸等选项。在结帐页面上，在显示付款表之前，请使用突出显示或提醒来识别缺少的信息。</p><p><strong>Collect optional information\nbefore checkout begins.</strong> There’s\nno way to input data on the payment sheet, so collect any optional information\nsuch as promo codes, redemption codes, gift messages, and delivery instructions\nahead of time.</p><p>在结帐开始之前收集可选信息。没有办法在付款表上输入数据，因此请提前收集任何可选信息，例如促销代码，兑换代码，礼品信息和送货指示。</p><p><strong>If necessary, gather complex\nshipping information yourself before showing the payment sheet.</strong> The payment sheet lets people select a single shipping speed and\ndestination for an entire order. If your customers can choose different\nshipping speeds and destinations for individual items in an order, collect\nthose details before Apple Pay checkout begins.</p><p>如有必要，请在显示付款单之前自行收集复杂的运输信息。付款单允许用户为整个订单选择一个送货速度和目的地。如果您的客户可以为订单中的单个商品选择不同的送货速度和目的地，请在Apple Pay结帐开始之前收集这些详细信息。</p><p><strong>Prefer information from Apple Pay.</strong> Assume that Apple Pay information is complete and up to date.\nEven if your app has existing contact, shipping, and payment information,\nconsider fetching the latest from Apple Pay during checkout to increase the\nlikelihood of accuracy and reduce potential corrections.</p><p>首选来自Apple Pay的信息。假设Apple Pay信息是完整的并且是最新的。即使您的app已有联系方式，运输信息和付款信息，建议您在结帐时从Apple Pay抓取最新版本，以提高准确性，并减少可能的修正。</p><p><strong>Display an order confirmation or\nthank you page.</strong> After\ncheckout, use an order confirmation page to provide details about when the\norder will ship and how to check its status. Listing Apple Pay on the\nconfirmation page isn’t necessary, but if you do list it, show it after the\nlast four digits of the account used to process the transaction or as a\nseparate note. For example: &#34;1234 (Apple Pay)&#34; or &#34;Paid with\nApple Pay.&#34;</p><p>显示订单确认或感谢页面。结帐后，使用订单确认页面提供订单何时发货以及如何检查其状态的详细信息。在确认页面上列出Apple Pay是不必要的，但如果您列出它，它显示在用于处理交易的帐户的最后四位数字之后，或作为单独的注释。例如：“1234（Apple Pay）”或“用Apple Pay支付”。</p><p><strong>Don&#39;t require account creation\nprior to purchase.</strong> If you\nwant people to register for an account, ask them to do so on the order\nconfirmation or thank you page. Prepopulate as many registration fields as\npossible using information provided by the payment sheet during checkout.</p><p>在购买之前不需要创建帐户。如果您希望人们注册一个帐户，请他们在订单确认或感谢页面。使用付款单在结帐期间提供的信息尽可能多地预填充注册字段。</p><h3>Customize the Payment Sheet自定义付款单</h3><p>You can customize the contents of the\npayment sheet depending on the information needed to complete the transaction.</p><p>您可以依据完成交易所需的信息来自定义付款单的内容。</p><p><strong>Only present and request essential\ninformation.</strong> People\nmay get confused or concerned if the payment sheet includes extraneous\ninformation. For example, it makes sense to see a contact email address but not\na shipping address if merchandise will be delivered electronically. Showing or\nasking for a shipping address in this scenario may give the false impression\nthat something will be physically delivered.</p><p>只显示和必要信息。如果付款单包括无关信息，人们可能会困惑或者担心。例如，如果商品通过通过电子方式发送，联系邮箱地址就比运输地址更有意义。在这个情境下显示或者要求运输信息可能会留下有东西会被物理运送的错误印象。</p><p><strong>Let people choose the shipping\nmethod in the payment sheet.</strong> To the\nextent space permits, show a clear description, a cost, and, optionally, an\nestimated delivery date for each available option.</p><p>让人们在付款单里选择运输方法。在空间允许的范围内，为每个可用选项显示清楚的说明，成本和（可选）估计交货日期。</p><p><b>Keep line items short.</b> Make line items specific and easily understandable at a\nglance. Whenever possible, they should fit on a single line.</p><p>订单项要短。 使订单项一目了然，易于理解。 尽可能让它们在一条线上。</p><p><b>Use line items to explain additional charges, discounts,\nand pending costs.</b> A line item includes a label and cost.\nDon’t use line items to show an itemized list of products that make up the\npurchase.</p><p>使用订单项说明额外费用，折扣和待处理费用。 订单项包含标签和费用。 不要使用订单项来显示组成购买的产品的逐项列表。</p><p><b>Provide a business name after the word <i>PAY</i> on\nthe same line as the total.</b> Use the same business name people will\nsee when they look for the charge on their bank or credit card statement. This\nprovides reassurance that payment is going to the right place. If your app acts\nas an intermediary and is not the end merchant for a payment, clearly indicate\nthis in the following format: PAY [END_MERCHANT_NAME] (VIA [YOUR_APP_NAME]).</p><p>在与总金额相同行上的PAY字之后提供商家名称。 使用人们在他们的银行或信用卡对帐单上查找时会看到的相同商家名称。 这确保付款到正确的地方。 如果app作为中介人，并且不是付款的最终商家，请以下列格式清楚指明：PAY\n[END_MERCHANT_NAME]（VIA\n[YOUR_APP_NAME]）。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38d0525cc65b67931282df4a403b1704_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"257\" data-rawheight=\"294\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"257\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;257&#39; height=&#39;294&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"257\" data-rawheight=\"294\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"257\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-38d0525cc65b67931282df4a403b1704_b.png\"/></figure><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-05be9e9fcd1a79cb45004fde7119f9e4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"260\" data-rawheight=\"271\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"260\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;260&#39; height=&#39;271&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"260\" data-rawheight=\"271\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"260\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-05be9e9fcd1a79cb45004fde7119f9e4_b.png\"/></figure>Clearly\ndisclose when additional costs may be incurred after payment authorization.</b> In some apps, the total cost may be unknown at checkout time. For\nexample, the price of a car ride based on distance or time might change after\ncheckout. Or, a customer might want to add a tip after a product has been\ndelivered. In situations like these, provide a clear explanation in the payment\nsheet and a subtotal marked as &#34;AMOUNT PENDING.&#34; If you are\npreauthorizing a specific amount, make sure the payment sheet accurately\nreflects this information too.</p><p>在支付授权之后可能出现附加花费时，要清楚地透露信息。在有些app中，结账时可能不知道总花费。比如，基于时间或距离的乘车价格在结账之后可能改变。或者，客户可能在商品运达后想给加点小费。在这些情况下，在付款单上提供一个清晰的解释并且将小计标记为“总价待定”。如果您预授权了特定的总额，确保付款单上准确反映了这个信息。</p><h4>Supporting\nSubscriptions支持订阅</h4><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e4f4a7cf749bb15668584e9bedf9c93f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"262\" data-rawheight=\"336\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"262\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;262&#39; height=&#39;336&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"262\" data-rawheight=\"336\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"262\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e4f4a7cf749bb15668584e9bedf9c93f_b.png\"/></figure><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-28fb04069849828f2ef092118b879f9f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"258\" data-rawheight=\"334\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"258\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;258&#39; height=&#39;334&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"258\" data-rawheight=\"334\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"258\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-28fb04069849828f2ef092118b879f9f_b.png\"/></figure>Your app can use Apple Pay to request\nauthorization for a recurring fee. This may be a fixed amount such as a monthly\nmovie ticket subscription, or a variable amount such as a weekly produce order.\nThe initial authorization can also include discounts and additional fees.</p><p>App可以用Apple Pay来为经常性付费要求许可。可能是一个固定的总额，比如月度电影票订阅，或者变化的总额，比如每周产品订单。最初的授权也可以包含打折和附加费用。</p><p><strong>Clarify subscription details\nbefore showing the payment sheet.</strong> Before asking the user to authorize a recurring payment, make\nsure they fully understand the billing frequency and any other terms of\nservice.</p><p>在显示付款单之前理清订阅细节。在要求用户授权经常性付费之前，确认他们完全理解了账单频率以及其他服务协议。</p><p><strong>Include line items that reiterate\nbilling frequency, discounts, and additional upfront fees.</strong> Use these line items to remind the user what they&#39;re\nauthorizing.</p><p>包含重申结算频率，折扣，附加的前期费用等订单项。用订单项来提醒用户他们在为什么授权。</p><p><strong>Clarify the current payment amount\nin the total line.</strong>Make sure the user knows what they&#39;re being billed at the time\nof authorization.</p><p>在总计行澄清当前支付总额。确认用户知道他们在授权时知道要支付多少钱。</p><p><strong>Only show the payment sheet when a\nsubscription change results in additional fees.</strong> When the user changes their subscription, authorization isn&#39;t\nnecessary if the cost decreases or remains the same.</p><p>只在订阅修改产生附加费用时显示付款单。当用户修改订阅，如果花费减少或保持一样就不必再要授权了。</p><h2><b>GameKit</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3f932a6629c085711ca806cb6d4de000_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"287\" data-rawheight=\"597\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"287\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;287&#39; height=&#39;597&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"287\" data-rawheight=\"597\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"287\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-3f932a6629c085711ca806cb6d4de000_b.png\"/></figure>GameKit provides features you can use\nto create great social games. Games can post scores and achievements, display\nleaderboards, add friends, discover new games, and more.</p><p>GameKit提供可用于创造优秀社交游戏的的特性。游戏中心可以发布比分和成就，显示排行榜，添加朋友，发现新游戏，及更多。</p><p><strong>Don’t design a custom sign-in\nscreen.</strong> People\nare automatically prompted to sign into GameKit-enabled games if they’re not\nalready signed in on their device. Displaying a custom sign-in screen is\nrepetitive and can be confusing to people who are expecting the standard one.</p><p>不要设计一个自定义的登入屏。如果尚未在其设备上登录，系统会自动提示用户登录支持GameKit的游戏。设计一个自定义的登入屏就是重复工作，而且会让预期看到标准屏的人困惑。</p><p><strong>In\ngeneral, use standard GameKit interfaces.</strong> In rare cases, it might make sense for a game to include a\ncustom version of a GameKit-provided screen, but doing so risks confusing\npeople. The standard GameKit screens are designed to provide a familiar\nexperience to a large gaming community across all Apple platforms.</p><p>总的来说，使用标准的GameKit接口。 在极少数情况下，对于一个游戏来说包含一个GameKit提供屏的自定义版本是有意义的，但这样做可能会让人感到困惑。 标准的GameKit屏旨在为所有Apple平台上的大型游戏社区提供熟悉的体验。</p><p><strong>Let people turn off</strong><strong>voice chat.</strong> Some people might not want voice chat to be on automatically\nwhen they start your game, and everyone appreciates the ability to turn off\nvoice chat in certain situations.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/gamekit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">GameKit</a>.</p><p>让人们关掉语音聊天。有些人可能不想在开始游戏时自动开启语音聊天，并且每个人都喜欢在某个情景下能关掉语音聊天的能力。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/gamekit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">GameKit</a>】</p><h2><b>HealthKit</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-23a5a4f2df08ee9bb831a38cbc76617e_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"296\" data-rawheight=\"599\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"296\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;296&#39; height=&#39;599&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"296\" data-rawheight=\"599\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"296\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-23a5a4f2df08ee9bb831a38cbc76617e_b.png\"/></figure>The Health app serves as a central\nrepository for health and fitness data in iOS. With the user’s permission, apps\nbuilt with HealthKit can communicate with the Health app to access and share\ninformation. A user might permit a nutrition app, for example, to retrieve\nweight and activity data, so the app can define calorie consumption goals and\nmake dietary recommendations. A nutrition app could also send the number of\ncalories actually consumed to the Health app to include in global progress\nmetrics and share with other apps.</p><p>Health健康app是iOS中健康和健身的存储库。有了用户的许可，用HealthKit建立的app能和Health app通讯来获取、分享信息。例如，用户可能允许一个营养app检索体重和活动数据，这样app能定义卡路里消耗目标并作出减肥建议。营养app也可以发送实际消耗的卡路里数给Health\napp来包含在全球发展指标中并和其他app分享。</p><p><strong>Request access to health data for\nvalid reasons.</strong>HealthKit is designed for use in health and fitness apps. People\nare unlikely to trust apps that request access to unnecessary or seemingly\nunrelated private health data.</p><p>为有效理由请求访问健康数据。HealthKit设计用于健康和健身app。 人们不太可能信任那些请求访问不必要或看似无关的私人健康数据的app。</p><p><strong>Request access to health data only\nwhen needed.</strong> It makes\nsense to request access to weight information when filling out a weight-loss\nprofile, for example, not immediately after the app launches. Requesting\nin-context health data helps communicate your app’s intentions.</p><p>仅在需要时请求访问健康数据。 例如，在填写减肥文件时请求访问体重信息是有意义的，而不是在app启动后立即请求。 请求情景中的健康数据有助于传达app的意图。</p><p><strong>Use the standard permission screen\nto clarify intent.</strong>People expect to see the system-provided permission screen when\nasked to approve access to health data. Add short but descriptive messages to\nthis screen to clarify why the information is needed and the benefits of\ngranting access. Avoid adding custom screens that replicate the standard\npermission screen’s behavior or content.</p><p>使用标准许可屏来表明意图。在被要求准许获取健康信息时，人们预期看到系统提供的许可屏。给这屏添加短但富有描述性的信息，来表明为什么需要这个信息以及准许获取带来的好处。避免添加模仿标准许可屏行为或内容的自定义屏。</p><p><strong>Manage health data sharing solely\nthrough the system’s privacy settings.</strong> People expect to globally manage access to health information in\nSettings &gt; Privacy. Don’t build additional screens in your app that affect\nthe flow of health data. Doing so results in confusion and an inefficient\ninterface.</p><p>只在系统隐私设置里管理健康数据分享。人们预期在设置——隐私中全局管理获取健康信息。在app中不要建立多余的屏来影响健康数据流程。这么做会导致困惑和低效率的界面。</p><p><strong>Don&#39;t use Health app icons,\nimages, or screenshots.</strong> Like all\nApple imagery, these designs are copyrighted and shouldn’t appear in your app\nor marketing materials. You can include an Activity ring element in your app to\ndisplay Move, Exercise, and Stand progress. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/technologies/healthkit/%23activity-rings\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Activity Rings</a>.</p><p>不要使用Health\napp icon、图片和截屏。如同所有Apple图片，这些设计是有版权的而且不应该出现在您的app或者宣传物料中。您可以在app中包含活动环元素来展示活动，练习和站立进度。</p><p><strong>Don&#39;t use the term</strong><em><b>HealthKit</b></em><strong>.</strong> HealthKit is the development framework used to access data\nstored in the Health app. If you need to explain how your app works with this\ndata, use the term <em>the Health app</em>. For\nexample, you might say that your app “saves information to the Health app” or\n“uses data from the Health app.”</p><p>不要用HealthKit这个术语。HealthKit是一个用于获取Health app中存储数据的开发框架。如果您需要解释app如何用这些数据，请用Health\napp这个说法。例如，您可能想说您的app“向Health app存储数据”或者“用Health app的数据”</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/healthkit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">HealthKit</a>.</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/healthkit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">HealthKit</a>】</p><h3><b>Activity Rings活动环</b></h3><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fd41047ae06f69603bc3cb15e73254d9_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"256\" data-rawheight=\"523\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"256\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;256&#39; height=&#39;523&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"256\" data-rawheight=\"523\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"256\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fd41047ae06f69603bc3cb15e73254d9_b.png\"/></figure><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-083de19d59402fce5f20482be8180c2f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"258\" data-rawheight=\"523\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"258\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;258&#39; height=&#39;523&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"258\" data-rawheight=\"523\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"258\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-083de19d59402fce5f20482be8180c2f_b.png\"/></figure>Apps can enhance\ntheir health and wellness offerings by displaying an Activity ring element that\nshows an individual’s progress toward Move, Exercise, and Stand goals. This\nelement always contains three rings, whose colors and meanings match those\nprovided by the Activity app.</p><p>App可以通过显示活动环元素来增强健康与保健功能。活动环显示个人朝向移动，锻炼，站立目标的进程。这个元素总是包含三个环，颜色和寓意和Activity\napp中提供的相匹配。</p><p><strong>Use Activity rings for\nMove, Exercise, and Stand information only.</strong> Activity rings are designed to consistently represent progress\nin these specific areas. Don’t attempt to replicate or modify Activity rings\nfor other purposes. Never use Activity rings to display other types of data.\nNever show Move, Exercise, and Stand progress in another ring-like element.</p><p>只为移动，锻炼和站立信息使用活动环。活动环旨在这些特定领域呈现一致的信息。不要为了其他目的试图复制或修改活动环。不要用活动环显示其他种类的信息。永远不要用其他环状元素显示移动，锻炼和站立进程。</p><p><strong>Use Activity rings to\nshow progress for a single person.</strong> Never use Activity rings to represent data for more than one\nperson, and make sure it’s obvious whose progress is shown, such as by using a\nlabel, a photo, or an avatar.</p><p>一个活动环只显示一个人的活动进程。永远不要用活动环来显示一个以上人数的数据，并且确认显示谁的进度很明显，比如用个标签，照片或者头像。</p><p><strong>Don’t use Activity\nrings for ornamentation.</strong> Activity\nrings should provide information to people, not embellish your app’s design.\nNever display Activity rings in labels or background graphics.</p><p>不要将活动环作为装饰。活动环应该为人们提供信息，不是用来点缀您的app的。不要在标签或者背景图形中显示活动环。</p><p><strong>Don’t use Activity\nrings for branding.</strong> Use\nActivity rings strictly to display Activity progress in your app.\nNever use Activity rings in your app’s icon or marketing materials.</p><p>不要将活动环用于推广。活动环仅用于在app中显示活动进程。不要将活动环用于app icon或市场推广物料。</p><p><strong>Maintain Activity ring and\nbackground colors.</strong> For a\nconsistent user experience, the visual appearance of Activity rings must always\nbe the same, regardless of the context in which they appear. Never change the\nlook of the rings or background by using filters, changing colors, or modifying\nopacity. Instead, design the surrounding interface to blend with the rings. For\nexample, enclose the rings within a circle. Always scale the rings\nappropriately so they don’t seem disconnected or out of place.</p><p>保持活动环和背景颜色。为了一致的用户体验，活动环的视觉外观必须一致一样，无论他们出现在什么情境下。永远不要用滤镜、修改颜色或者修改透明度来改变环的外观。相反，将周边界面设计成与环相融合的。例如，将环括在一个圆中。总是将环缩放得当，这样他们看起来就不会脱离环境。</p><p><strong>Maintain Activity ring margins.</strong> An Activity ring element must include a minimum outer margin of\nno less than the distance between rings. Never allow other elements to crop,\nobstruct, or encroach upon this margin or the rings themselves. To display an\nActivity ring element within a circle, adjust the corner radius of the\nenclosing view rather than applying a circular mask.</p><p>保持活动环的边距。活动环元素必须包含不小于环间距的最小外边距。永远不要让其他元素裁剪、阻碍和侵犯边距或环本身。要在圆圈内显示活动环元素，调整包围视图的角半径，而不是用圆形遮罩。</p><p><strong>Differentiate other ring-like\nelements from Activity rings.</strong> Mixing\ndifferent ring styles can lead to a visually confusing interface. If you must\ninclude other rings, use padding, lines, or labels to separate them from\nActivity rings. Color and scale can also help provide visual separation.</p><p>将活动环和其他环状元素区分开。 混合不同的环形可能导致视觉混乱的界面。 如果必须包括其他环，请使用填充，线条或标签将其与活动环分离。 颜色和比例也可以帮助提供视觉分离。</p><p><strong>Provide app-specific information\nonly in Activity notifications.</strong> The system already delivers Move, Exercise, and Stand progress\nupdates. Don’t repeat this same information, and never show an Activity ring\nelement in your app’s notifications. It’s fine to reference Activity progress\nin a notification, but do so in a way that’s unique to your app and doesn’t\nreplicate the same information provided by the system.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/healthkitui/hkactivityringview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">HKActivityRingView</a>.</p><p>仅在活动通知中提供app专用信息。 系统已提交移动，锻炼和站立进度更新。 请勿重复此相同的信息，并且不要在应用的通知中显示活动环元素。 可以在通知中提及活动进度，但是请确保这样做对于app来说是唯一途径，并且不会复制系统提供的相同信息。</p><h2><b>HomeKit</b></h2><p>HomeKit lets people securely control\nconnected accessories in their homes from the iOS device they&#39;re holding or\nwith their voice using Siri. These accessories include locks, lights, shades,\ncameras, garage doors, sensors, and thermostats. They communicate with iCloud\nor a server to receive instructions and provide status updates. This\ncommunication can take place directly or through an iOS device in the home that\noperates as a hub, such as Apple TV or iPad.</p><p>iOS includes a Home app that provides a\nstandard set of controls for managing, configuring, and interacting with\naccessories. Your app can also integrate with HomeKit to provide a custom or\nbranded experience.</p><p>HomeKit允许用户从他们持有的iOS设备或使用声音通过Siri安全地控制家中的连接配件。 这些配件包括锁，灯，窗帘，照相机，车库门，传感器和恒温器。 它们与iCloud或服务器通信以接收指令并提供状态更新。 这种通信可以直接进行，或者通过在作为集线器（例如Apple TV或iPad）操作的家庭中的iOS设备进行。</p><p>iOS包括一个Home app，它提供了一套标准的控件，用于管理，配置和与配件交互。 您的应用程序还可以与HomeKit集成，以提供自定义或品牌体验。</p><h3>Make Home Automation Approachable</h3><h3>让家庭自动化成为可能</h3><p>Home automation can be intimidating, so\nit’s very important to use friendly, conversational language that people\nunderstand. Throughout your app, avoid using acronyms and technical jargon that\nmight cause confusion or frustration. Use the following terms to provide a\nconsistent and approachable experience:<b>家庭自动化可以是吓人的，所以使用人们理解的友好的会话语言是非常重要的。\n在app中，避免使用可能导致混乱或沮丧的缩略语和技术术语。 使用以下术语提供一致的、平易近人的体验：</b></p><p><strong>Home</strong><strong>家</strong></p><p>Represents a\n  physical home. People might have multiple homes that are far apart, such as a main home and a\n  vacation home. Or, they may have homes that are close together, but considered separate,\n  such as a main home and a guest cottage on the same property. Home names should\n  be customizable.</p><p>表示物理家庭。 人们可能有多个相距很远的家庭，例如主要家庭和度假屋。 或者，他们可能有靠近在一起的家，但被认为是分开的，例如在同一财产的主要家庭和客人小屋。\n  家庭名称应该是可定制的。</p><p><strong>Room</strong><strong>房间</strong></p><p>Represents a\n  physical room in a home. Rooms don’t have specific characteristics such as\n  size or location. They’re simply meaningful names, such as “living room” or\n  “kitchen.” Rooms provide a way to organize accessories based on their actual\n  location within a home, and enable voice commands like “Siri, turn on the\n  kitchen lights.” Room names should be customizable.</p><p>代表家中的实体房间。 房间没有具体的，大小或位置之类的特点。 它们只是有意义的名字，例如“客厅”或“厨房”。房间提供了一种根据家中的实际位置来组织配件的方法，并且能够执行诸如“Siri，打开厨房灯”的声音命令。 名称应可自定义。</p><p><strong>Zone</strong><strong>区域</strong></p><p>Represents a\n  specific area in a home, such as &#34;upstairs” or “downstairs.” Zones\n  provide a way to group, organize, and target multiple rooms, typically in\n  close proximity to one another, and enable voice commands like “Siri, turn on\n  all of the lights downstairs.” Zone names should be customizable.</p><p>表示家庭中的特定区域，例如“楼上”或“楼下”。区域提供了对多个房间进行分组，组织和定位的方式，通常彼此接近，并且启用语音命令，例如“Siri，打开 所有的灯楼下。“区域名称应该是可定制的。</p><p><strong>Accessory</strong><strong>配件</strong></p><p>A physical,\n  connected HomeKit accessory, such as a camera or light. People add\n  accessories to rooms in their homes.</p><p>一个物理的，连接的HomeKit配件，如相机或灯。\n  人们在他们的家里给房间添加配件。</p><p><strong>Service</strong><strong>服务</strong></p><p>A controllable\n  feature of an accessory, such as the light on a connected lamp. Some\n  accessories offer multiple services. For example, a connected garage door\n  might let you individually control both the light and the door, or a\n  connected outlet might let you control the top outlet and the bottom outlet\n  separately. Instead of using the term “service” in your app, use meaningful\n  terms that clearly identify the service, such as “garage door” or “garage\n  light.” Service names should be customizable.</p><p>附件的可控特征，例如所连接的灯上的灯。 一些配件提供多种服务。 例如，连接的车库门可能允许您单独控制灯和门，或者连接的出口可以分别控制顶部出口和底部出口。在app中使用有意义的、清楚地标识服务的术语，而不是用术语“服务”，如“车库门”或“车库灯”。服务名称应该是可定制的。</p><p><strong>Characteristic</strong><strong>特性</strong></p><p>A controllable\n  attribute of a service. For example, on a ceiling fan, the light service\n  might have power state (on/off) and brightness characteristics, and the fan\n  service might have a speed (off, low, high) characteristic. Instead of\n  referring to the term “characteristic” in your app, use meaningful terms that\n  identify the characteristic, such as “brightness” and “speed.” Use\n  appropriate controls to let people change characteristics. For example, use a\n  switch to let people toggle a service on and off.</p><p>服务的可控属性。 例如，在吊扇上，灯光服务可能具有电源状态（开/关）和亮度特性，并且风扇服务可能具有速度（关，低，高）特性。请在app中使用识别特性的有意义的术语，例如“亮度”和“速度”，而不是引用术语“特性”，。使用适当的控件让人们改变特性。\n  例如，使用开关可以让人们切换服务开关。</p><p><strong>Action</strong><strong>动作</strong></p><p>The act of\n  changing a characteristic of a service. For example, turning a light on or\n  off, or adjusting the speed of a fan. Actions are initiated by people and\n  through automation.</p><p>改变服务特性的行为。例如，开灯或关灯，或者调整风扇速度。动作是人启动的并且通过自动化。</p><p><strong>Scene</strong><strong>场景</strong></p><p>A group of\n  actions for controlling one or more services. Someone might, for example,\n  create a “Movie Time” scene that dims the lights and lowers the shades, or a\n  “Bedtime” scene that locks the door and turns off all lights except the one\n  next to the bed.</p><p>控制一个或更多服务的一组动作。例如，有的人可能，创建一个电影时光场景，调暗灯光，降低遮阳帘；或者睡觉时间场景，锁上门，关掉除床头灯之外的所有灯。</p><p><strong>Automation</strong><strong>自动化</strong></p><p>Causes\n  accessories to react to certain situations, such as when your location\n  changes, a particular time of day occurs, another accessory turns on or off,\n  or a sensor detects something.</p><p>让配件根据某个场景变化，比如当地址改变时，一天中某个特定的时间，其他配件开启或者关掉，或者传感器探测某物。</p><h3>Provide a Great Experience提供优秀体验</h3><p>Through HomeKit, your app can help\npeople:</p><p>通过HomeKit，app可以帮助人们：</p><p>·       \nSet up and manage homes, rooms, zones, and scenes</p><p>·       \n设置和管理家庭，房间，区域，场景。</p><p>·       \nFind, add, remove, and interact with accessories</p><p>·       \n找到，添加，移除，与配件交互</p><p>·       \nGive trusted family and friends access to control accessories</p><p>·       \n给信任的家庭和朋友控制配件的权限</p><p>·       \nUse Siri to control accessories with voice commands</p><p>·       \n用Siri通过语音指令控制配件</p><p>·       \nCheck the status of accessories</p><p>·       \n检查配件状态</p><p>·       \nAutomate common accessory behaviors and settings</p><p>·       \n自动化常见配件行为和设置</p><p><strong>Make accessory setup quick,\nintuitive, and automatic whenever possible.</strong> Ideally, your app automatically detects new accessories and\npresents them prominently. Don’t force people to create an account before they\ncan add an accessory.</p><p>让配件设置尽可能快速，直接，自动化。理想情况下，app自动探测新配件并且突出显示他们。不要强迫人们在能添加配件之前创建一个账号。</p><p><strong>Prompt users to assign accessories\nto rooms after setup.</strong> After\nconfiguring a new accessory, immediately prompt people to add the accessory to\na room. If a home or room hasn’t been created yet, provide a way to create one.\nIf there’s only one room in a home, present options for adding the accessory to\nthat room and creating a new room.</p><p>在设置之后提示用户将配件分配给房间。在配置新配件之后，立刻提示人们将配件添加到一个房间。如果家庭或者房间还没被创建，提供创建的方法。如果家里只有一个房间，显示将配件添加到那个房间以及创建新房间的选项。</p><p><strong>Make sure accessories are easy to\nidentify.</strong> Accessories\nshould be recognizable when users interact with them, during the setup process,\nand when adjusting settings later. If a living room contains multiple lights,\nfor example, provide a way to differentiate each one. In this scenario, you\nmight provide a control that physically flashes a light to identify it and let\npeople give each light’s service a unique name, such as “desk lamp” or\n“chandelier.”</p><p>确保配件容易识别。当用户和配件交互时，设置过程期间，以及稍后调整设置时，他们应该是可识别的。例如，如果一个起居室包含多盏灯，提供区别每个灯的方法。在这个情境中，您可能提供一个物理闪烁灯的控件来识别它并且让人们给每个灯服务一个独特的名字，比如“台灯”或“吊灯”。</p><p><strong>Provide multiple ways to locate\naccessories.</strong> People\nwant to interact with accessories quickly, such as unlocking the door while\nwalking up to the house. Implement ways to filter and search for accessories by\nname, type, or location in the home. Consider providing a dashboard of favorite\naccessory services.</p><p>提供多种方式来定位配件。人们想快速与配件交互，比如在走回家的过程中解锁家门。提供通过名称、种类或者在家中的位置来过滤、搜索配件的方法。考虑提供最爱配件服务面板。</p><p><strong>Report accessory statuses\naccurately.</strong> If an\naccessory can’t be reached, don’t assume its status. If a lock is unreachable,\nfor example, don’t say it’s locked or unlocked based on the last known status.\nInstead, explain that the lock is currently unreachable.</p><p>准确报告配件状态。如果配件不能连接，不要猜测它的状态。比如，如果一个锁连不上，不要基于上次状态说它锁上了或者没锁。相反，说现在这个锁连不上了。</p><p><strong>Integrate with Siri.</strong> Siri makes it easy to perform sophisticated operations with a\nsingle statement. Siri recognizes the names of homes, rooms, zones, services,\nand scenes, and can understand statements like “Siri, lock the front door,”\n“Siri, turn off the upstairs lights,” “Siri, make it warmer in the media room,”\nand “Siri, set the house to movie mode.”</p><p>和Siri整合。 Siri让通过简单陈述完成复杂操作更加容易。Siri识别家庭、房间、区域、服务、场景的名称，并且能理解类似“Siri，锁前门”“Siri，观点楼上的灯”“Siri，让媒体室暖和点”“Siri，将房子调整为电影模式”之类的陈述。</p><p><strong>Assist with name conflicts.</strong> Siri requires that home, room, zone, service, and scene names be\nunique. When name conflicts arise, explain the problem clearly and offer\nalternatives that make sense and are easy to remember.</p><p>处理名称冲突。Siri要求家庭、房间、区域、服务、场景名字都是独一无二的、当名字发生冲突，清楚地解释这个问题并且提供有意义的容易记的替代方案。</p><p><strong>When there are multiple homes, set\na primary home.</strong> Siri\nneeds to know which home to target when saying something like “Turn on my\nliving room lights.” If there’s only one home, that home is targeted for all\ncommands. If the person has multiple homes and no primary home is configured,\nthe current home—the one the person is in at the moment—is targeted.</p><p>当有多个家庭时，设置主要家庭。 Siri需要知道哪个家是当说“打开我的客厅灯光”时的目标。如果只有一个家，那这个家是所有命令的目标。 如果该人具有多个家庭并且没有配置主家庭，则当前家 - 目前该人所在的家—是目标。</p><p><strong>Present editable service names\ninstead of accessory names.</strong> Some\naccessories have multiple services, such as a ceiling fan with different\nservices for the light and the fan. In this scenario, telling Siri to “Turn on\nthe dining room light” should activate the light service and telling Siri to\n“Turn on the dining room fan” should activate the fan service. Provide clear\nand concise default service names that are well-known words or phrases, but let\npeople customize these names if desired. For example, someone might want to\nrename a connected outlet or switch to “desk lamp” if that’s what the outlet or\nswitch controls. Never use company names or model numbers for service names.</p><p>显示当前可编辑的服务名称，而不是附件名称。 一些配件具有多种服务，例如一个带有灯和风扇不同服务的吊扇。 在这种情况下，告诉Siri“打开饭厅灯”应该启动光服务，告诉Siri“打开饭厅风扇”应该启动风扇服务。 提供清晰简洁的默认服务名称，这些名称是熟知的单词或短语，但如果需要，可以让用户自定义这些名称。 例如，有人可能想重命名连接的插座或切换到“台灯”，如果这是插座或开关控制。 切勿对服务名称使用公司名称或型号。</p><p><strong>During setup, teach people the\ncommands Siri understands.</strong> When\nappropriate throughout your app, show examples of phrases that work with Siri,\nsuch as “You can say ‘Siri, set the house to movie mode.’ to activate this\nconfiguration.”</p><p>在安装过程中，教人们Siri理解的命令。 在整个app的适当时候，显示与Siri一起使用的短语示例，例如“您可以说”Siri，将房子设置为电影模式“以激活此配置。</p><p><strong>Make automation intuitive.</strong> HomeKit accessories can be controlled automatically, based on\nconditional relationships such as time, location, and the behavior of other\naccessories. For example, the kitchen lights could be set to come on when the\ngarage door opens and it’s after sunset. Setting up conditional relationships\nlike this can be confusing, so make this process as simple as possible. Design\nclear interfaces and use verbiage that mirrors the way people speak.</p><p>使自动化直观。 HomeKit配件可以根据条件关系自动控制，如时间，位置和其他配件的行为。 例如，厨房灯可以设置为在车库门打开时和日落后开。 设置这样的条件关系可能会令人困惑，所以使这个过程尽可能简单。 设计清晰的界面和使用反映人们说话的方式的说法。</p><p>For implementation guidelines and other\ninformation, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/NetworkingInternet/Conceptual/HomeKitDeveloperGuide/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">HomeKit Developer\nGuide</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/homekit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">HomeKit</a>. If\nyou’re an MFi licensee, visit the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//mfi.apple.com/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">MFi portal</a> for\nguidance on naming and messaging for accessory packaging.</p><h2><b>iCloud</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f5a358b91d7a75f578e873c0aaf4e098_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"516\" data-rawheight=\"334\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"516\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f5a358b91d7a75f578e873c0aaf4e098_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;516&#39; height=&#39;334&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"516\" data-rawheight=\"334\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"516\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f5a358b91d7a75f578e873c0aaf4e098_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f5a358b91d7a75f578e873c0aaf4e098_b.png\"/></figure>iCloud is a service that lets people\nseamlessly access the content they care about—photos, videos, documents, and\nmore—from any device, without performing explicit synchronization. A\nfundamental aspect of iCloud is transparency. People don’t need to know where\ncontent resides.They can just assume they’re always accessing the latest\nversion.</p><p>iCloud是一项服务，可让用户无需特地同步即可从任何设备无缝访问他们关心的内容（照片，视频，文档等）。 iCloud的一个基本方面是透明度。 人们不需要知道内容驻留在哪里。他们可以假设他们总是访问最新版本。</p><p><strong>Make it easy to use your app with\niCloud.</strong> People\nenable iCloud in Settings and expect apps to work with it automatically. If you\nthink people might want to choose whether to use iCloud with your app, show a\nsimple option the first time your app opens that provides a choice between\nusing iCloud for all data or not at all.</p><p>用iCloud轻松使用APP。 人们在“设置”中启用iCloud，并期望APP自动使用。 如果您认为人们可能想要选择是否在APP中使用iCloud，请在app第一次打开时显示一个简单的选项，以便为所有数据使用iCloud或根本不使用iCloud。</p><p><strong>Avoid asking which documents to\nkeep in iCloud.</strong> Most\npeople expect all of their content to be available in iCloud and don’t want to\nmanage the storage of individual documents. Consider how your app handles and\nexposes content, and try to perform more file-management tasks automatically.</p><p>避免询问在iCloud中保留哪些文档。 大多数人希望他们的所有内容在iCloud中可用，并且不想管理单个文档的存储。 考虑app如何处理和公开内容，并尝试自动执行更多的文件管理任务。</p><p><strong>Keep content up to date when\npossible.</strong> In\niCloud-enabled apps, its best when people always have access to the most recent\ncontent. However, you need to balance this experience with respect to device\nstorage and bandwidth constraints. If your app works with very large documents,\nit may be better to let people control when updated content is downloaded. If\nyour app fits in this category, design a way to indicate that a more recent\nversion of a document is available in iCloud. When a document is updating,\nprovide subtle feedback if the download takes more than a few seconds.</p><p>尽可能保持内容最新。 在支持iCloud的应用中，最好让用户总是可以访问最新内容。但是，您需要在设备存储和带宽限制方面平衡这一体验。 如果APP使用非常大的文档，最好让用户控制下载更新内容的时间。 如果APP恰属此类，请设计一种方式来指示iCloud中提供了更新版本的文档。 文档更新时，如果下载时间超过几秒钟，请提供微反馈。</p><p><strong>Respect iCloud storage space.</strong> iCloud is a finite resource for which people pay. Use iCloud to\nstore information people create and understand, and avoid using it for app\nresources or content you can regenerate. Even if your app doesn’t implement\niCloud support, remember that iCloud backups include the contents of every\napp’s Documents folder. To avoid using up too much space, be picky about the\ncontent you place in the Documents folder.</p><p>尊重iCloud存储空间。 iCloud是人们付费使用的有限资源。 使用iCloud存储人们创建和了解的信息，并避免将其用于app资源或可重新生成的内容。 即使APP没有使用iCloud支持，请记住iCloud备份包括每个APP文档文件夹的内容。 为了避免占用太多空间，请谨慎选择您放置在“文档”文件夹中的内容。</p><p><strong>Make sure your app behaves\nappropriately when iCloud is unavailable.</strong> If someone manually disables iCloud or turns on Airplane Mode,\nyou don’t need to display an alert notifying them the iCloud is unavailable.\nThey already know this. However, it may still be helpful to unobtrusively let\nthem know that changes they make won’t be available on other devices until\niCloud access is restored.</p><p>当iCloud不可用时，请确保app运行正常。如果有人手动禁用iCloud或打开飞行模式，则不需要显示警报通知iCloud不可用。他们已经知道了。但是，通不太引人瞩目的方式让他们知道，在iCloud访问恢复之前，它们所做的更改将在其他设备上不可用，这可能仍有帮助。</p><p><strong>Keep app state information in\niCloud.</strong> In\naddition to storing documents and other files, you can use iCloud to store\npreferences and information about the state of your app. For example, a\nmagazine app might store the last page viewed so when the app is opened on\nanother device, someone can continue reading from where they left off. If you\nuse iCloud to store preferences, make sure it’s for ones people want applied to\nall of their devices. For example, some settings might be more useful at work\nthan at home.</p><p>在iCloud中保留app状态信息。 除了存储文档和其他文件，您可以使用iCloud存储首选项和有关app状态的信息。 例如，杂志app可能会存储最后一次查看的页面，因此当app在另一台设备上打开时，某人可以继续从上次停止的页面进行阅读。 如果您使用iCloud存储首选项，请确保用户想把这些设置用在所有设备上。 例如，一些设置在工作中比在家更有用。</p><p><strong>Warn about the consequences of\ndeleting a document.</strong> When\nsomeone deletes a document in an iCloud-enabled app, the document is removed\nfrom iCloud and all other devices too. Show a warning and ask for confirmation\nbefore performing the deletion.</p><p>警告删除文档的后果。 当某人在启用iCloud的app中删除文档时，该文档也会从iCloud和所有其他设备中删除。 在执行删除之前显示警告并要求确认。</p><p><strong>Make conflict resolution prompt\nand easy.</strong> To the\nextent possible, try to detect and resolve version conflicts automatically. If\nthis can’t be done, display an unobtrusive notification that makes it easy to\ndifferentiate and choose between the conflicting versions. Conflict resolution\nshould always occur as early as possible, so time isn’t wasted in the wrong\nversion.</p><p>使冲突解决提示和容易。 尽可能尝试自动检测和解决版本冲突。 如果无法完成此操作，请显示不显眼的通知，以便轻松区分并在冲突的版本之间进行选择。 冲突解决应该总是尽早发生，这样时间就不会被浪费在错误的版本了。</p><p><strong>Include iCloud content in search\nresults.</strong> People\nwith iCloud accounts assume their content is universally available, and they\nexpect search results to reflect this perspective.</p><p>搜索结果中包含iCloud内容。有iCloud账号的人们设想他们的内容是全局可用的，并且期望搜索结果反应在这个方面。</p><p>For implementation guidelines, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/iCloudDesignGuide/Chapters/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">iCloud Design Guide</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/DataManagement/Conceptual/CloudKitQuickStart/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">CloudKit Quick Start</a>.</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/iCloudDesignGuide/Chapters/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">iCloud Design Guide</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/DataManagement/Conceptual/CloudKitQuickStart/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">CloudKit Quick Start</a>.】</p>",
