            "content": "<h2><b>Custom Keyboards自定义键盘</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c1832a53014fc6abee1c2d0d31d5a6c4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"288\" data-rawheight=\"301\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"288\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;288&#39; height=&#39;301&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"288\" data-rawheight=\"301\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"288\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c1832a53014fc6abee1c2d0d31d5a6c4_b.png\"/></figure>A keyboard\nextension replaces the standard keyboard with a custom keyboard. Custom\nkeyboards are enabled in the Settings app, under General &gt; Keyboards. Once\nenabled, the keyboard is available during text entry within any app, except\nwhen editing secure text fields and phone number fields. People can enable\nmultiple custom keyboards, and switch between them at any time.</p><p>键盘扩展用自定义键盘替代标准键盘。在设置Settings—通用—键盘里启用自定义键盘。一旦启用，这个键盘在任何app内文本输入期间都能用，除了编辑保密文本域以及电话号码。人们可以启用多种自定义键盘，并且在任何时候切换。</p><p><b>Make sure you really need a\ncustom keyboard.</b>Custom keyboards make sense when you want to expose unique keyboard\nfunctionality systemwide, such as a novel way of inputting text or the ability\nto type in a language not supported by iOS. If you only want a custom keyboard\nin your app, consider creating a custom input view instead. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/custom-keyboards/%23custom-input-views\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Custom\nInput Views</a>.</p><p>确认您确实需要一个自定义键盘。当您想在全系统展现特殊的键盘功能，比如一个新颖的输入文本的方式或者输入一种iOS不支持的语言。如果您只想在您的app中用一个自定义键盘，还是考虑创建一个自定义输入视图吧。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/custom-keyboards/%23custom-input-views\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Custom\nInput Views</a>】</p><p><b>Provide an obvious and easy\nway to switch between keyboards.</b> People know that the Globe key on the\nstandard iOS keyboard, which replaces the Emoji key when you have multiple\nkeyboards enabled, quickly switches to other keyboards. They expect a similarly\nintuitive experience in your keyboard. Note that the Globe key replaces the Emoji\nkey when you have multiple keyboards installed.</p><p>为键盘之间的切换提供显而易见的容易的方式。人们知道标准iOS键盘上的那个地球键，当您启用多种键盘时代替Emoji键，能快速切换至其他键盘。他们期待一个在您键盘上相似的直觉的体验。注意，当您安装了多种键盘时，地球键会替代Emoji键。</p><p><b>Consider providing a keyboard\ntutorial in your app.</b> People are used to the standard keyboard, and\nlearning a new keyboard takes time. Make the onboarding process easier by\nproviding usage instructions in your app—not in the keyboard itself. Tell\npeople how to enable your keyboard, activate it during text entry, use it, and\nswitch back to the standard keyboard.</p><p>For\nimplementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/CustomKeyboard.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Custom\nKeyboard</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App\nExtension Programming Guide</a>.</p><p>考虑在app中提供键盘教程。人们习惯于标准键盘，并且学习新键盘的使用方式要花时间。在app中，而不是在键盘本身，通过提供用法指南让上手过程更容易。告诉人们如何启用您的键盘，在文本输入期间激活它，使用它，然后切换回标准键盘。</p><p>详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/CustomKeyboard.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Custom\nKeyboard</a>】in【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App\nExtension Programming Guide</a>.】</p><h3>Custom Input Views自定义输入视图</h3><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4229cb73e9e36e0f53b5dc086a57bd3c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"290\" data-rawheight=\"299\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"290\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;290&#39; height=&#39;299&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"290\" data-rawheight=\"299\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"290\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4229cb73e9e36e0f53b5dc086a57bd3c_b.png\"/></figure><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-66d743fe955de79dca590b4e7d5f5377_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"288\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"288\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;288&#39; height=&#39;300&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"288\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"288\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-66d743fe955de79dca590b4e7d5f5377_b.png\"/></figure>A custom input view replaces the\nstandard keyboard with a custom keyboard, but only in your app, rather than\nsystemwide. Use a custom input view to provide a unique and efficient method of\ndata entry. Numbers, for example, implements custom input views for entering\namounts, dates, and other values while editing a spreadsheet.</p><p>自定输入视图用自定义键盘替代标准键盘，但是只在您的app中，而不是整个系统里。用自定义输入视图来提供独特的高效的数据输入思路。例如，Numbers在编辑电子表格时，使用自定义输入视图来键入总量，时间，以及其他值。</p><p><strong>Make functionality obvious.</strong> The controls on a custom input view should make sense in the\ncontext of your app. Data entry should be clear and intuitive, so additional\ninstruction isn’t necessary.</p><p>让功能显而易见。在自定义输入视图上的控件应该在app情境中有意义。数据输入应该是清楚的直观的，所以附加的指示是不必要的。</p><p><strong>Play\nthe standard keyboard click sound during typing.</strong> The keyboard click sound provides audible feedback while the\nuser is tapping buttons on the keyboard. Tapping custom controls in your input\nview should produce this sound too. Note that this sound is only available to\nvisible custom input views, and people can disable the sound systemwide in\nSettings &gt; Sounds. For implementation details, see the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uidevice/1620050-playinputclick\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">playInputClick</a>method of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uidevice\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIDevice</a>.</p><p>在打字期间播放标准键盘声效。键盘声效在用户点击键盘按钮时提供听觉反馈。在输入视图中点击自定义控件也应该产生这种声音。注意，这种声音只在可见的自定义输入视图有效，并且人们可以在设置—声音中让声音在整个系统中关闭。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uidevice/1620050-playinputclick\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">playInputClick</a>method of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uidevice\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIDevice</a>.】</p><p><strong>Provide an input accessory view if\nnecessary.</strong> Some apps\nimplement an additional custom input accessory view, which appears above the\nkeyboard. In Numbers, an input accessory view helps people enter standard or\ncustom calculations.</p><p>必要的话提供输入附件视图。有些app使用附加的自定义输入附件视图。这种视图在键盘上方出现。在Numbers里，一个输入附件是图帮助人们输入标准或自定义计算。</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/StringsTextFonts/Conceptual/TextAndWebiPhoneOS/InputViews/InputViews.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Custom Data Input\nViews</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/StringsTextFonts/Conceptual/TextAndWebiPhoneOS/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Text Programming\nGuide for iOS</a>.</p><p>详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/StringsTextFonts/Conceptual/TextAndWebiPhoneOS/InputViews/InputViews.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Custom Data Input\nViews</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/StringsTextFonts/Conceptual/TextAndWebiPhoneOS/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Text Programming\nGuide for iOS</a>.】</p><h2><b>Document Providers文档提供程序</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6fc3d42db5e60e669ecdc4a46efa98a1_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"293\" data-rawheight=\"597\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"293\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;293&#39; height=&#39;597&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"293\" data-rawheight=\"597\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"293\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6fc3d42db5e60e669ecdc4a46efa98a1_b.png\"/></figure>A document provider extension implements a custom interface for\nimporting, exporting, opening, or moving an app’s documents from within other\napps on the system. When a document provider extension loads, its interface\ndisplays in a modal view containing a navigation bar.</p><p>文档提供扩展用一个自定义界面来导入、导出、打开或者在系统上从其他app里移动app文档。当文档提供扩展加载时，界面显示在包含一个导航条的模态视图中。</p><p><strong>When users open or import files,\nshow only context-specific documents and information.</strong>When\nsomeone uses your extension to open or import documents, only display documents\nthat are appropriate for the current context. For example, if a PDF-editing app\nloads your extension, only list PDF files as possible documents that can be\nopened or imported. Be sure to list other information that may be helpful too,\nsuch as modification dates, sizes, and whether documents are local or remote.</p><p>当用户打开或者导入文档，只显示特定情境的文档和信息。当某些人使用扩展来打开或者导入文档，只显示适合当前情境的文档。例如，如果一个PDF编辑app加载您的扩展，那就只显示PDF文档作为可能被打开或导入的文档。确认列出可能有帮助的信息，例如修改时间，大小，以及文档是本地的还是远程的。</p><p><strong>Let people select a destination\nwhen exporting and moving documents.</strong> Unless your app stores documents in a single directory, let\nusers navigate to a specific destination in your directory hierarchy. Consider\nproviding a way to add new subdirectories.</p><p>当输出和移动文档时让人们选择目的地。除非您的app在单个目录中存储文档，否则要让用户在目录层次结构中选择特定的目的地。考虑提供添加新的子目录的方法。</p><p><strong>Don’t provide a custom navigation\nbar.</strong> Your\nextension loads within a modal view that already includes a navigation bar.\nProviding a second navigation bar is confusing and takes space away from your\ncontent.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/FileProvider.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Document Provider</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Extension\nProgramming Guide</a>.</p><p>不要提供自定义的导航条。您的扩展在一个已经包含导航条的模态视图中加载。提供第二个导航条会让人困惑，并且占据内容的位置。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/FileProvider.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Document Provider</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Extension\nProgramming Guide</a>.】</p><h2><b>Home Screen Quick Actions</b></h2><p>主屏快速动作</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-44738ea89bf5348438a30b56d497e52a_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"301\" data-rawheight=\"597\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"301\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;301&#39; height=&#39;597&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"301\" data-rawheight=\"597\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"301\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-44738ea89bf5348438a30b56d497e52a_b.png\"/></figure>Home\nscreen quick actions are a convenient way to perform useful, app-specific\nactions right from the Home screen, using 3D Touch. Apply a little pressure to\nan app icon with your finger—more than you use for tap and hold—to see a list\nof available quick actions. Tap one to activate it. Mail, for example, includes\nquick actions that take you right to the Inbox or the VIP mailbox, initiate\nsearch, and create a new message. Each Home screen quick action includes a\ntitle, an icon on the left or right (depending on your app’s position on the\nhome screen), and an optional subtitle. The title and subtitle are always\nleft-aligned in left-to-right languages. Your app can even dynamically update\nits quick actions when new information is available. For example, Messages\nprovides quick actions for opening your most recent conversations.</p><p>主屏快速动作是一个通过3D Touch在主屏实现有用的、app特定动作的方便方式。用手指给app icon施加一点压力——而不是用长按——来查看可用快速动作列表。点击一个来激活它。例如，Mail邮件，包含立刻到达收件箱或VIP邮箱、启动搜索以及创建新邮件这几个快速动作。每个主屏快速动作包含一个标题，一个在左侧或右侧的图标（取决于app在主屏上的位置），以及一个可选的副标题。标题和副标题在从左开始书写的语言中总是左对齐。当新信息可达，您的app甚至可以动态更新快速启动。例如，Messages提供打开最新对话的快速动作。</p><p><strong>TIP</strong>Some\napps display a widget above their list of quick actions. For example, the\nStocks quick action list appears below a widget showing your current stock\nvalues. Consider implementing a widget to provide an even more engaging\nexperience. For widget design guidelines, see<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/widgets/%23home-screen-quick-action-widgets\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Home\nScreen Quick Action Widgets</a>.</p><p>有些app在快速启动列表上显示一个widget。例如，Stocks的快速动作列表显示在一个展示您当前股票价格的widget下面。考虑使用widget来提供更多互动的体验。Widget Design Guideline详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/widgets/%23home-screen-quick-action-widgets\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Home\nScreen Quick Action Widgets</a>】</p><p><strong>Create\nquick actions for compelling, high-value tasks.</strong> For example, Maps lets people search near their current location\nor get directions home without first opening the Maps app. Every app should\nenable at least one useful quick action; you can provide a total of four.</p><p>为更吸引人更有价值的任务创建快速动作。例如，地图让人们不用打开app就能搜索当前位置附近或者获得回家方向。每个app应该启用至少一个有用的快速动作；最多能提供四个。</p><p><strong>Avoid using quick\nactions to ease navigation.</strong> If it’s\ndifficult or time-consuming to visit important areas in your app, first fix\nyour navigation to work well for everyone. Next, focus on providing quick\nactions that enable useful, creative tasks.</p><p>避免使用快速动作来简化导航。如果在您的app中难以访问重要区域，首先应该修改导航以为每个人良好工作。然后，集中精力为快速动作提供启动有用的有创意的任务。</p><p><strong>Avoid making\nunpredictable changes to quick actions.</strong> Dynamic quick actions are a great way to keep actions relevant.\nFor example, it may make sense to update quick actions based on the current\nlocation or recent activities in your app, time of day, or changes in settings.\nHowever, actions shouldn’t change in ways that are unpredictable or confusing.</p><p>避免对快速动作做出不可预计的改变。动态快速动作是一个保持动作相关的好方法。例如， 基于当前位置或者app中的最近活动，一天中的时间，或者设置更改来更新快速动作可能会有意义。然而，动作不应该以不可预料或者让人困惑的方式改变。</p><p><strong>Provide a succinct\ntitle for each quick action.</strong> An\naction’s title should instantly communicate the results of the action; for\nexample, “Directions Home,” “Create New Contact,” and “New Message.” If you\nneed to give more context, provide a subtitle too. Mail uses subtitles to\nindicate whether there are unread messages in the inbox and VIP folder. Don’t include\nyour app name or any extraneous information in the title or subtitle, keep the\ntext short to avoid truncation, and take localization into account as you write\nthe text.</p><p>为每个快速动作提供一个简洁的标题。一个动作标题应该立刻传达出动作的结果；例如，“导航至家里”“创建新联系人”，以及“新信息”。如果您需要给出更多上下文，提供一个副标题吧。Mail用副标题来显示收件箱和VIP信箱里是否有未读邮件。在标题和副标题里不要包含app的名字或者任何外来信息，文本短一点避免被截短，并且当您撰写文本时将本地化带入考虑。</p><p><strong>Don’t use quick actions\nfor notification.</strong> People\nexpect to receive notifications from apps in other ways. See<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/features/notifications/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Notifications</a>.</p><p>不要用快速动作作为通知。人们期望通过其他方式受到app通知。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/features/notifications/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Notifications</a>.】</p><p><strong>Provide a recognizable\nicon for each quick action.</strong> Whenever\npossible, use the familiar system icons. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/graphics/system-icons/%23quick-action-icons\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Quick Action Icons</a>. If you\ndesign your own icons, download the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/design/downloads/Quick-Action-Guides.zip\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Quick Action Icon\nTemplate</a> and\nfollow the guidelines in<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/graphics/custom-icons/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Custom Icons</a>.</p><p>为每个快速启动提供一个辨识度高的icon。可能的话，使用熟悉的系统icon。查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/graphics/system-icons/%23quick-action-icons\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Quick Action Icons</a>.】如果您设计自己的icon，下载【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/design/downloads/Quick-Action-Guides.zip\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Quick Action Icon\nTemplate</a>】并且遵守<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/graphics/custom-icons/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Custom Icons</a>.的guideline</p><p><strong>Don&#39;t use an emoji in\nplace of an icon.</strong> Emojis\ndon&#39;t align properly with right-aligned text. Also, emojis are full color,\nwhereas quick action icons are monochromatic.</p><p>不要用emoji代替icon。Emoji与右对齐文本无法正确对齐。此外，emoji是全彩色的，而快速动作icon是单色的。</p><h2><b>Messaging信息</b></h2><p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/messaging/%23imessage-apps\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">iMessage apps</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/messaging/%23stickers\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Sticker packs</a> are messaging extensions that let people share content with\nfriends, communicate expressively, and share collaborative experiences.</p><p><a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/messaging/%23imessage-apps\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">iMessage apps</a> 和<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/messaging/%23stickers\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Sticker packs</a>是让人们与朋友分享内容，充分表达交流，分享合作体验的信息扩展。</p><h3>iMessage Apps</h3><p>An iMessage app\nprovides an interactive experience within the context of a Messages\nconversation. iMessage apps enable people to share data and media, collaborate\non shared tasks, and play games with one another.</p><p>iMessage app在Messages对话的情境下提供交互体验。iMessage\napp使人们能够分享数据和媒体，在分享的任务上合作，和领一个人玩游戏。</p><p><strong>Design an intuitive\ninterface.</strong> If your iMessage\napp provides static content, such as text, photos, or videos, make sure it’s\neasy for people to browse and select items for insertion into the conversation.\nIf your app is interactive, such as a multiplayer game board or collaborative\ntakeout order, make sure its functionality is useful and understandable.</p><p>设计一个直觉界面。如果iMessage\napp提供静态内容，例如文本，照片或者视频，确保对于人们来说浏览和选择插入对话的项目很容易。如果app是可交互的，例如一个多人游戏板或者协作外卖订单，确保它的功能是有用而且可理解的。</p><p><strong>Provide focused\ncontent.</strong> For\nclarity and ease of use, each messaging extension should have a single focus.\nDon’t try to design one app that combines both stickers and ridesharing, for\nexample.</p><p>提供重点内容。为了清晰和易用性，每个信息扩展应该有一个重点。例如，不要试图设计一个结合贴纸和共享乘车的app。</p><p><strong>Provide a fun,\ncollaborative experience.</strong> iMessage\napps are typically used in the context of fast-paced, informal conversations\nbetween two or more people. Creatively leverage this environment to encourage\nback-and-forth participation through sharing, editing, or augmenting content.\nIf all parties are using the app together, content updates occur in real time.</p><p>提供有趣的，合作的经验。iMessage\napp通常用于快速的，几个人的非正式对话这种情境下。创造性地利用这种环境，通过分享、编辑或者增强内容来鼓励反复参与。如果所有参与方一起使用这个APP，内容会实时更新。</p><p><strong>Highlight interesting\niOS app content.</strong> Extend\nthe functionality of your iOS app by surfacing its content in the Messages\nspace. Think about what kinds of information people might want to share and how\nthey can interact with your app within the context of an active conversation.</p><p>突出有趣的iOS app 内容。通过在Messages控件中显示他的内容扩展iOS app的功能。考虑人们可能想要分享何种信息，他们能如何在主动对话中与app交互。</p><p><strong>Inset content to avoid\ncropping.</strong> Your\napp&#39;s content is presented in message bubbles with rounded corners, so don&#39;t\nput essential information in the corners.</p><p>插入内容以避免裁剪。App的内容呈现在圆角的信息泡泡中，所以不要将重要信息放在角落里。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0479976834cfa16c15a39b107220855f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"256\" data-rawheight=\"570\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"256\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;256&#39; height=&#39;570&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"256\" data-rawheight=\"570\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"256\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-0479976834cfa16c15a39b107220855f_b.png\"/></figure><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b8e195190bfa56bfd71e6d508d842ba2_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"257\" data-rawheight=\"566\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"257\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;257&#39; height=&#39;566&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"257\" data-rawheight=\"566\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"257\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b8e195190bfa56bfd71e6d508d842ba2_b.png\"/></figure>Differentiate compact and expanded views.</b> Your\napp appears in a compact view below a conversation. This view should visually\ndistinguish your app from other apps and provide access to frequently used\nfeatures. People can also open your app in an expanded view to access advanced\nfeatures or see more options at once. Note that horizontal scrolling isn’t\npermitted in the compact view.</p><p>区分紧凑视图和扩展视图。App在对话下显示为紧凑视图。这个视图应该在视觉上将您的app同其他app区分开并且提供获取常用特征的入口。人们也可以在扩展视图中打开app来获取高级特征或者一次看到更多选项。注意在紧凑视图中横向滚动被禁用。</p><p><b>Allow text editing in the expanded view only.</b> The\ncompact view is roughly the same height as the keyboard. To ensure that users\ncan see what they’re editing, allow text entry only in the expanded view.</p><p>只允许在扩展视图中编辑文字。紧凑视图大概跟键盘一样高。为了确保用户能看到他们在编辑什么，只有在扩展视图中才能输入文本。</p><h3>Stickers贴纸</h3><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-33cdac289ce6b957869a80c3ef91fbc4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"296\" data-rawheight=\"601\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"296\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;296&#39; height=&#39;601&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"296\" data-rawheight=\"601\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"296\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-33cdac289ce6b957869a80c3ef91fbc4_b.png\"/></figure>Stickers offer a\nfun, engaging way for people to express themselves in a Messages conversation\nwithout typing or using emojis. A sticker is an image or an animation that can\nbe sent or placed on messages, photos, and other stickers to add emphasis and\ncommunicate emotion.</p><p>在Messages对话中，贴纸为人们提供有趣的吸引人的方式来表达自我，又不用打字或者使用emoji。贴纸是能被发送的或者放在信息上、照片上、以及其他贴纸上来强调、交流情绪的一张图或者一个动画。</p><p><strong>Design for\nexpressiveness.</strong> People\nuse stickers to visually convey moods and reactions. Strive to deliver stickers\nthat connect with people at an emotional level. Consider incorporating imagery,\nwords, and phrases to add new dimensions to conversations.</p><p>为了表达而设计。人们用贴纸视觉化地传达情绪和反应。力求发送与人们在情感上有联系的贴纸。考虑包含意象，词语，以及短语来为对话添加新的维度。</p><p><strong>Think globally.</strong> Messaging is a universal form of communication. Aim for stickers\nthat have broad, international appeal.</p><p>放眼全球。短信是一个通用的交流方式。瞄准具有广泛的的国际吸引力的贴纸。</p><p><strong>Use descriptive image\nnames or provide alternative text labels.</strong> Although they aren’t visible onscreen, image names and\nalternative text labels let VoiceOver audibly describe stickers, making\nnavigation easier for people with visual impairments.</p><p>使用描述性的图片名或提供替代文字标签。尽管他们在屏幕上不可见，图片名和替代文字标签让VoiceOver用声音描述贴纸，让视障人群导航更容易。</p><p><strong>Add vitality through\nanimation.</strong> Although\nstickers can be static images, animated stickers are a great way to impart\nenergy in a conversation. Be sure to use a frame rate high enough to keep\nmotion fluid.</p><p>通过动画增加活力。尽管贴纸可以是静态图片，动画贴纸是一个在对话中传到能量的好方法。确认使用足够高的帧速率来保证动作流畅。</p><p><strong>Test placement\npossibilities.</strong> Users can\nscale, rotate, and place stickers over parts of a conversation. Make sure your\nstickers are legible against different colors and imagery, regardless of their\nposition or size.</p><p>测试放置可能性。用户能在对话的部分上缩放，旋转和放置贴纸。确认您的贴纸是清晰可辨的不同颜色和图像，无论位置或大小。</p><p><strong>Consider using vibrant colors and\ntransparency.</strong> Vivid\ncolors add richness and excitement to a conversation. Transparency allows\nmeaningful placement of stickers onto messages, photos and other stickers.</p><p>考虑使用充满活力的颜色和透明度。生动的颜色为对话添加丰富度和激情。透明度允许在邮件，照片和其他贴纸上有意义地放置贴纸。</p><h4>Sticker Sizes贴纸尺寸</h4><p>Messages supports three sticker sizes,\nwhich are displayed in a grid-based browser. Pick a size that works best for\nyour content and prepare all of your stickers at that size.</p><p>Messages支持三种贴纸尺寸，显示在网格基础的浏览器中。选择一个最适合您的内容的尺寸并且用那种尺寸准备所有贴纸。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1be44c32bb59a7a3a853de66a168996e_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"293\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1be44c32bb59a7a3a853de66a168996e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;553&#39; height=&#39;293&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"293\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1be44c32bb59a7a3a853de66a168996e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1be44c32bb59a7a3a853de66a168996e_b.png\"/></figure>Scale stickers appropriately.</strong> Although Messages scales larger stickers down if necessary, it’s\nbest to provide prescaled stickers for optimal quality and performance.</p><p>适当地缩放贴纸。尽管Messages在必要时将大贴纸缩小，最好提供最优质量最佳表现的预设贴纸。</p><p><strong>Be mindful of file size\nrestrictions.</strong> For\nefficiency, each individual sticker may not exceed 500KB. Note that Xcode saves\nPNG animations using a 24-bit palette, which may lead to larger than expected\nfile sizes.</p><p>小心文件大小限制。为了效率，每个独立贴纸不应该超过500KB。注意Xcode用24色存储PNG动画，这可能导致超出预期的文件大小。</p><h4>Sticker\nFormats贴纸格式</h4><p>Messages supports stickers in the\nfollowing file formats:</p><h3><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0e43a18ba0a60302f67c7de1306716ae_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"158\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0e43a18ba0a60302f67c7de1306716ae_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;553&#39; height=&#39;158&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"158\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0e43a18ba0a60302f67c7de1306716ae_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-0e43a18ba0a60302f67c7de1306716ae_b.png\"/></figure>iMessage App and Sticker Pack Icons</h3><p>Like iOS apps, iMessage apps and sticker\npacks need recognizable app icons.</p><p>像iOS app那样，iMessage\napp和贴纸宝需要辨识度高的app icon。</p><p><strong>Keep the background simple and\nprovide a single focus point.</strong> Design an\nicon with a single, centered point that captures attention at a glance. Include\na simple background that doesn’t overpower other icons.</p><p>保持背景简单并且提供一个重点。设计有一个单独的中心点的icon，能迅速抓人眼球。包含一个不会压过其他icon的简单背景。</p><p><strong>Keep icon corners square.</strong> The system applies a mask that rounds icon corners\nautomatically.</p><p>让Icon角是方的。系统会自动使用一个遮罩，让icon角变圆。</p><p><strong>Provide different sized icons.</strong> Your icon appears in the App Store, Messages, notifications, and\nSettings. To ensure that your icon looks great in any context and on any\ndevice, you can provide variations of your icon in the following sizes:</p><p>提供不同尺寸的图标。您的图标在App Store， Messages，通知和Settings出现。为了确认您的icon在任何情境任何设备下看起来都很棒，您可以提供一下尺寸的图标变种：</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7ab790cc7a695e268aac9c5b1ad9e62e_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"93\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7ab790cc7a695e268aac9c5b1ad9e62e_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;553&#39; height=&#39;93&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"93\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7ab790cc7a695e268aac9c5b1ad9e62e_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-7ab790cc7a695e268aac9c5b1ad9e62e_b.png\"/></figure>For additional guidance on designing\ngreat app icons, much of which can be applied to iMessage app and sticker pack\nicons, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/graphics/app-icon/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Icon</a>.</p><p>设计图标详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/graphics/app-icon/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Icon</a>.】</p><p>To download an iMessage app and sticker\npack icon Photoshop template, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/resources/%23templates\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Resources</a>.</p><p>下载iMessage app和贴纸包图标Photoshop模板，查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/resources/%23templates\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Resources</a>.】</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/messages\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">The Messages Framework</a>.</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/messages\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">The Messages Framework</a>.】</p><h2><b>Photo Editing照片编辑</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9e9fac7d1c6876f643941b9ab0cc20c3_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"215\" data-rawheight=\"431\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"215\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;215&#39; height=&#39;431&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"215\" data-rawheight=\"431\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"215\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9e9fac7d1c6876f643941b9ab0cc20c3_b.png\"/></figure>Photo editing extensions let people\nmodify photos and videos within the Photos app by applying filters or making\nother changes. Edits are always saved in the Photos app as new files, safely\npreserving the original versions.</p><p>To access a photo editing extension, a\nphoto must be in edit mode. While in edit mode, tapping the extension icon in\nthe toolbar displays an action menu of available editing extensions. Selecting\none displays the extension’s interface in a modal view containing a navigation\nbar. Dismissing this view confirms and saves the edit, or cancels it and returns\nto the Photos app.</p><p>照片编辑扩展让人们在Photos中通过使用滤镜或作出其他调整，来调整照片和视频。编辑后的照片总是作为新文件存储在Photos里，出于安全考虑保留源文件。</p><p>为了获取照片编辑扩展，照片必须在编辑模式。当在编辑状态下，在工具栏点击扩展按钮显示一个可用编辑扩展动作菜单。选取一个包含导航栏的模态视图中显示扩展的界面。关闭这个视图会确认并且保存编辑，或者取消它并返回Photos。</p><p><strong>Confirm cancellation of edits.</strong> Editing a photo or video can be time consuming. If someone taps\nthe Cancel button, don’t immediately discard their changes. Ask them to confirm\nthat they really want to cancel, and inform them that any edits will be lost\nafter cancellation. There’s no need to show this confirmation if no edits have\nbeen made yet.</p><p>确认编辑取消。编辑一个照片或者视频可能很花时间。如果有人点击取消按钮，不要立刻丢弃更改。让用户确认他们真的想取消，并且通知他们任何编辑在取消之后都会丢失。如果没有做任何编辑就没必要显示确认信息。</p><p><strong>Don’t provide a custom navigation\nbar.</strong> Your\nextension loads within a modal view that already includes a navigation bar.\nProviding a second navigation bar is confusing and takes space away from the\ncontent being edited.</p><p>不要提供自定义导航条。您的扩展在一个已经包含导航条的模态视图内加载。提供第二个导航条会让人困惑并且占据编辑内容的位置。</p><p><strong>Let\npeople preview edits.</strong> It’s hard\nto approve an edit if you can’t see what it looks like. Let people see the\nresult of their work before closing your extension and returning to the Photos\napp.</p><p>让人们预览编辑结果。如果您不能看到编辑成什么样，就很难确认它。让人们在关闭扩展回到Photos之前看到工作的成果。</p><p><strong>Use your app icon for your photo\nediting extension icon.</strong> This\ninstills confidence that the extension is in fact provided by your app.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/Photos.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Photo Editing</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Extension\nProgramming Guide</a>.</p><p>使用app icon作为照片编辑扩展的icon。这使得人们相信该扩展实际上是由您的应用程序提供的。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/Photos.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Photo Editing</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Extension\nProgramming Guide</a>.】</p><h2><b>Sharing and Actions分享和动作</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9148286a262e9959763109863e483a62_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"299\" data-rawheight=\"598\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"299\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;299&#39; height=&#39;598&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"299\" data-rawheight=\"598\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"299\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-9148286a262e9959763109863e483a62_b.png\"/></figure>Share extensions provide a convenient\nway to share information from the current context with apps, social media\naccounts, and other services. Action extensions let people initiate\ncontent-specific tasks, such as adding a bookmark, copying a link, or saving an\nimage. People access share extensions and action extensions by tapping an\nAction button in an app to display an activity view. An activity view shows\nonly extensions relevant to the current context. You wouldn’t see text\nmanipulation actions while editing a video, for example. Within an activity\nview, share extensions are listed above action extensions.</p><p>分享扩展程序提供了一种方便的方法，可从当前情境中与应用程序，社交媒体帐户和其他服务共享信息。 动作扩展可让用户启动特定内容的任务，例如添加书签，复制链接或保存图片。用户通过点击应用中的操作按钮来获取活动视图，从而访问共享扩展程序和操作扩展程序。 活动视图仅显示与当前情境相关的扩展。 例如，在编辑视频时，您将看不到文本处理操作。 在活动视图中，共享扩展位于操作附加信息上方。</p><p><strong>Enable a single, focused task.</strong> An extension isn’t a mini-app. It performs a narrowly scoped\ntask related to the current context.</p><p>启用单个集中任务。 扩展程序不是一个小app。 它执行与当前上下文相关的小范围任务。</p><p><strong>Craft a familiar interface.</strong> For share extensions, the system-provided composition view is\nfamiliar and provides a consistent sharing experience throughout the system.\nUse it whenever possible. For action extensions, include your app name, or\ndesign an interface that’s recognizable and feels like a natural extension of\nyour app.</p><p>制作一个熟悉的界面。 对于共享扩展，系统提供的组合视图是熟悉的，并在整个系统中提供一致的共享体验。 尽可能使用它。 对于动作扩展程序，请添加您的应用程序名称，或者设计一个可识别的界面，就像app的自然扩展一样。</p><p><strong>Streamline and limit interaction.</strong> The best extensions let people perform a task in just a few\nsteps. For example, a share extension might immediately post an image to a\nsocial media account with a single tap. Only provide an interface when\nnecessary.</p><p>精简并限制交互。最好的扩展能让人们在几步之内执行操作任务。例如，分享扩展能只点击一下就将照片发到社交媒体账户上。只提供必要的界面。</p><p><strong>Avoid placing modal views above\nyour extension.</strong> Extensions\nare displayed within a modal view by default. While an alert might make sense\nabove an extension, avoid layering additional modal views.</p><p>避免在扩展上放置模态视图。默认状态下扩展被显示在模态视图中。因为警报可能在扩展上有意义，避免堆叠附加的模态视图。</p><p><strong>Use your main app to denote the\nprogress of lengthy operations.</strong> An activity view should dismiss immediately after initiating\nsharing or an action. Time-consuming tasks should continue in the background,\nand your main app should provide some way to check the status of these tasks.\nDon’t use notifications for this. People don’t want to see a notification every\ntime a task completes, although it’s fine to notify them if there’s a problem.</p><p>用主app表示长操作的进度。活动视图在启动分享或其他动作之后应该立刻关闭。花时间的任务应该在后台继续，并且在主app上应该提供一些查看这些任物的方法。不要为了这个用通知。尽管如果有问题的话用来通知人们是很好的，但是他们不想在每次任务完成时看到一个通知。</p><p><strong>Use a template image for an action\nextension icon.</strong> A\ntemplate image uses a mask to create an icon. Use black and white with\nappropriate transparency and antialiasing, and don’t include a drop shadow.\nTemplate images should be centered in an area measuring about 70px by 70px.</p><p>为动作扩展icon使用模板图片。模板图片用遮罩创建icon。用带有适当透明度抗锯齿的黑色和白色，不要用投影。模板图片应该居中在测量约70px\nX70px的区域。</p><p><strong>TIP</strong>Share\nextensions automatically use your app icon, instilling confidence that the\nextension is in fact provided by your app.</p><p>分享扩展自动使用app icon。这使得人们相信该扩展实际上是由您的应用程序提供的。</p><p>For additional guidelines, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/activity-views/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Activity Views</a>. For\nimplementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/Share.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Share</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/Action.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Action</a>in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Extension\nProgramming Guide</a>.</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/activity-views/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Activity Views</a>. For\nimplementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/Share.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Share</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/Action.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Action</a>in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Extension\nProgramming Guide</a>.】</p><h2><b>Widgets</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6b7f06ddffcf70c091d9363b0ac195d2_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"575\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6b7f06ddffcf70c091d9363b0ac195d2_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;553&#39; height=&#39;575&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"553\" data-rawheight=\"575\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"553\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6b7f06ddffcf70c091d9363b0ac195d2_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-6b7f06ddffcf70c091d9363b0ac195d2_b.png\"/></figure>A widget is an extension that displays\na small amount of timely, useful information or app-specific functionality. For\nexample, the News widget shows top headlines. Calendar provides two widgets,\none that shows today’s events and one that shows what’s up next. Notes lets you\npreview recent notes and quickly create new notes, reminders, photos, and\ndrawings. Widgets are highly customizable and can contain buttons, text, layout\ncustomizations, images, and more.</p><p>Widget是一种显示少量及时，有用信息或应用程序特定功能的扩展。 例如，“新闻”窗口小部件显示顶部标题。 日历提供了两个小部件，一个显示今天的事件，一个显示下个事件。 Notes可让您预览最近的笔记，并快速创建新笔记，提醒，照片和绘图。 Widget是高度可定制的，可以包含按钮，文本，布局自定义，图像等。</p><p>Widgets appear above the quick action\nlist when you apply pressure to an app icon on the Home screen using 3D Touch.\nPeople also add the widgets they care about to the Search screen, which is\naccessed by swiping to the right on the Home screen and the Lock screen. Your\ngoal should be to design a widget that people want to add to the Search screen.</p><p>当您使用3D Touch在主屏幕上对应用程序图标施加压力时，widget会显示在快速操作列表上方。 用户还可以将他们关心的widget添加到搜索屏，通过在主屏和锁屏上向右滑动即可访问。 您的目标应该是设计人们想要添加到搜索屏的widget。</p><p><strong>Design a great glanceable\nexperience.</strong> People\nuse widgets to get brief updates and perform very simple tasks, so it’s\nessential to deliver the right amount of information and interactivity.\nWherever possible, provide tasks that can be completed in a single tap. Panning\nand scrolling within widgets isn’t supported.</p><p>设计超棒的一瞥之间的体验。 人们用widget来获取简短更新，执行非常简单的任务，因此，提供适当数量的信息和交互至关重要。 尽可能提供一次点就能完成的任务。 Widget中不支持平移和滚动。</p><p><strong>Show content quickly.</strong> People spend very little time looking at widgets and shouldn’t\nneed to wait for content to load. Cache information locally so you can always\nshow recent information while getting updates.</p><p>快速显示内容。 人们用很少的时间查看widget，并且不需要等待内容加载。 在本地缓存信息，以便您可以始终在获取更新时显示最近信息。</p><p><strong>Provide ample margins and padding.</strong> Avoid extending content to the edges of a widget. In general,\nprovide a margin of at least a few pixels between each edge and the content.\nUse the app icon at the top of your widget for alignment guidance. Content\ntends to work well when lined up with the center of this icon. If your app\noffers a grid-style layout, make sure you provide sufficient and equal padding\nbetween grid items. If possible, limit grids of icons and buttons to four per\nrow.</p><p>提供足够的边距和填充。 避免将内容扩展到widget边缘。 总的来说，在每个边缘和内容之间提供至少几像素的边缘。 使用窗口小部件顶部的应用图标进行对齐指导。 当与此图标的中心对齐时，内容会工作得很好。 如果您的应用提供网格样式的布局，请确保在网格项之间提供足够和相等的填充。 如果可能，将图标和按钮的网格限制为每行四个。</p><p><strong>Be adaptable.</strong> The width of a widget varies, depending on the device and\norientation. The height and information displayed by a widget depends on\nwhether it’s collapsed or expanded (not all widgets support expansion). A\ncollapsed widget is the height of roughly two and a half table rows. An\nexpanded widget is ideally no taller than the height of the screen. The quick\naction list only shows widgets in a collapsed state. When collapsed, a widget\nshows essential information that can stand alone. When expanded, a widget shows\nadditional information that enhances the primary information. The Weather\nwidget, for example, shows the current weather conditions when collapsed, but\nadds the hourly forecast when expanded.</p><p>适应性强。 widget的宽度根据设备和方向而异。 widget显示的高度和信息取决于窗口是否折叠或展开（并非所有widget都支持展开）。 折叠的widget高度大约是两个半表格行。 理想状态下，展开的widget不比屏幕的高度高。 快速动作列表仅显示处于折叠状态的widget。 当折叠时，widget显示独立存在的基本信息。 展开时，widget显示增强主要信息的其他信息。 例如，“天气”widget折叠时显示当前天气状况，但在展开时添加每小时预报。</p><p><strong>Avoid customizing the background\nof a widget.</strong> The light,\nblurred widget background provided by the system is designed for consistency\nand legibility. Use it whenever possible. Never use a photo as a background, as\nit may clash with the Lock and Home screen wallpaper.</p><p>避免自定义widget背景。 系统提供的浅色的，模糊的widget背景是为了一致性和易读性而设计。 尽可能使用它。 切勿用照片作为背景，因为它可能会与锁屏和主屏壁纸发生冲突。</p><p><strong>In general, use the system font in\nblack or dark gray for text.</strong> The\nsystem font is designed for legibility, and dark colors work well with the\nstandard widget background.</p><p>总的来说，为文本使用黑色或深灰色的系统字体。系统字体为可读性而设计，并且深色与标准widget背景很搭。</p><p><strong>When appropriate, let people jump\nto your app to do more.</strong> Your\nwidget should operate independently from your app. However, if people might\noccasionally need to do more than what your widget offers, make it easy to do\nso. Don’t include an “Open App” button that takes space away from your content.\nInstead, let people tap the content itself to see or edit it in your app. In\nthe Calendar widget, for example, you can tap an event to open it in the\nCalendar app. Never use your widget to open other apps.</p><p>适当时，让人们跳转到app完成更多任务。 widget应该独立于app运行。 但是，如果人们偶尔可能需要完成超出widget提供的任务，让这件事容易一点。 不要包含“启动app”按钮，这会占据内容的空间。 相反，让用户点击内容本身来在应用中查看或修改内容。 例如，在日历widget中，您可以点击某个事件，以便在日历应用中将其打开。 不要用widget打开其他app。</p><p><strong>Pick a good widget name.</strong> An app icon and a title appear above each widget’s content. In\ngeneral, your widget’s name should match your app’s name. If your app offers\nmultiple widgets, consider using your app name for the primary one and clear,\nconcise names for the others. If you use custom titles, consider prefixing them\nwith your app name. For example, the Maps widget for showing nearby locations\nis titled Maps Nearby. The inclusion of your app name instills confidence that\nthe widget is in fact provided by your app.</p><p>给widget选个好名字。 每个widget的内容上方都会显示一个app icon和标题。 一般来说，widget名称应该与app名称相符。 如果app提供多个widget，请考虑给有基本功能那个用app名，为其他应用提供清晰简洁的名称。 如果用自定义标题，请考虑为它们缀上app名。 例如，用于显示附近位置的地图widget名为“附近的地图”。 添加app名称会让您确信这个widget实际上是由app提供的。</p><p><strong>Let people know when\nauthentication adds value.</strong> If your\nwidget provides additional functionality when someone is logged into your app,\nmake sure people know about this. For example, an app that shows upcoming\nreservations might include a message that says “Sign into the app to view your\nreservations.” when people aren’t logged in.</p><p>让人们知道身份验证何时增加了价值。 如果widget在有人登入app时提供其他功能，请确定使用者知道这项功能。 例如，显示即将到来的预订的app可能会在人们未登录时显示“登录app以查看您的预订”的消息。</p><p><strong>Choose a widget for the quick\naction list.</strong> If your\napp has multiple widgets, pick one to appear in the quick action menu that\nappears when someone applies pressure to your app icon on the Home screen using\n3D Touch.</p><p>为快速动作列表选择一个widget。 如果app有多个widhet，当有人用3D Touch在主屏上对app图标施加压力时，请选择一个显示在快速动作菜单中。</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Extension\nProgramming Guide</a>.</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Conceptual/ExtensibilityPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Extension\nProgramming Guide</a>】</p>",

            "title": "iOS10人机界面指南：UI-控件（一）", 
            "content": "<h2><b>Buttons按钮</b></h2><p>Buttons initiate app-specific actions,\nhave customizable backgrounds, and can include a title or an icon. The system\nprovides a number of predefined button styles for most use cases. You can also\ndesign fully custom buttons.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>.</p><p>按钮启动app特定的动作，有自定义背景，并且能包含一个标题或者一个图标。系统为大多数使用场景提供一系列预定制的按钮风格。您也可以设计全部自定义的按钮。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>】</p><h3><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fda9367f504498b2745e2ac9287e65c6_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-fda9367f504498b2745e2ac9287e65c6_b.png\"/></figure>System\nButtons系统按钮</h3><p>System buttons often\nappear in navigation bars and toolbars, but may be used anywhere.</p><p>系统按钮经常出现在导航条和工具条上，但是可能被用在任何地方。</p><p><strong>Use verbs in titles.</strong> An action-specific title shows that a button is interactive and\nsays what happens when you tap it.</p><p>标题要使用动词。一个特定动作标题说明按钮是可交互的并且说明了当您点击它时会发生什么。</p><p><strong>Use title-case for\ntitles.</strong> Capitalize\nevery word except articles, coordinating conjunctions, and prepositions of four\nor fewer letters.</p><p>标题要首字母大写。除了冠词、并列连词以及四个或以下字母的介词之外的每个词都要大写首字母，</p><p><strong>Keep titles short.</strong> Overly long text can crowd your interface and may get truncated\non smaller screens.</p><p>标题要短。过长的文本会让界面看起来很挤，并且在小屏幕上可能被截短。</p><p><strong>Consider adding a border or a\nbackground only when necessary.</strong> By default, a system button has no border or background. In some\ncontent areas, however, a border or background is necessary to denote\ninteractivity. In the Phone app, bordered number keys reinforce the traditional\nmodel of making a call, and the background of the Call button provides an\neye-catching target that’s easy to hit.</p><p>For implementation details, see the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypesystem\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeSystem</a> button type of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>.</p><p>只在必要时考虑添加描边或者背景。默认情况下，系统按钮是没有描边或者背景的。然而，在某些内容区域，为了描述交互性，描边或者背景是必要的。在Phone电话 app中，描边的数字键加强了传统的打电话形式，Call呼叫按钮的背景提供了吸引眼球的目标，很容易点击。</p><h3>Detail\nDisclosure Buttons详情按钮</h3><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ee2498e0fae7bafd8d9e74ec782ff89f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ee2498e0fae7bafd8d9e74ec782ff89f_b.png\"/></figure>A Detail Disclosure\nbutton opens a view—typically, a modal view—containing additional information\nor functionality related to a specific item onscreen. Although you can use them\nin any type of view, Detail Disclosure buttons are commonly used in tables to\naccess information about specific rows.</p><p>详情按钮会打开一个视图——通常是模态视图——包含附加信息或者屏幕上特定项目的相关功能。尽管您可以在任何一种视图里使用它们，详情按钮通常用在表格中，来获取关于某特定行的信息。</p><p><strong>Use Detail Disclosure\nbuttons appropriately in tables.</strong>When a Detail\nDisclosure button is present in a table row, tapping the button shows\nadditional information. Tapping elsewhere selects the row or results in\napp-defined behavior. If you want people to tap the entire row to see\nadditional detail, don’t use a Detail Disclosure button. Instead, use a detail\ndisclosure accessory control, which appears as a chevron. See<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellaccessorytype\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellAccessoryType</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.</p><p>For implementation details, see the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypedetaildisclosure\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeDetailDisclosure</a> button type of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>.</p><p>在表格中恰当使用详情按钮。当详情按钮显示在表格行中，点击按钮来显示附加信息。点击其他地方选择该行或者导致app定义的行为。如果您想让人们点击整行来看到附加详情，不要使用详情按钮。用看上去像箭头的详情披露附件来代替。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypedetaildisclosure\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeDetailDisclosure</a> button type of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>.】</p><h3>Info Buttons信息按钮</h3><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-649a547f8f661233086b48b179c36b1c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-649a547f8f661233086b48b179c36b1c_b.png\"/></figure>An Info button reveals configuration details about an app,\nsometimes on the back of the current view, after flipping the view around. Info\nbuttons come in two styles—light and dark. Pick the style that best coordinates\nwith your app’s design and doesn’t get lost onscreen.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see the<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypeinfolight\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeInfoLight</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypeinfodark\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeInfoDark</a>button\ntypes of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>.</p><p>一个信息按钮揭开app的配置细节，有时候在当前视图的背面，在翻转视图之后。信息按钮有两种风格，浅色的和深色的。挑选与您app设计最相配的那种，并且不要在屏幕上迷失？？？？</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypeinfolight\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeInfoLight</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypeinfodark\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeInfoDark</a>button\ntypes of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>.】</p><h3>Add\nContact Buttons添加联系人按钮</h3><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ef8e0f25c0b01b6d3101bc846166fd23_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-ef8e0f25c0b01b6d3101bc846166fd23_b.png\"/></figure>Users can tap an Add\nContact button to browse a list of existing contacts and to select one for\ninsertion into a text field or other view. In Mail, for example, you can tap\nthe Add Contact button in the To field of a message to select a recipient from\nyour list of contacts.</p><p>用户可以点击添加联系人按钮来浏览一系列已经保存的联系人并且选一个来插入文本域或者其他视图。例如，在Mail邮件中，您可以在一条信息的To区域点击添加联系人按钮来从一列联系人中选择收件人。</p><p><strong>Allow keyboard entry in\naddition to the Add Contact button.</strong> The Add Contact button provides an alternative, not a\nreplacement, to typing contact information. It’s fine to provide it as a\nshortcut for adding existing contacts, but let people enter contact information\nwith the keyboard too.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see the<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypecontactadd\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeContactAdd</a> button type of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>.</p><p>除了添加联系人按钮之外，允许键盘输入。添加联系人按钮提供一个选择，而不是代替打字输入联系人信息。为添加已存的联系人提供捷径是好的，但也要让人能用键盘输入联系人信息。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibuttontype/uibuttontypecontactadd\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButtonTypeContactAdd</a> button type of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibutton\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIButton</a>.】</p><h2><b>Edit Menus编辑菜单</b></h2><p>People can touch and\nhold or double-tap an element in a text field, a text view, a web view, or an\nimage view to select content and reveal edit options, such as Copy and Paste.</p><p>人们可以在文本域、文本视图、网页视图或者图像视图里长按或者双击元素来选择内容并且揭开编辑选项，比如复制和粘贴。</p><p><strong>Show appropriate\ncommands for the current context.</strong>By default, the\noptions include Cut, Copy, Paste, Select, Select All, and Delete commands, any\nof which can optionally be disabled. If nothing is selected, the menu shouldn’t\nshow options that require a selection, such as Copy or Cut. Similarly, the menu\nshouldn’t have a Select option if something is already selected.</p><p>为当前情景显示适当的命令。默认情况下，选项包括剪切，复制，粘贴，选择，选择所有以及删除命令，这些都可以关掉。如果什么都没选，菜单就不会显示需要选择的选项，比如复制和剪切。同样，如果已经选中了什么，菜单就不应该有选择这个选项。</p><p><strong>Let people use the standard\ngestures to access edit options.</strong> People expect to reveal the menu by touching and holding or\ndouble-tapping content, such as text or a photo. Your app should respond to\nboth gestures. You can define what becomes selected when someone double-taps.\nIn a text view, selection by word should be the default.</p><p>让人们使用标准手势来获取编辑选项。人们期待通过长按或者双击内容来揭开菜单，比如文本或者照片。App应该对两种手势都作出回应。您可以定义当某人双击时什么被选中。在文本视图中，选区应该默认以词为单位。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-90ef48690a8189e8ae149ea06dab961a_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-90ef48690a8189e8ae149ea06dab961a_b.png\"/></figure>Adjust\nplacement of edit options, if necessary.</strong> By default, the menu is positioned above or below the insertion\npoint or selection, depending on available space, and includes a pointer to the\nrelated content. Although you can’t change the shape of the menu, its position\nis configurable—you can prevent it from covering important content or parts of\nyour interface.</p><p>必要时，调整编辑选项的位置。默认情况下，菜单被放在插入点或者选区的上面或下面，取决于可用空间，并且包含一个指向相关内容的箭头。尽管您不能改变菜单的形状，它的位置是可调整的——您可以让它表面覆盖界面的重要内容或重要部分。</p><p><strong>Don’t implement other controls\nwith the same functionality as the edit menu.</strong> Providing multiple ways to initiate an operation results in an\ninconsistent user experience and leads to confusion. If your app lets people\nuse the menu to copy content, for example, don’t implement a copy button too.</p><p>不要用其他相同功能的控件作为编辑菜单。为启动一个动作提供多种方式会导致不一致的用户体验并且导致困惑。例如，如果app能让人们用菜单拷贝内容，那就不要使用拷贝按钮。</p><p><strong>Allow potentially useful\nnoneditable text to be selected and copied.</strong> People often want to add static content, such as an image label\nor social media status, to an email, a note, or a web search.</p><p>允许可能有用的不可编辑的文本被选择和拷贝。人们经常想给邮件、笔记或者网页搜索添加静态内容，比如一个图像标签或者社交媒体状态</p><p><strong>Don’t add edit options to a\nbutton.</strong> If you do\nthis, people attempting to reveal the options will end up activating the button\ninstead.</p><p>不要为按钮添加编辑选项。如果您这样做，人们会试图用激活按钮替代揭开选项。</p><p><strong>Make edit operations undoable.</strong> The menu doesn’t require confirmation before its actions are\nperformed. Because someone could change their mind after performing an\noperation, always implement undo and redo support.</p><p>让编辑操作可以撤销。在动作执行前，菜单不会请求确认。因为有的人会在执行操作之后改变主意，请一直支持撤销和重做功能。</p><p><strong>Expand edit options with useful\ncustom commands.</strong> You can\nadd value by providing additional app-specific commands. Like the standard\ncommands, any custom commands should operate on selected text or objects.</p><p>用有用的自定义命令扩展编辑选项。您可以通过提供附加的app特有命令增添价值。就像标准命令那样，任何自定义命令应该在选中的文本或物体上操作。</p><p><strong>Show custom commands after the\nsystem-provided ones.</strong> Don’t\nintersperse custom commands with the system-provided ones, which are well known\nand frequently used.</p><p>在系统提供的命令之后显示自定义命令。不要让系统提供的命令成为自定义命令的点缀，系统命令为人所熟知并且经常使用。</p><p><strong>Minimize the number of custom\ncommands.</strong> Don’t\noverwhelm people with too many choices.</p><p>最小化自定义命令的数量。不要让人们被太多选择压倒。</p><p><strong>Keep custom command names short.</strong> Command names should be verbs or short verb phrases that\nsuccinctly describe the action to be performed. Use title-style\ncapitalization—capitalize every word except articles, coordinating conjunctions,\nand prepositions of four or fewer letters.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/StringsTextFonts/Conceptual/TextAndWebiPhoneOS/UsingCopy%2CCut%2CandPasteOperations/UsingCopy%2CCut%2CandPasteOperations.html%23//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40009542-CH11-SW1\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Copy, Cut, and Paste\nOperations</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/StringsTextFonts/Conceptual/TextAndWebiPhoneOS/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Text Programming\nGuide for iOS</a> and<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uimenucontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIMenuController</a>.</p><p>自定义命令的名字要短。命令名应该是动词或者简洁描述即将执行动作的动词短语。除了冠词、并列连词、以及四个字母以下的介词外，都要首字母大写。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/StringsTextFonts/Conceptual/TextAndWebiPhoneOS/UsingCopy%2CCut%2CandPasteOperations/UsingCopy%2CCut%2CandPasteOperations.html%23//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40009542-CH11-SW1\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Copy, Cut, and Paste\nOperations</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/StringsTextFonts/Conceptual/TextAndWebiPhoneOS/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Text Programming\nGuide for iOS</a> and<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uimenucontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIMenuController</a>.】</p><h2><b>Labels标签</b></h2><p>A label describes an\nonscreen interface element or provides a short message. Although people can’t\nedit labels, they can sometimes copy the content of labels. Labels can display\nany amount of static text, but are best kept short.</p><p>标签描述了屏幕上的交互元素或者提供短信息。尽管人们不能编辑标签，他们有时能拷贝标签的内容。标签能显示任意数量的静态文本，但是最好还是短一点。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fae6a42c08c96ba1cf8c8d79e1a0c9b9_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-fae6a42c08c96ba1cf8c8d79e1a0c9b9_b.png\"/></figure>Keep labels legible.</strong> Labels can include plain or styled text. If you adjust the style\nof a label or use custom fonts, be sure to not sacrifice legibility. It’s best\nto adopt Dynamic Type so your labels still look good when a user changes text\nsize on their device. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/visual-design/typography/%23dynamic-type-sizes\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Dynamic Type</a>. You\nshould also test your labels with accessibility options enabled, such as bold\ntext. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/interaction/accessibility/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Accessibility</a>.</p><p>To learn about text, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/Strings/introStrings.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">String Programming\nGuide</a>. To learn about creating styling text, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/AttributedStrings/AttributedStrings.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Attributed String\nProgramming Guide</a>. For label implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uilabel\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UILabel</a>.</p><p>标签保持可读。标签可以包含朴素或者风格化的文本。如果您调整标签的样式或者使用自定义字体，确认不要牺牲可读性。最好采用动态文本，这样当用户在设备上改变文本大小时，您的标签还能看上去不错。详见【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/visual-design/typography/%23dynamic-type-sizes\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Dynamic Type</a>】</p><p>您也应该在无障碍选项打开时测试标签，比如粗体文本。详见【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/interaction/accessibility/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Accessibility</a>】</p><p>了解文本，详见【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/Strings/introStrings.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">String Programming\nGuide</a>】；了解创建样式文本，详见【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/AttributedStrings/AttributedStrings.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Attributed String\nProgramming Guide</a>】，关于标签使用，详见【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uilabel\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UILabel</a>.】</p><h2><b>Page Controls页面控件</b></h2><p>A page control shows\nthe position of the current page in a flat list of pages. It appears as a\nseries of small indicator dots, representing the available pages in the order\nthey were opened. A solid dot denotes the current page. Visually, these dots\nare always equidistant, and are clipped if too many appear onscreen. Users can\ntap the leading or trailing edge of a page control to visit the next or\nprevious page, but they can&#39;t tap a specific dot to go to a specific\npage. Navigation always occurs sequentially, usually by swiping the page\nto one side.</p><p>页面控件用简单的页面列表，显示当前页面的位置。它显示为一系列小的指示点，代表以打开顺序排列的可用页面。实心点代表当前页面。视觉上，这些点总是等距离的，并且如果屏幕上出现太多的话就会被剪切掉。用户可以点击页面控件的首端或者尾端来访问下一页或前一页，但是他们不能点到特定的点上去到特定的页面。导航总是按顺序出现，通常通过从一侧扫页面。</p><p><strong>Don’t use a page\ncontrol with hierarchical pages.</strong> A page control doesn’t show how pages are related or indicate\nwhich page corresponds to each dot. This type of control is designed for pages\nthat are peers to one another.</p><p>不要在层级页面之间使用页面控制。页面控制不显示页面之间的联系或者说明每个点对应哪个页面。这种控件是为了平级页面设计的。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-be3fbf1019a5fcf9171516ec84352b64_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-be3fbf1019a5fcf9171516ec84352b64_b.png\"/></figure>Don’t display too many pages.</strong> More than about 10 dots are hard to count at a glance, and more\nthan about 20 open pages are time-consuming to visit in sequence. If your app\nneeds to display more than 20 pages as peers, consider using a different\narrangement—such as a grid—that enables nonsequential navigation.</p><p>不要显示太多页面。超过十个点就很难在一瞥之间数清，按顺序浏览超过20个点就很耗时间。如果您的app需要显示超过20个评级页面，考虑使用一种不同的安排——比如表格——能实现非顺序的导航。</p><p><strong>Center page controls at the bottom\nof the screen.</strong> A page\ncontrol should always be centered and positioned between the bottom of the\ncontent and the bottom of the screen. This keeps it visible, without blocking\ncontent.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipagecontrol\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPageControl</a>.</p><p>在页面底部居中放置页面控件。一个页面控件应该总是居中而且在内容末端和屏幕底部之间。这使得它可见，不会遮挡内容。</p><p>详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipagecontrol\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPageControl</a>】</p><h2><b>Pickers选择器</b></h2><p>A picker includes\none or more scrollable lists of distinct values, each of which has a single\nselected value—appearing in darker text in the center of the view. A picker is\noften displayed at the bottom of the screen or in a popover when the user is\nediting a field or tapping a menu. Pickers can also appear inline, such as\nwhile editing a date in a Calendar event. The height of a picker is roughly the\nheight of five rows of list values. The width of a picker is either the width\nof the screen or its enclosing view, depending on the device and context.</p><p>选择器包含一个或以上不同值的滚动列表，每个有一个单独的选中的值——外观是视图中央的黑色文本。选择器通常显示在屏幕底端，或者当用户编辑一个域或点击菜单时在一个弹出框里。选择器也可以内联显示，比如在Calendar日历事件中编辑日期时。选择器的高度大概是五行列表值的高度。选择器的宽度可以与屏幕同宽或者与它的封闭视图等宽，取决于设备和情境</p><p><strong>Use predictable and\nlogically ordered values.</strong> Many\nvalues in a picker may be hidden when the scrollable lists are stationary. It&#39;s\nbest when people can predict what these values are, such as with a list of\nalphabetized countries, so they can move through the lists quickly.</p><p>使用可预见的、按逻辑排列的值。当滚动列表静止时，选择器中的很多值可能被隐藏。最好人们能预见这些值是什么，比如一列按字母顺序排列的国家，这样他们能快速浏览列表。</p><p><strong>Avoid switching screens\nto show a picker.</strong> A picker\nworks well when displayed in context, below or in close proximity to the field\nbeing edited.</p><p>避免切换屏幕来显示选择器。当被显示在情境中，选择器会发挥作用，低于或者接近正在编辑的字段。</p><p><strong>Use a table instead of\na picker for large value lists.</strong>Long lists can be\ntedious to navigate in a picker. A table has adjustable height and can include\nan index, making scrolling much faster.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipickerview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPickerView</a>.</p><p>对于大值列表，请使用表格替代选择器。通过选择器导航一个长长的列表可能会很乏味。表格可以调整高度，而且能包含索引，让滚动更快速。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipickerview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPickerView</a>】</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c411fdd7b780fe8d5f7c7d23ba9485e7_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"272\" data-rawheight=\"482\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"272\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;272&#39; height=&#39;482&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"272\" data-rawheight=\"482\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"272\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-c411fdd7b780fe8d5f7c7d23ba9485e7_b.png\"/></figure><h3><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2fd52a958e23479aa50f7149577cab9b_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"270\" data-rawheight=\"481\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"270\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;270&#39; height=&#39;481&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"270\" data-rawheight=\"481\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"270\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-2fd52a958e23479aa50f7149577cab9b_b.png\"/></figure>Date Pickers日期选择器</h3><p>A date picker is an\nefficient interface for selecting a specific date, time, or both. It also\nprovides an interface for displaying a countdown timer.</p><p>A date picker has\nfour modes, each of which presents a different set of selectable values.</p><p>日期选择器是一个高效的界面，用于选择特定的日期，时间或者两者。它也提供显示倒数计时器的界面。</p><p>日期选择器有四个模式，每个代表不同的可选择值。</p><p>·       \n<strong>Date.</strong> Displays months, days of the month, and years.</p><p>·       \n<strong>日期。</strong> 显示月份，天数，以及年。</p><p>·       \n<strong>Time.</strong> Displays hours, minutes, and (optionally) an AM/PM designation.</p><p>·       \n<strong>时间。</strong>显示小时，分钟，上午下午（可选）</p><p>·       \n<strong>Date and time.</strong> Displays dates, hours, minutes, and (optionally) an AM/PM\ndesignation.</p><p>·       \n<strong>日期和时间。</strong>显示日期，小时，分钟，上午下午(可选)</p><p>·       \n<strong>Countdown timer.</strong> Displays hours and minutes, up to a maximum of 23 hours and 59\nminutes.</p><p>·       \n<strong>倒数计时器。</strong>显示小时和分钟，最大显示23小时59分钟。</p><p>The exact values\nshown in a date picker and their order depend upon the user’s locale.</p><p>确切的值显示在日期选择器中，并且他们的顺序取决于用户位置。</p><p><strong>Consider providing less\ngranularity when specifying minutes.</strong> By default, a minute list includes 60 values (0 to 59). You can\noptionally increase the minute interval as long as it divides evenly into 60.\nFor example, you might want quarter-hour intervals (0, 15, 30, and 45).</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uidatepicker\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIDatePicker</a>.</p><br/><p>当特定分钟时，考虑提供更少的间隔。默认情况下，一分钟包含60个值（0-59）。您可以选择增加分钟间隔只要他平均分为六十份。例如，您可能想要刻钟的间隔。</p>",
