            "userName": "伍睿", 
            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/55ad36e0c5bc228f82bb1c0030fc3dfd", 
            "upvote": 0, 
            "title": "iOS10人机界面指南：UI-视图（二）", 
            "content": "<h2><b>Popovers弹出框</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-15b18aa1ff32da33171c236bf943e355_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"421\" data-rawheight=\"316\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"421\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-15b18aa1ff32da33171c236bf943e355_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;421&#39; height=&#39;316&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"421\" data-rawheight=\"316\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"421\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-15b18aa1ff32da33171c236bf943e355_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-15b18aa1ff32da33171c236bf943e355_b.png\"/></figure>A popover is a transient view that\nappears above other content onscreen when you tap a control or in an area.\nTypically, a popover includes an arrow pointing to the location from which it\nemerged. Popovers are most appropriate on larger screens and can contain any\nvariety of elements, including navigation bars, toolbars, tab bars, tables,\ncollections, images, maps, and custom views. When a popover is visible,\ninteractions with other views are normally disabled until the popover is\ndismissed. Use a popover to show options or information related to the content\nonscreen. Many iPad apps, for example, show a popover of sharing options when\nyou tap the Share button.</p><p>一个弹出框是一种短暂的视图。当您点击一个控件或者某区域时，弹出框在屏幕上的其他内容之上出现。一般来说，弹出框包括一个指向出现位置的箭头。弹出框在大屏幕上最为合适，并且能包含各种元素，包括导航条，工具条，标签来，列表，集合，图像，地图以及自定义视图。当弹出框可见时，与其他视图的交互通常就不可用了，直到弹出框被关掉。使用弹出框显示与屏幕内容相关的选项和信息。例如，很多iPad app会在您点击分享按钮时显示一个关于分享选项的弹出框。</p><p><strong>Use a Close button for\nconfirmation and guidance only.</strong> A Close button, such as Cancel or Done, is worth including if it\nprovides clarity, such as exiting with or without saving changes. In general, a\npopover should close automatically when its presence is no longer necessary. In\nmost cases, a popover should close when someone taps outside of its bounds or\nselects an item in the popover. If multiple selections can be made, the popover\nshould remain open until someone explicitly dismisses it or taps outside of its\nbounds.</p><p>只在确认和指南类内容使用关闭按钮。一个关闭按钮，例如取消或完成，只有在提供清晰的语义时才可以使用，比如保存修改退出或者不保存修改退出。总的来说，弹出框应该在不再需要时自动关闭。在大多数情况下，弹出框应该在某人点击到界外或者在弹出框里选一个选项之后关闭。如果可以做多种选择，弹出框应该保持开放，直到某人特地关掉它或者点击界外。</p><p><strong>Always save work when\nautomatically closing a popover.</strong> It’s easy to dismiss a popover unintentionally by tapping\nanother part of the screen. Discard work only when someone taps an explicit\nCancel button.</p><p>当自动关闭弹出框时，总是存储工作。通过点击屏幕的其他部分很容易无意识地关掉一个弹出框。只有在某人点击一个明显的取消按钮时才放弃工作。</p><p><strong>Position popovers appropriately\nonscreen.</strong> A\npopover’s arrow should point as directly as possible to the element that\nrevealed it. Because popovers can’t be dragged around the screen, a popover\nshouldn’t cover essential content people may need to see while using the\npopover. A popover also shouldn’t cover the element that was tapped to show the\npopover.</p><p>在屏幕上恰当安排弹出框的位置。弹出框的箭头应该尽可能直接指向弹出的元素。因为弹出框不能在屏幕上拖拽，弹出框不应该覆盖人们使用它期间可能需要看的内容。弹出框也不应该覆盖弹出它的元素。</p><p><strong>Show one popover at a time.</strong> Displaying multiple popovers clutters the interface and causes\nconfusion. Never show a cascade or hierarchy of popovers, in which one emerges\nfrom another. If you need to show a new popover, close the open one first.</p><p>一次只显示一个弹出框。显示多个弹出框会让界面杂乱，引起困惑。永远不要显示一堆弹出框或者好几层弹出框，就是那种一个从另一个中出现的。如果您需要显示一个新的弹出框，先把已经打开的关掉。</p><p><strong>Don’t show another view over a\npopover.</strong> Except\nfor an alert, nothing should be displayed on top of a popover.</p><p>不要在弹出框上再显示一个视图。除非是警报，否则任何东西都不能显示在一个弹出框之上。</p><p><strong>When possible, let users close one\npopover and open another with a single tap.</strong> Avoiding extra taps is especially desirable when several\ndifferent bar buttons each open a popover.</p><p>可能的话，让用户可以用一个简单的点击来关掉一个弹出框再打开另一个。当好几个不同的条状按钮每个都能打开一个弹出框时，避免多余点击就尤为重要了。</p><p><strong>Avoid making a popover too big.</strong> A popover shouldn’t take over the entire screen. Make it only\nbig enough to display its contents and point to the place it came from. Be\naware that the system might adjust the size of a popover to ensure it fits well\nonscreen.</p><p>避免弄出太大的弹出框。弹出框不应该接管整个屏。让它有足够大的地方显示内容并且指向来处就可以了。注意，系统可能调整弹出框的尺寸以确保它适应屏幕。</p><p><strong>Make sure custom popovers look\nlike popovers.</strong> Although\nyou can customize many of the visual aspects of a popover, avoid creating a\ndesign people might not recognize as a popover. Popovers tend to work best when\nthey contain standard controls and views.</p><p>确定自定义的弹出框看起来像弹出框。尽管您可以自定义弹出框的许多视觉元素。避免创造一个人们可能不认为是弹出框的设计。当弹出框包含标准控件和视图时可能运行最好。</p><p><strong>Provide a smooth transition when\nchanging the size of a popover.</strong> Some popovers provide both condensed and expanded views of the\nsame information. If you adjust the size of a popover, animate the change to\navoid giving the impression that a new popover replaced the old one.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipopoverpresentationcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPopoverPresentationController</a>.</p><p>变更弹出框的尺寸时，提供一个顺滑的过渡。有些弹出框同时为同一信息提供缩略图和扩展视图。如果您要调整弹出框的尺寸，请给这个改变加上动画，以免给人留下这种印象——新的弹出框取代了旧的。</p><p>详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipopoverpresentationcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPopoverPresentationController</a>.】</p><h2><b>Scroll Views滚动视图</b></h2><p>A scroll view allows\nusers to browse content, such as text in a document or a collection of images,\nthat’s larger than the visible area. As people swipe, flick, drag, tap, and\npinch, a scroll view follows the gesture, revealing or zooming content in a way\nthat feels natural. A scroll view itself has no appearance, but does display\ntransient scrolling indicators as people interact with it. A scroll view can also\nbe configured to operate in paging mode, where scrolling reveals an entirely\nnew page of content rather than moving around the current page.</p><p>滚动视图让用户能浏览比可视区域大的内容，比如文档中的文本或者图片集合。当人们横扫，滑动，拖拽，点击，捏合，滚动视图会随着手势用自然地感觉揭开或者缩放内容。滚动视图本身没有外观，但是在人们与之交互时会显示临时的滚动条。滚动视图也可以设置为在页面模式操作。页面模式中，滚动可以揭开一整页新内容，而不是在当前页面中到处晃。</p><p><strong>Support zoom behavior\nappropriately.</strong> If it\nmakes sense in your app, let people pinch or double-tap to zoom in and out.\nWhen you enable zoom, set maximum and minimum scale values that make sense. For\nexample, zooming in on text until a single character fills the screen probably\ndoesn’t make sense in most apps.</p><p>适时支持缩放行为。如果在app中有意义，请让人们可以捏合或者双击来缩放。当您开启缩放功能，请设置有意义的最大或者最小缩放范围。例如，在大多数app里，将文本放大至单个字母占满屏幕没什么意义。</p><p><strong>Consider showing a page\ncontrol element when a scroll view is in paging mode.</strong> A page control shows how many pages, screens, or other chunks of\ncontent are available and indicates which one is currently visible. If you show\na page control with a scroll view, disable the scrolling indicator on the same\naxis to avoid confusion. For additional guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/page-controls/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Page Controls</a>.</p><p>考虑当滚动视图在页面模式时显示一个页面控制元素。页面控制显示内容有多少页，多少屏，或者其他的计量单位，并且显示哪一个是当前可见的。如果您在滚动视图里显示一个页面控件，请将同轴的滚动条关掉以免困惑。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/page-controls/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Page Controls</a>.】</p><p><strong>Don’t place a scroll\nview inside of another scroll view.</strong>Doing so creates an\nunpredictable interface that’s difficult to control.</p><p>不要在滚动视图内再放一个滚动视图。这么做会创建一个难以控制的不可预料的界面</p><p><strong>In general, display one scroll\nview at a time.</strong> People\noften make large swipe gestures when scrolling, and it can be hard to avoid\ninteracting with a neighboring scroll view on the same screen. If you need to\nput two scroll views on one screen, consider allowing them to scroll in\ndifferent directions so one gesture is less likely to affect both views. For\nexample, when an iPhone is in portrait orientation, the Stocks app shows stock\nquotes that scroll vertically above company-specific information that scrolls\nhorizontally.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiscrollview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIScrollView</a>.</p><p>总的来说，同一时间只显示一个滚动视图。人们经常在滚动时做大幅度的横扫动作，并且在同一屏幕上很难避免与相邻的滚动视图交互。如果您需要将两个滚动视图放在同一屏上，考虑让他们在不同方向上滚动，这样一个手势就可能不太会影响到两个视图。比如，当一个iPhone在纵向模式时，股票app显示横向滚动的企业信息，在它上面显示纵向滚动的股票报价。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiscrollview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIScrollView</a>.】</p><h2><b>Split Views拆分视图</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5fab7e9e547d3ac329cc2d26eee2b57f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"509\" data-rawheight=\"382\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"509\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5fab7e9e547d3ac329cc2d26eee2b57f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;509&#39; height=&#39;382&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"509\" data-rawheight=\"382\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"509\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5fab7e9e547d3ac329cc2d26eee2b57f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-5fab7e9e547d3ac329cc2d26eee2b57f_b.png\"/></figure>A split view manages the presentation\nof two side-by-side panes of content, with persistent content in the primary\npane and related information in the secondary pane. Each pane can contain any\nvariety of elements, including navigation bars, toolbars, tab bars, tables,\ncollections, images, maps, and custom views. Split views are often used with\nfilterable content; a list of filter categories appears in the primary pane,\nand the filtered results for the selected category are shown in the secondary\npane. If your app requires it, the primary pane can overlay the secondary pane\nand can be hidden offscreen when not in use. This is particularly useful when\nthe device is in portrait orientation, as it allows more room for viewing\ncontent in the secondary pane.</p><p>拆分视图管理两个并排的内容窗口，基本窗口显示持续的内容，第二窗口显示相关信息。每个窗口包含任何种类的元素，包括导航条，工具条，标签栏，表格，集合，图像，地图，以及自定义视图。拆分视图通常用于可过滤的内容：一列可过滤的分类出现在基础窗口，挑选种类的过滤结果显示在第二窗口。如果您的app需要它。基础窗口可以叠在第二窗口上，不用的时候还可以藏在屏幕之外。当设备处于纵向模式时尤其有用，因为它能给在第二窗口查看内容更多空间。</p><p><strong>Choose a split-view layout that\nworks well with your content.</strong> By\ndefault, a split view devotes a third of the screen to the primary pane and\ntwo-thirds to the secondary pane. The screen can also be split into halves.\nChoose an appropriate split based on your content, and make sure the panes\ndon’t look unbalanced. Avoid creating a secondary pane that’s narrower than the\nprimary pane.</p><p>选择一个与内容相适配的拆分视图布局。默认情况下，拆分视图中，三分之一留给基础窗口，三分之二留给第二窗口。也可以把屏幕分成一半一半。根据内容选择合适的拆分，并且确认这些窗口不会看起来失衡。避免创建比基础窗口还窄的第二窗口。</p><p><strong>Persistently highlight\nthe active selection in the primary pane.</strong> Although\nthe secondary pane’s content can change, it should always correspond to a clearly\nidentifiable selection in the primary pane. This helps people\nunderstand the relationship between the panes.</p><p>一直突出基础窗口里的活动选择。尽管第二窗口的内容可以改变，它应该一直回应基础窗口中清晰可辨的选择。这能帮助人们理解窗口之间的关系。</p><p><strong>In general, restrict navigation to\none side of a split view.</strong> Placing\nnavigation in both panes of a split view makes it hard for people to stay\noriented and discern the relationship between the two panes.</p><p>总的来说，只在拆分视图的一侧使用导航。将导航放在拆分视图的两边会让人们难以找到方向，并且难以辨别两个窗口的关系。</p><p><strong>Provide multiple ways to access a\nhidden primary pane.</strong> On\nlayouts where the primary pane may be offscreen, be sure to provide a\nbutton—typically in a navigation bar—to reveal the pane. Unless your app uses\nthe swipe gesture to perform other functions, let people swipe from the side of\nthe screen to access the primary pane too.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uisplitviewcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UISplitViewController</a>.</p><p>提供多种到达隐藏的基础窗口的方式。在基础窗口可能在屏幕之外的布局中，确认提供一个按钮——通常在导航条里——用来揭开窗口。除非您的app使用横扫手势来实行其他功能，让人们从屏幕一端横扫也能获取基础窗口。</p><h2><b>Tables表格</b></h2><p>A table presents data as a scrolling,\nsingle-column list of rows that can be divided into sections or groups. Use a\ntable to display large or small amounts of information cleanly and efficiently\nin the form of a list. Generally speaking, tables are ideal for text-based\ncontent, and often appear as a means of navigation on one side of a split view,\nwith related content shown on the opposite side. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/split-views/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Split Views</a>.</p><p>表格将数据呈现为一个滚动的单栏多列列表，行可以被分成多个区域或组合。用表格来简洁高效地通过列表方式显示大量或少量信息。总的来说，表格对于文本内容很理想，而且经常作为导航方式出现在拆分视图的一侧，另一边显示相关内容。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/split-views/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Split Views</a>.】</p><p>iOS implements two styles of table,\nplain and grouped.</p><p>iOS用两种风格的表格，纯表格和分组表格。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8bce4a02229620afb0aa85976f47763a_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"259\" data-rawheight=\"461\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"259\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;259&#39; height=&#39;461&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"259\" data-rawheight=\"461\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"259\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-8bce4a02229620afb0aa85976f47763a_b.png\"/></figure>Plain.</strong> Rows can be separated into labeled sections, and an optional\nindex can appear vertically along the right edge of the table. A header can\nappear before the first item in a section, and a footer can appear after the\nlast item.</p><p>纯表格。行可以被分为多个标签区域，并且一个可选索引可能垂直出现在表格右边缘。一个区域的第一个项目之前可能出现页眉，最后一个项目之后可能出现一个页脚。</p><br/><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-34755a6961f0fb3bc0764a51bc87f6e4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"257\" data-rawheight=\"228\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"257\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;257&#39; height=&#39;228&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"257\" data-rawheight=\"228\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"257\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-34755a6961f0fb3bc0764a51bc87f6e4_b.png\"/></figure><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f0baf9ca2a5ba89957996eb263af4c48_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-f0baf9ca2a5ba89957996eb263af4c48_b.png\"/></figure>Grouped.</strong> Rows are displayed in groups, which can be preceded by a header\nand followed by a footer. This style of table always contains at least one\ngroup and each group always contains at least one row. A grouped table doesn’t\ninclude an index.</p><p>分组表格。行被成组显示，可能前面有页眉，后面有页脚。这种表格总是包含至少一个分组并且每个分组一直包含至少一行。分组表格不包括索引。</p><p><strong>Think about table width.</strong> Thin tables can cause truncation and wrapping, making them hard\nto read and scan quickly at a distance. Wide tables can also be difficult to\nread and scan, and can take away space from content.</p><p>考虑表格宽度。太窄的表格可能会引起内容被砍掉或者被压缩，让他们难以阅读，有点距离时难以快速扫视。宽表格也可能难读难扫，并且可能占据内容空间。</p><p><strong>Begin showing table content\nquickly.</strong> Don’t\nwait for extensive table content to load before showing something. Fill\nonscreen rows with textual data immediately and show more complex data—such as\nimages—as it becomes available. This technique gives people useful information\nright away and increases the perceived responsiveness of your app. In some\ncases, showing stale, older data may make sense until fresh, new data arrives.</p><p>快速开始显示表格内容。不要在显示一些东西时等待广泛表内容加载。立刻用文本数据填充屏幕上的行并且显示更复杂的数据——比如图像——当它可获取时。这个技巧能立刻给人有用的信息并且增加app的感知响应。在某些情况下，显示陈旧的老数据也可能有意义，直到新鲜的新数据到来。</p><p><strong>Communicate progress as content\nloads.</strong> If a\ntable’s data takes time to load, show a progress bar or spinning activity\nindicator to reassure people that your app is still alive.</p><p>内容加载时传达进程。如果表格数据需要时间加载，显示进度条或者旋转活动指示符来向人们再保证您的app还在运行。</p><p><strong>Keep content fresh.</strong> Consider updating your table’s content regularly to reflect\nnewer data. Just don’t change the scrolling position. Instead, add the content\nto the beginning or end of the table, and let people scroll to it when they’re\nready. Some apps display an indicator when new data has been added, and provide\na control for jumping right to it. It’s also a good idea to include a refresh\ncontrol, so people can manually perform an update at any time. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/refresh-content-controls/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Refresh Content\nControls</a>.</p><p>保持内容新鲜，考虑有规律地更新表格内容来反应新数据。不要只是改变滚动位置。相反的，在表格开始或者结尾添加内容，并且在准备好时让人们滚动它。有些app在新数据添加时显示一个指示符，并且提供一个用于直接到达它的控件。包含一个刷新控件也是好主意，这样人们就可以在任何时候手动更新。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/refresh-content-controls/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Refresh Content\nControls</a>.】</p><p><strong>Avoid combining an index with\ntable rows containing right-aligned elements.</strong> An index is controlled by performing large swiping gestures. If\nother interactive elements reside nearby, such as disclosure indicators, it may\nbe difficult to discern the user’s intent when a gesture occurs and the wrong\nelement may be activated.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableView</a>.</p><p>避免将一个索引和包含右对齐元素的表格行放在一起。做大幅度的滑动动作可以控制索引。如果其他交互元素在附近，例如展开指示器，当手势出现时，可能很难辨别用户意图，并且可能激活错误的元素。</p><h3>Table Rows表格行</h3><p>You use standard table cell styles to\ndefine how content appears in table rows.</p><p>使用标准表格单元格风格来定义内容如何出现在表格行中。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2a66b6c8421ea8706938931223a85f36_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"240\" data-rawheight=\"213\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"240\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;240&#39; height=&#39;213&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"240\" data-rawheight=\"213\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"240\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-2a66b6c8421ea8706938931223a85f36_b.png\"/></figure>Default.</strong> An optional image on the left side of the row, followed by a\nleft-aligned title. It’s a good option for displaying items that don’t require\nsupplementary information. For implementation details, see the<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellstyle/uitableviewcellstyledefault\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellStyleDefault</a> constant of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.</p><p>默认。行左侧是一个可选图片，截止是一个左对齐的标题。对于显示不需要补充的信息项目来说，这是个很好的选择。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellstyle/uitableviewcellstyledefault\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellStyleDefault</a> constant of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.】</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-23c860fddd093f3781f6881ed29309d4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-23c860fddd093f3781f6881ed29309d4_b.png\"/></figure>Subtitle.</strong> A left-aligned title on one line and a left-aligned subtitle on\nthe next. This style works well in a table where rows are visually similar. The\nadditional subtitle helps distinguish rows from one another. For implementation\ndetails, see the<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellstyle/uitableviewcellstylesubtitle\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellStyleSubtitle</a> constant of<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.</p><p>副标题。一行是左对齐的标题，另一行是左对齐的副标题。这种方式在每行看起来差不多的时候很好用。附加的副标题帮助区分每一行。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellstyle/uitableviewcellstylesubtitle\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellStyleSubtitle</a> constant of<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.】</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-21f5225f6659d45f076a58c874bcab13_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-21f5225f6659d45f076a58c874bcab13_b.png\"/></figure>Value\n1.</strong> A\nleft-aligned title with a right-aligned subtitle in a lighter font on the same\nline. For implementation details, see the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellstyle/uitableviewcellstylevalue1\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellStyleValue1</a> constant of<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.</p><p>Value1.左对齐的标题和同一行浅色字的右对齐副标题。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellstyle/uitableviewcellstylevalue1\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellStyleValue1</a> constant of<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.】</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f055cfe7dcc70dfe833f2031982d635e_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f055cfe7dcc70dfe833f2031982d635e_b.png\"/></figure>Value\n2.</strong> A\nright-aligned title, followed by a left-aligned subtitle in a lighter font on\nthe same line. For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellstyle/uitableviewcellstylevalue2\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellStyleValue2</a>constant\nof <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.</p><p>Value2.一个右对齐的标题，同一行浅色字左对齐的副标题。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcellstyle/uitableviewcellstylevalue2\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCellStyleValue2</a>constant\nof <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.】</p><p>All standard table cell styles also\nallow graphical elements, such as a checkmark or disclosure indicator. Of\ncourse, adding these elements decreases the space available for titles and\nsubtitles.</p><p>所有标准表格单元格风格也允许图形元素，例如对号或者展开指示符。当然，添加这些元素会减少标题和副标题的可用面积。</p><p><strong>Keep text succinct to avoid\nclipping.</strong> Truncated\nwords and phrases are hard to scan and decipher. Text truncation is automatic\nin all table cell styles, but it can present more or less of a problem\ndepending on which cell style you use and where truncation occurs.</p><p>让文本保持简洁，避免缩减文字。缩减的词语和短语难以扫描和解密。文本缩减在所有表格风格里都是自动的，但是它可能多少有点问题，这取决于您使用哪种表格单元格风格，以及缩减出现在哪。</p><p><strong>Consider using a custom title for\na Delete button.</strong> If a row\nsupports deletion and it helps provide clarity, replace the system-provided\nDelete title with a custom title.</p><p>考虑为删除按钮使用自定义标题。如果行支持删除并且帮助提供清晰度，？？？可以用自定义的标题替代系统提供的删除标题。</p><p><strong>Provide feedback when a selection\nis made.</strong> People\nexpect a row to highlight briefly when its content is tapped. Then, people\nexpect a new view to appear or something to change, such as a checkmark\nappearing, that indicates a selection has been made.</p><p>当做出选择时要提供反馈。人们期望当内容被点击时一行会稍微高亮。然后，人们期望一个新的视图出现或者什么东西发生改变，比如一个对号出现，带编者已经做出选择。</p><p><strong>Design a custom table cell style\nfor nonstandard table rows.</strong> Standard\nstyles are great for use in a variety of common scenarios, but some content or\nyour overall app design may call for a heavily customized table appearance. To\nlearn how to create your own cells, see<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/TableView_iPhone/TableViewCells/TableViewCells.html%23//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40007451-CH7-SW18\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Customizing\nCells</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/TableView_iPhone/AboutTableViewsiPhone/AboutTableViewsiPhone.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Table\nView Programming Guide for iOS</a>.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.</p><p>为非标准表格行设计一个自定义表格单元格风格。标准风格对于各种常见场景很有用，但是有些内容或者您的全局app设计可能需要一个高度自定义的表格外观，为了学习如何创建您自己的单元格，查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/TableView_iPhone/TableViewCells/TableViewCells.html%23//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40007451-CH7-SW18\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Customizing Cells</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/TableView_iPhone/AboutTableViewsiPhone/AboutTableViewsiPhone.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Table View\nProgramming Guide for iOS</a>.】</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitableviewcell\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITableViewCell</a>.】</p><h2>Text Views文本视图</h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b1dd2f0eac82895424a84831c515157c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;555&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-b1dd2f0eac82895424a84831c515157c_b.png\"/></figure>A text view displays multiline, styled text content. Text views\ncan be any height and enable scrolling when the content extends outside of the\nview. By default, content within a text view is left-aligned and uses the\nsystem font in black. If a text view is editable, a keyboard appears when you\ntap inside the view.</p><p>文本视图显示多行，有样式的文本内容。文本视图可能是任何高度并且在内容扩展到视图之外时可以滚动。默认情况下，文本视图内的内容时左对齐的，并且使用黑色系统字体。如果文本视图是可编辑的，当您在试图内点击时会出现键盘。</p><p><strong>Keep text legible.</strong> Although you can use multiple fonts, colors, and alignments in\ncreative ways, it’s essential to maintain the readability of your content. It’s\na good idea to adopt Dynamic Type so your text still looks good if people\nchange text size on their device. You should also test your content with\naccessibility options enabled, such as bold text.</p><p>保持文本可读性。尽管您可以用各种文字，颜色，用富有创意的方式对齐，保持内容的可读性还是最重要的。采用动态字体是个好主意，这样如果人们改变设备上的文本尺寸时，您的文本还是看起来很是很棒。您也应该</p><p><strong>Show the appropriate\nkeyboard type.</strong> iOS\nprovides several different keyboard types, each designed to facilitate a\ndifferent type of input. To streamline data entry, the keyboard displayed\nduring the editing of a text view should be appropriate for the type of content\nin the field. For a complete list of available keyboard types, see the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uikeyboardtype\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIKeyboardType</a> constant of<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitextinputtraits\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITextInputTraits</a>.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitextview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITextView</a>.</p><p>显示恰当的键盘类型。iOS提供几种不同的键盘类型，每个都为了加强不同类型的输入而设计。为了精简数据输入，在文本编辑视图中显示的键盘对于文本域中的内容来说应该是合适的。详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uikeyboardtype\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIKeyboardType</a> constant of<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitextinputtraits\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UITextInputTraits</a>.】</p><h2><b>Web Views网页视图</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-72ddfc569d98ae74c67b289a592ef547_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"254\" data-rawheight=\"451\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"254\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;254&#39; height=&#39;451&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"254\" data-rawheight=\"451\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"254\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-72ddfc569d98ae74c67b289a592ef547_b.png\"/></figure>A web view loads and\ndisplays rich web content, such as embedded HTML and websites, directly within\nyour app. Mail uses a web view, for example, to show HTML content in messages.</p><p>网页视图能在app内直接加载并显示丰富的网页内容，例如嵌入的HTML和网址。例如，邮件Mail使用网页视图来显示信息中的HTML内容。</p><p><strong>Enable forward and back\nnavigation when appropriate.</strong> Web views\nsupport forward and back navigation, but this behavior is disabled by default.\nIf people will use your web view to visit multiple pages, enable forward and\nback navigation, and provide corresponding controls to initiate these features.</p><p>适当时允许前进或后退。网页视图支持前进或后退，但是默认关闭这个行为。如果人们可能在网页视图中查看多个页面，那就允许前进或者，并且提供相应启动这些特性的控件。</p><p><strong>Avoid using a web view\nto build a web browser.</strong> Using a\nweb view to let people briefly access a website without leaving the context of\nyour app is fine, but Safari is the primary way people browse the web on iOS.\nAttempting to replicate the functionality of Safari in your app is unnecessary\nand discouraged.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/webkit/wkwebview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">WKWebView</a>.</p><p>避免使用网页视图来建立浏览器。使用网页视图来让人们不离开app的情景来简要获取是好的，但是Safari才是人们在iOS上浏览网页的基础方式。试图在app中复制Safari功能的行为是不必要的、不被鼓励的。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/webkit/wkwebview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">WKWebView</a>.】</p>",

            "upvote": 0, 
            "title": "iOS 10 人机界面指南：UI-视图（一）", 
            "content": "<h2><b>Action Sheets动作菜单</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-dbf73513f3c134fed8a7abbe6095a272_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;555&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-dbf73513f3c134fed8a7abbe6095a272_b.png\"/></figure>An action sheet is a specific style of alert that appears in\nresponse to a control or action, and presents a set of two or more choices\nrelated to the current context. Use an action sheet to let people initiate\ntasks, or to request confirmation before performing a potentially destructive\noperation. On smaller screens, an action sheet slides up from the bottom of the\nscreen. On larger screens, an action sheet appears all at once as a popover.</p><p>动作菜单是一种特殊的警报，用于回应一个控件或动作，并且呈现与当前情景相关的两个或更多选项。使用动作菜单以让人们启动任务，或者在实行一个可能具有破坏性的操作之前请求确认。在小屏幕上，动作菜单从屏幕底部滑上来。在大屏幕上，动作菜单作为poppver立刻出现。</p><p><strong>Provide a Cancel button\nif it adds clarity.</strong> A Cancel\nbutton instills confidence when the user is abandoning a task. Cancel buttons\nshould always be included in action sheets at the bottom of the screen.</p><p>如果能增加明晰度，提供一个取消按钮。当用户正在放弃任务时，取消按钮灌输信心。？？？取消按钮应该一直包含在屏幕底端的动作列表中。</p><p><strong>Make destructive\nchoices prominent.</strong> Use red\nfor buttons that perform destructive or dangerous actions, and display these\nbuttons at the top of an action sheet.</p><p>让具有毁灭性的选项更显眼。给实行毁灭性的或者危险性动作的按钮使用红色，并且在动作列表的顶端显示。</p><p><strong>Avoid enabling\nscrolling in an action sheet.</strong> If an\naction sheet has too many options, people must scroll to see all of the\nchoices. Scrolling requires extra time to make a choice and is hard to do\nwithout inadvertently tapping a button.</p><p>在动作列表中避免使用滚动。如果动作列表有太多选项，人们必须滚动查看所有选择。滚动要都更多时间来做选择，并且没有不经意间点击按钮很难做？？？？？</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see the<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertcontrollerstyle/uialertcontrollerstyleactionsheet\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertControllerStyleActionSheet</a> constant in<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertController</a>.</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertcontrollerstyle/uialertcontrollerstyleactionsheet\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertControllerStyleActionSheet</a> constant in<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertController</a>】</p><h2><b>Activity Views活动视图</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-225557284fa370dff353349d0fe2efee_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;555&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-225557284fa370dff353349d0fe2efee_b.png\"/></figure>An activity is a\ntask, such as Copy, Favorite, or Find, that’s useful in the current context.\nOnce initiated, an activity can perform a task immediately, or ask for more\ninformation before proceeding. Activities are managed by an activity view,\nwhich appears as a sheet or popover, depending on the device and orientation.\nUse activities to give people access to custom services or tasks your app can\nperform.</p><p>一个活动就是一个任务，例如拷贝，收藏，或者寻找，在当前情境下有用。一旦启动，一个活动会立刻实行一个任务，或者在继续前进之前要求更多信息。活动是通过活动视图管理的，作为表单或者popover出现，根据设备和方向改变。使用活动以使人们获得自定义服务或者app可以实行的任务。</p><p>The system provides\na number of built-in activities, including Print, Twitter, Message, and\nAirplay. These tasks always appear first in activity views and can’t be\nreordered. You don’t need to create custom activities that perform these\nbuilt-in tasks. Activity views also display share and action extensions from\nother apps. See<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/sharing-and-actions\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Sharing and Actions</a>.</p><p>系统提供一系列内置活动，包括打印，分享到Twitter，用Message分享，通过Airplay播放。这些任务一直首先出现在活动视图并且不能重排顺序。您不必为内置任务创建自定义活动。活动视图也展示分享和其他app的扩展动作。</p><p><strong>Design simple template\nimages to represent your custom activities.</strong> A template image uses a mask to create an icon. Use black and\nwhite with appropriate transparency and antialiasing, and don’t include a drop\nshadow. Template images should be centered in an area measuring about 70px by\n70px.</p><p>设计简单的模板图片来展示自定义活动。模板图片使用遮罩来创建图标。使用恰当透明度和抗锯齿的黑白，不要包括投影。模板图片应该在大约70pxX70px的区域中心。</p><p><strong>Craft activity titles\nthat succinctly describe your tasks.</strong>Titles appear below\nthe icons in an activity view. Short titles work best. When a title is too\nlong, iOS first shrinks the text and then—if the title is still too\nlong—truncates it. In general, avoid including your company or product name in\na title.</p><p>仔细斟酌活动标题，以简洁地描述任务。在活动视图中标题出现在图表下面。短标题最好用了。当标题太长时，iOS首先会收缩文本，然后，如果标题还是太长，截短它。总的来说，在标题中避免包含公司或者产品命长</p><p><strong>Make sure activities are\nappropriate for the current context.</strong> Although system-provided tasks can’t be reordered in an\nactivity, they can be excluded if they aren’t applicable to your app. For\nexample, to prevent people from printing images, you can exclude the Print\nactivity. You can also identify which custom tasks to show at any given time.</p><p>确认活动对于当前情景是合适的。尽管系统提供的任务不能在活动中重新排序，如果他们对于app不适用，可以不用他们。例如，为了避免人们打印图片，您可以剔除打印活动。您也可以在任何给定的时间识别那些自定义任务出现。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0cee3ddef04bef6c999355aa3c0d13bd_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-0cee3ddef04bef6c999355aa3c0d13bd_b.png\"/></figure>Use the Action button\nto display an activity view.</strong>People are accustomed to accessing\nsystem-provided activities when they tap the Action button. Avoid confusing\npeople by providing an alternative way to do the same thing.</p><p>使用动作按钮来显示一个活动视图。人们习惯于在点击活动按钮时获取系统提供的活动。避免通过给做同一件事不同的方法使人困惑。</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiactivityviewcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIActivityViewContoller</a>and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiactivity\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIActivity</a>.</p><p>详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiactivityviewcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIActivityViewContoller</a>and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiactivity\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIActivity</a>.】</p><h2><b>Alerts警报</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d8b5bab822c4f54d95d6bcc97486d0c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"556\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;556&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"556\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-4d8b5bab822c4f54d95d6bcc97486d0c_b.png\"/></figure>Alerts convey\nimportant information related to the state of your app or the device, and often\nrequest feedback. An alert consists of a title, an optional message, one or\nmore buttons, and optional text fields for gathering input. Aside from these\nconfigurable elements, the visual appearance of an alert is static and can’t be\ncustomized.</p><p>警报传递与app或者设备状态相关的重要信息。一个警报由标题，选择信息，一个或以上按钮，以及可选的用于输入的文本域组成。除了这些配置元素，警报的外观是稳定的且不可自定义的。</p><p><strong>Minimize\nalerts.</strong> Alerts\ndisrupt the user experience and should only be used in important situations\nlike confirming purchases and destructive actions (such as deletions), or\nnotifying people about problems. The infrequency of alerts helps ensure that\npeople take them seriously. Ensure that each alert offers critical information\nand useful choices.</p><p>尽量少用警报。警报打扰用户体验而且应该只被用于重要的场景，比如确认购买或者破坏性行为（比如删除），或者通知人们一些问题。警报的不常见性确保人们把他们当回事。确保每个警报提供关键信息和有用的选择。</p><p><strong>Test the appearance of\nalerts in both orientations.</strong> An alert\nmay appear differently in landscape mode and portrait mode. Optimize alert text\nso it reads well in any orientation without scrolling.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertController</a>.</p><p>在两个方向测试警报的外观。在横向模式和纵向模式中警报可能看起来不一样。优化警报文本，这样它就能在任意方向阅读量好，不用滚动。</p><h3>Alert Titles and Messages警报标题和信息</h3><p><strong>Write short, descriptive,\nmultiword alert titles.</strong> The less\ntext people have to read onscreen, the better. Try to craft a title that avoids\nadding extra text as a message. Because single-word titles rarely provide\nuseful information, consider asking a question or using short sentences.\nWhenever possible, keep titles to a single line. Use sentence-style\ncapitalization and appropriate punctuation for complete sentences. Don’t use\nending punctuation for sentence fragments.</p><p>写短的，描述性的，多个字的警报标题。人们在屏幕上需要读的文本越少越好。尽量斟酌标题，作为信息避免添加多余文本。因为一个词的标题很少会提供有用信息，考虑用疑问句或者使用短句子。任何可能的时候，保持标题在一行里。为了完整的句子，请使用句首大写和恰当的标点。不要为句子中断使用句号。</p><p><strong>If you must provide a message,\nwrite short, complete sentences.</strong> Try to keep messages short enough to fit on one or two lines to\nprevent scrolling. Use sentence-style capitalization and appropriate\npunctuation.</p><p>如果您必须提供信息，请写短的完整句子。尽量保持信息长度正好在一两行，避免滚动。请用句首大写和恰当的标点。</p><p><strong>Avoid sounding accusatory,\njudgmental, or insulting.</strong> People\nknow that alerts notify them about problems and dangerous situations. As long\nas you use a friendly tone, it’s better to be negative and direct than positive\nand oblique. Avoid pronouns such as you, your, me, and my, which are sometimes\ninterpreted as insulting or patronizing.</p><p>避免看上去有非难、判断或者侮辱意味。人们知道警报会就问题和危险情况通知他们。只要您使用友好的语气，直接否定比隐晦肯定要更好。避免使用您，您们的，我，我的之类的代词，有时候会被理解为侮辱或者傲慢。</p><p><strong>Avoid explaining the alert\nbuttons.</strong> If your\nalert text and button titles are clear, there should be no need to explain what\nthe buttons do. In rare cases where you must provide guidance, use the word <em>tap</em>,\npreserve capitalization when referencing buttons, and don’t enclose button\ntitles in quotes.</p><p>避免解释警报按钮。如果您的警报文本和按钮标题很清楚，那就不需要解释按钮的作用是什么了。在极少您必须提供指南的情况下，使用“tap”，当指按钮时保留字母大写，并且不要将标题放在引号中。</p><h3>Alert Buttons警报按钮</h3><p><strong>Generally, use two-button alerts.</strong> Two-button alerts provide an easy choice between two\nalternatives. Single-button alerts inform, but give no control over the\nsituation. Alerts with three or more buttons create complexity and can require\nscrolling, which is a bad user experience. If you find that you need more than\ntwo choices, consider using an action sheet instead. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/action-sheets/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Action Sheets</a>.</p><p>总的来说，使用两个按钮的警报样式。两个按钮的警报在两个选项中提供简单的选择。单个按钮的警报只是通知消息，但是对情况没有控制权。三个或以上按钮的警报就复杂了，并且可能需要滚动屏幕，体验就不好了。如果您发现您需要两个以上的选择，考虑使用动作列表代替。详情见【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/action-sheets/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Action Sheets</a>.】</p><p><strong>Give alert buttons succinct,\nlogical titles.</strong> The best\nbutton titles consist of one or two words that describe the result of selecting\nthe button. As with all button titles, use title-style capitalization and no\nending punctuation. To the extent possible, use verbs and verb phrases that\nrelate directly to the alert title and message—for example, View All, Reply, or\nIgnore. Use OK for simple acceptance. Avoid using Yes or No.</p><p>请赋予警报按钮简洁有逻辑的标题。最好的按钮标题由一两个描述选择该按钮结果的词组成。与所有按钮标题一样，使用首字母大写，不用句号。在可能的范围内，使用直接与警报标题和信息相关的动词或动词短语——例如，查看所有，回复或者忽略。用OK表示简单的接受。避免使用Yes or No</p><p><strong>Place buttons where people expect\nthem.</strong> In\ngeneral, buttons people are most likely to tap should be on the right. Cancel\nbuttons should always be on the left.</p><p>请把按钮放在人们期望的地方。总的来说，人们最可能点击的按钮应该在右边。取消按钮应该一直在左边。</p><p><strong>Label cancellation buttons\nappropriately.</strong> A button\nthat cancels an alert’s action should always be labeled Cancel.</p><p>恰当的标记取消按钮。取消警报动作的按钮应该一直标记为“Cancel”</p><p><strong>Identify destructive buttons.</strong> If an alert button results in a destructive action, such as\ndeleting content, set the button’s style to Destructive so that it gets\nappropriate formatting by the system. For implementation details, see the<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertactionstyle/uialertactionstyledestructive\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertActionStyleDestructive</a> constant of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertaction\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertAction</a>.\nAdditionally, provide a Cancel button so people can safely opt out of the\ndestructive action. Make the Cancel button bold by marking it as the default\nbutton.</p><p>识别毁灭性的的按钮。如果一个警报按钮会导致毁灭性的动作。比如删除内容，将按钮样式设置为毁灭性的的，这样系统就能准确安排。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertactionstyle/uialertactionstyledestructive\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertActionStyleDestructive</a> constant of <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uialertaction\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIAlertAction</a>】。另外，请提供一个取消按钮，这样人们可以安全地选择退出毁灭性的动作。通过标记为默认按钮让取消按钮更醒目。</p><p><strong>Allow the Home button to cancel\nalerts.</strong> Pressing\nHome while an alert is visible exits the app. It should also produce the same\neffect as clicking the cancellation button—that is, the alert is dismissed\nwithout performing any action. If your alert doesn’t have a cancellation\nbutton, consider implementing a cancel action in your code that runs when the\nHome button is pressed.</p><p>允许Home键取消警报。当警报可见时，按Home键会离开app。它应该和点取消按钮产生同一作用——那就是，不执行任何警报操作。如果您的警报没有取消按钮，考虑使用在代码中使用在按Home键之后就运行的取消动作。</p><h2><b>Collections集合</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0368c08f75cbfc7d25c857f956cfc6e8_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"556\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;556&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"556\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-0368c08f75cbfc7d25c857f956cfc6e8_b.png\"/></figure>A collection manages\nan ordered set of content, such as a set of photos, and presents it in a\ncustomizable and highly visual layout. Because a collection doesn’t enforce a\nstrictly linear format, it’s particularly well-suited to displaying items that\nvary in size. Generally speaking, collections are ideal for showing off\nimage-based content. Backgrounds and other decorative views can optionally be\nimplemented to visually distinguish subsets of items.</p><p>一个集合管理着一系列内容，比如一系列照片，并且用自定义的极具视觉的布局呈现。因为集合不执行严格的线性格式，它非常适于显示不同尺寸的项目。总的来说，集合对于展示图片类的内容是非常理想的。背景和其他装饰性的视图可以选择性使用，用于视觉上区分项目的分类。</p><p>Collections support\nboth interactivity and animation. By default, you can tap to select, touch and\nhold to edit, and swipe to scroll. If your app requires it, more gestures can\nbe added for performing custom actions. Within a collection, animations can be\nenabled whenever items are inserted, deleted, or reordered, and custom\nanimations are also supported.</p><p>集合支持交互和动画。默认操作是，点击选择，长按编辑，滑动以滚动。如果app需要，可以添加更多的手势以实现个性化动作。在集合内，插入、删除、重排顺序都可以用动画，也支持自定义动画。</p><p><strong>Avoid\ncreating radical new designs when a standard row or grid layout is sufficient.</strong> A collection should enhance the user experience, not become the\ncenter of attention. Make it easy to select an item. If it’s hard to tap an\nitem in your collection, people will get frustrated and lose interest before\nreaching the content they want. Use adequate padding around content to keep the\nlayout clean and prevent overlapping of content.</p><p>当标准行或网格布局够用时，避免创建激进的新设计。集合应该增强用户体验，而不是成为注意力中心。让选择项目更容易。如果在您的集合里点击项目很难，人们会感觉沮丧并且在获得他们想要的内容之前就失去兴趣。在内容之间留充足的空，让布局看起来干净，并且避免内容重叠。</p><p><strong>Consider using a table\ninstead of a collection for text.</strong>It’s generally\nsimpler and more efficient to view and digest textual information when it’s displayed\nin a scrollable list.</p><p>对于文本，考虑使用列表而不是集合。总的来说，当文本信息显示在可滚动的列表中，查看和理解会更简单高效。</p><p><strong>Use caution when making dynamic\nlayout changes.</strong> The\nlayout of a collection can be changed at any time. If you dynamically change\nthe layout while people are viewing and interacting with it, be sure the change\nmakes sense and are easy to track. Unmotivated layout changes can make your app\nseem unpredictable and difficult to use. If focus or context is lost due to a\nlayout change, people are likely to feel like they’re no longer in control.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uicollectionview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UICollectionView</a>.</p><p>动态改变布局的注意事项。集合的布局可以在任何时候被修改。如果您在人们查看、与之交互时动态改变布局，确认这个改变有意义并且很容易追踪。无意义的布局改变会让您的app看起来不可预料又难用。如果因为布局更改而失去焦点或情景，人们会觉得他们失去了控制。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uicollectionview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UICollectionView</a>.】</p><h2><b>Image\nViews图像视图</b></h2><p>An image view displays\na single image or an animated sequence of images over a transparent or opaque\nbackground. Within an image view, images may be stretched, scaled, sized to\nfit, or pinned to a specific location. Image views are noninteractive by\ndefault.</p><p>图像视图在一个透明或不透明的背景上显示一个单独图像或者图像的动态结果。在图像视图中，图像可以扩展，放大，尺寸调整或者贴到某个特定位置。图像视图默认是不可交互的。</p><p><strong>If possible, ensure\nthat all images within an image view are consistently sized.</strong> If your images are different sizes, the image view adjusts them\nseparately. Using consistently sized images is more efficient than using images\nof varying size. It’s even more efficient to use images that are prescaled and\ndon’t require any adjustments.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiimageview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIImageView</a>.</p><p>如果可能，确保在图像视图里的所有图像大小一致。如果图像大小不一，图像视图会分别跳帧他们。使用统一大小的图像比使用不同大小的图像效率更高。使用事先调整大小的图像更高效，而且不需要任何调整。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiimageview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIImageView</a>.】</p><p><strong>NOTE</strong>An\nimage that’s been configured as a template image discards its color and adopts\nany tint that’s been applied to the enclosing image view. See<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiimagerenderingmode/uiimagerenderingmodealwaystemplate\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIImageRenderingModeAlwaysTemplate</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiimage\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIImage</a>.</p><p>注意：被设置为模板图像的图像丢弃颜色并且采用任何用于内附图像视图的填充。</p><h2><b>Maps地图</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f6546ea96890b654acee15f97b476f56_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;555&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f6546ea96890b654acee15f97b476f56_b.png\"/></figure><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5a61cb24e35dfec8e595ee5e17bdc39e_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;555&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"555\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-5a61cb24e35dfec8e595ee5e17bdc39e_b.png\"/></figure>A map view lets you\ndisplay geographical data within your app and supports most of the\nfunctionality provided by the built-in Maps app. A map view can be configured\nto show a standard map, satellite imagery, or both. It can include pins and\noverlays, and supports zooming and panning. If your app supports routing, such\nas in a run-tracking app, you can use a map view to display the route.</p><p>地图视图能在app内显示地理信息，并且支持内置地图app的大部分功能。地图视图可以设置为显示标准地图，卫星地图，或者两者兼有。它可以包括地图钉和覆盖物，并且支持缩放和平移。如果您的app支持路线追踪，比如在一个跑步追踪app中，您可以使用地图视图显示路线。</p><p><strong>In general, keep your\nmap interactive.</strong> People\nare accustomed to using gestures to interact with the Maps app, and expect to\nbe able to interact with your map in similar ways.</p><p>总的来说，保持您的地图是可交互的。人们已经适应了使用手势和地图app交互，并且期望能和您的地图通过熟悉的方式交互。</p><p><strong>Use expected pin\ncolors.</strong> A pin\nidentifies a point of interest on your map. People are familiar with the\nstandard pin colors in the Maps app. Avoid redefining the meaning of these\ncolors in your app. Use red for a destination, green for a starting location,\nand purple for a user-specified location.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/mapkit\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">MapKit</a>.</p><p>使用大家期望的地图钉颜色。地图钉表示地图上的一个兴趣点。人们对于地图app中用标准颜色的地图钉很熟悉。避免在app中重新定义颜色的意义。用红色作为终点，绿色作为起点，紫色作为用户特定的地点。</p><p>详情查看【MapKit】</p><h2><b>Page页面</b></h2><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5af0a8d5ae05ff42a0689294217ed250_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"258\" data-rawheight=\"459\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"258\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;258&#39; height=&#39;459&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"258\" data-rawheight=\"459\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"258\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-5af0a8d5ae05ff42a0689294217ed250_b.png\"/></figure>A page view controller provides a way\nto implement linear navigation between pages of content, such as in a document,\nbook, notepad, or calendar. A page view controller uses one of two styles to\nmanage transitions between pages during navigation—scrolling or page-curl. A\nscrolling transition has no specific appearance; pages fluidly scroll from one\nto the next. A page-curl transition causes pages to curl over as you swipe\nacross the screen, turning like pages in a physical book.</p><p>页面视图控制器提供一个在页面内容之间使用线性导航的方式，例如文档，书，日历。页面视图控制器用两种方式中的一种在导航中管理页面间的过渡-滚动或者卷页面。滚动过渡没有特定的外观；页面流畅地从一页滚动到下一页。卷页面过渡会让页面在您划过屏幕时卷起来，就像一本真正的书那样翻页。</p><p><strong>If appropriate, implement a way to\nnavigate nonlinearly.</strong> When a\npage view controller is used, pages flow sequentially and there’s no way to\njump between nonadjoining pages. If people may need to access pages out of\nsequence in your app, implement a custom control that provides this\nfunctionality.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipageviewcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPageViewController</a>.</p><p>适当时，使用非线性的导航方式。当页面视图控制器被使用时，页面按照顺序流动，非相邻的页面没法相互跳转。如果在app中，人们可能需要到达不按顺序的页面，请使用提供这种功能的自定义控件。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipageviewcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPageViewController</a>.】</p>",
