            "title": "iOS 10 人机界面指南：UI-条", 
            "content": "<h2><b>Navigation Bars导航条</b></h2><p>A navigation bar\nappears at the top of an app screen, below the status bar, and enables\nnavigation through a series of hierarchical app screens. When a new screen is\ndisplayed, a back button, often labeled with the title of the previous screen,\nappears on the left side of the bar. Sometimes, the right side of a navigation\nbar contains a control, such as an Edit or a Done button, for managing content\nwithin the active view. In a split view, a navigation bar may appear in a\nsingle pane of the split view. Navigation bars are translucent, may have a\nbackground tint, and can be configured to hide when appropriate, such as when\nthe keyboard is onscreen, a gesture occurs, or a view resizes.</p><p>导航条显示在app屏幕的上方，状态条下面，使在一系列app层级之间巡游成为可能。当显示新一屏时，一个后退按钮，经常标记为前一屏的标题，出现在导航条的左侧。有时候，导航条右侧包含一个控件，例如Edit编辑或者Done完成按钮，为了在当前视图中管理内容。在Split\nView中，导航条可能出现在一半视图中。导航条是半透明的，可能有背景色，恰当时可以被设置为隐藏的，比如当键盘在屏幕上，一个手势出现了，或者视图调整尺寸了。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b765dcf7374baa81330935d0f5d138a9_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b765dcf7374baa81330935d0f5d138a9_b.png\"/></figure>TIP</strong>Use\na toolbar when navigation isn’t needed or you want multiple controls for\nmanaging content. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-bars/toolbars/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Toolbars</a>.</p><p>当不需要导航条时或者您不需要多种控件来管理内容时，使用工具条。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-bars/toolbars/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Toolbars</a>.】</p><p><strong>Consider showing the title of the\ncurrent view in the navigation bar.</strong> In most cases, a title provides context by letting people know\nwhat they’re looking at. However, if titling a navigation bar seems redundant,\nyou can leave the title empty. For example, Notes doesn’t title the current\nnote because the first line of content supplies all the context needed.</p><p>考虑在导航条上显示当前视图的标题。在大多数情况下，标题通过让人们知道他们在看什么来提供情景。然而，如果给导航条加标题看起来冗余，您可以让它空着。例如，Notes备忘录不会给当前备忘加标题，内容第一行提供了所有需要的情景。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-55ec96a05cfa4e4babcbfd7225c1da47_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-55ec96a05cfa4e4babcbfd7225c1da47_b.png\"/></figure>Consider putting a\nsegmented control in a navigation bar at the top level of an app.</strong> This is especially useful if doing so helps to flatten your\ninformation hierarchy, making it easier for people to find what they’re looking\nfor. If you use a segmented control in a navigation bar, be sure to choose\naccurate back-button titles. For additional guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/segmented-controls/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Segmented Controls</a>.</p><p>考虑在app顶层导航条位置放置分段控件。如果这么做能帮助扁平您的信息层级，这相当有用，让人们找到他们寻找的东西更加容易。如果您在导航条处使用一个分段控件，确认选择精确的返回键标题，详情查看，【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/segmented-controls/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Segmented Controls</a>.】</p><p><strong>Avoid crowding a\nnavigation bar with too many controls.</strong> In general, a navigation bar should contain no more than the\nview’s current title, a back button, and one control that manages the view’s\ncontents. If you use a segmented control in the navigation bar, the bar\nshouldn’t include a title or any controls other than the segmented control.</p><p>避免在一个导航条上放太多控件。总的来说，导航条应该只包含当前视图标题，返回键，一个管理视图内容的控件。如果您在导航条上使用分段控件，那就不要放标题或者其他控件了。</p><p><strong>Don’t include multisegment\nbreadcrumb paths.</strong> The back\nbutton always performs a single action—returning to the previous screen. If you\nthink people might get lost without the full path to the current screen,\nconsider flattening your app’s hierarchy.</p><p>不要包含多分段面包屑路径。返回键总是实现单一功能，即回到前一屏。如果您认为人们没有回到当前视图的完整路径就会迷路，考虑扁平化您的app层级。</p><p><strong>Give text-titled buttons enough\nroom.</strong> If your\nnavigation bar includes multiple text buttons, the text of those buttons may\nappear to run together, making the buttons indistinguishable. Add separation by\ninserting a fixed space item between the buttons. For implementation details,\nsee the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibarbuttonsystemitem/uibarbuttonsystemitemfixedspace\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIBarButtonSystemItemFixedSpace</a> constant value in<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibarbuttonitem\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIBarButtonItem</a>.</p><p>给文本按钮足够大的控件。如果导航条包含多个文本按钮，按钮的文本可能看起来堆一起了，让按钮难以识别。通过在按钮之间插入一个固定的空间添加分割。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibarbuttonsystemitem/uibarbuttonsystemitemfixedspace\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIBarButtonSystemItemFixedSpace</a> constant value in<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibarbuttonitem\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIBarButtonItem</a>.】</p><p><strong>Consider temporarily hiding the\nnavigation bar when displaying full-screen content.</strong> The navigation bar can be distracting when you want to focus on\ncontent. Temporarily hide the bar to provide a more immersive experience. The\nMaps app hides the navigation bar and other interface elements when viewing a\nfull-screen map. If you implement this type of behavior, let users restore the\nnavigation bar with a simple gesture, such as a tap.</p><p>当显示全屏内容时，考虑暂时隐藏导航条。当您想专注内容时，导航条可能会分心。暂时隐藏导航条来提供更沉浸式的体验。当查看全屏地图时，Maps地图app隐藏导航条和其他界面元素。如果您使用这种行为，要让用户通过一个简单的手势重新加载导航条，比如轻点。</p><p><strong>Use the standard back button.</strong> People know that the standard back button lets them retrace\nsteps through a hierarchy of information. However, if you implement a custom\nback button, make sure it still looks like a back button, behaves intuitively,\nmatches the rest of your interface, and is consistently implemented throughout\nyour app. If you replace the system-provided back button chevron with a custom\nimage, supply a custom mask image too. iOS uses this mask to animate the button\ntitle during transitions.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uinavigationbar\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UINavigationBar</a>.</p><p>使用标准返回键。人们知道标准的返回键让他们回溯步骤在信息层级之间。然而，如果您使用一个定制返回键，确认它看上去还是像一个返回键，行为符合直觉，和界面其他部分搭配，并且在整个app中都使用。如果您用自定义图片替换系统提供的返回键头，同时提供一个定制的遮罩图片。iOS使用这个遮罩在过渡中使返回键动起来。</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uinavigationbar\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UINavigationBar</a>.】</p><h2><b>Search Bars搜索条</b></h2><p>People use a search bar to search\nthrough a large collection of values. There are two styles of search\nbars—prominent (the default) and minimal. Contacts employs the prominent style,\nwhich includes a noticeable tinted background. Photos uses the minimal style,\nwhich tends to blend more with the surrounding interface. Search bars are\ntranslucent by default, but can be made opaque. When applicable, a search bar\ncan be configured to automatically hide the navigation bar.</p><p>人们使用搜索条在一大堆值中搜索。搜索条有两种风格——明显的（默认）和最小的。联系人Contacts使用的是最小风格，包含一个引人注意的填充背景。照片Photos使用最小模式，趋向于和周围界面融合。搜索条默认是透明的，但是可以做成不透明的。适当时候，搜索条可以设置为自动隐藏在导航条后面。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3c559a8a0dde13dbf53e94bfd16fa1d1_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"240\" data-rawheight=\"214\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"240\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;240&#39; height=&#39;214&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"240\" data-rawheight=\"214\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"240\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3c559a8a0dde13dbf53e94bfd16fa1d1_b.png\"/></figure>                             Prominent                                </p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3615cbc4cd17bf327fb6098f3512532d_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"240\" data-rawheight=\"214\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"240\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;240&#39; height=&#39;214&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"240\" data-rawheight=\"214\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"240\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-3615cbc4cd17bf327fb6098f3512532d_b.png\"/></figure>Minimal</p><p>A search bar contains a single search\nfield, which can include placeholder text, a Clear button, a Bookmark button,\nand a Results List button. In addition to the search field, a search bar can\ncontain a Cancel button for exiting the search.</p><p>搜索条包含一个单独的搜索区域，可能包含展位文本，一个清除Clear按钮，一个书签Bookmark按钮，和一个结果列表按钮Results\nList。除了搜索区域，搜索条可能包含一个取消Cancel按钮用于离开搜索。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2f9b7bcc46ee8d1c56fd7fffbbcb7aa_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"37\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;37&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"37\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f2f9b7bcc46ee8d1c56fd7fffbbcb7aa_b.png\"/></figure>Placeholder text</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-54803922f27c74658bb6e38334fcee90_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"36\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;36&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"36\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-54803922f27c74658bb6e38334fcee90_b.png\"/></figure>Clear buttom       </p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4812ad08e655f41df1f3aa17cb0a09c6_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"36\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;36&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"36\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-4812ad08e655f41df1f3aa17cb0a09c6_b.png\"/></figure>Cancel button     </p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b66f8d1cb1a15b0a6233e4e38472d1f1_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"36\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;36&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"36\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-b66f8d1cb1a15b0a6233e4e38472d1f1_b.png\"/></figure>Bookmark button</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-300eb8a335c174620c3572ed7c1e0a9f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"36\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;36&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"36\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-300eb8a335c174620c3572ed7c1e0a9f_b.png\"/></figure>Results List button</p><p><strong>Use a search bar rather than a\ntext field to implement search.</strong> A text field doesn’t have the standard search bar appearance\nthat people expect.</p><p>使用搜索条而不是文本框实行搜索。文本框没有人们期待的搜索框外观。</p><p><strong>Enable the Clear and Cancel\nbuttons.</strong> Most\nsearch bars include a Clear button that erases the contents of the field, and a\nCancel button that immediately terminates the search.</p><p>使用清除和取消按钮。大多数搜索条包含一个清除按钮，用来清除文本框里的内容，以及一个取消按钮，能立即停止搜索。</p><p><strong>Pick a search bar style that\nreflects the importance of search in your app.</strong> If search is a primary function in your app, use the default,\nprominent style of search bar. If search is infrequent, use the minimal style.</p><p>根据搜索在app中的重要程度挑选搜索条风格。如果搜索在app中是一个基本功能，使用默认的显眼的搜索条风格。如果搜索不常用，使用最小模式。</p><p><strong>If necessary, provide\nhints and context in a search bar.</strong> The search field can contain placeholder text—such as “Search\nClothing, Shoes and Accessories” or simply “Search”—as a reminder of the\ncontext being searched. A succinct, one-line sentence with appropriate\npunctuation can also be displayed directly above the search bar to provide\nguidance. Stocks, for example, uses text above the search field to let people\nknow they can enter a company name or stock symbol.</p><p>必要时，在搜索条中提供暗示和文本。搜索区域可能包含占位文字——比如“搜索衣物，鞋子和饰品”或者只是“搜索”——作为被搜索文本的提醒。适时出现的一行简洁句子也可以直接显示在搜索条上方。例如，Stocks股票app，使用搜索区域上方的文本让人知道他们可以输入一个公司名或者股票代码。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-64bf7b2fd2c771a354e520d6c949e640_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-64bf7b2fd2c771a354e520d6c949e640_b.png\"/></figure><p><strong>Consider providing helpful\nshortcuts and other content below a search bar.</strong> Use the area under a search bar to help people get to content faster.\nSafari, for example, shows your bookmarks as soon as you tap the search field.\nSelect one to go right to it without entering any search terms. Stocks shows a\nlist of results as you type into the search field. Tap one at any time without\ntyping any more characters.</p><p>考虑在搜索条下方提供有帮助的捷径或者其他内容。使用搜索条下方的区域帮助人们更快达到内容。例如，Safari中，您一点搜索区域就会显示书签。选中一个，不用输入任何搜索项就能直达页面。Stocks股票在您往搜索区域输入时，显示一列结果。任何时候都可以再也不用多打一个字直接点击一个。</p><p><strong>Add the Bookmark or Results List\nbutton if it makes sense in your app.</strong> Use the Bookmark button to provide a shortcut to information\npeople may want to find again, such as saved, previous, or recent searches. Use\nthe Results List button to indicate the presence of results and then display\nthose results when the button is tapped. You can’t display both buttons\nsimultaneously.</p><p>在app中有意义时才添加书签列表或者结果列表按钮。使用书签按钮来为那些人们可能想再找一次的信息，比如已经保存的，前一个，或者最近搜索的。使用结果列表按钮来表示结果的存在，并且在按钮被点击时同时显示那些结果。</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uisearchcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UISearchController</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uisearchbar\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UISearchBar</a>.</p><p>详情请查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uisearchcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UISearchController</a>】和【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uisearchbar\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UISearchBar</a>】</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bb2bc2f291be02703a35626cde41e05c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-bb2bc2f291be02703a35626cde41e05c_b.png\"/></figure><h3>Scope Bars范围条</h3><p>A scope bar can be\nadded to a search bar to let people refine the scope of a search. A scope bar\nadopts the appearance of its search bar.</p><p>范围条可以附加在搜索条，以让人们细化搜索的范围。范围条采用搜索条的外观样式。</p><p><strong>Favor improving search\nresults over including a scope bar.</strong> A scope bar can be useful when there are clearly defined\ncategories in which to search. However, it’s best to improve search results so\nscoping isn’t necessary.</p><p>通过包含一个范围条有利于提升搜索结果。当范围条被清晰定义搜索类别时，他们会很有用。然而，最好还是提升搜索结果，这样就不必使用范围了。</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uisearchbar\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UISearchBar</a>.</p><p>详情查看【UISearchBar】</p><h2><b>Status Bars状态条</b></h2><p>The status bar appears along the upper\nedge of the screen and displays useful information about the device’s current\nstate, such as the time, cellular carrier, network status, and battery level.\nThe actual information shown in the status bar varies depending on the system\nconfiguration.</p><p>状态条出现在屏幕的上边缘，显示设备当前状态相关的有用信息，比如时间，蜂窝信号，网络状况，和电池电量。实际显示在状态条上的信息根据系统设置有所不同。</p><p><strong>Use the system-provided status\nbar.</strong> People\nexpect the status bar to be consistent systemwide. Don’t replace it with a\ncustom status bar.</p><p>使用系统提供的状态栏。人们希望状态栏在整个系统中保持一致。不要用一个个性化的状态条代替。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3a9ebc279d1917775139ad273801b1ef_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-3a9ebc279d1917775139ad273801b1ef_b.png\"/></figure>Light</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-28f35b5d07177effb666dcedd3af06ee_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-28f35b5d07177effb666dcedd3af06ee_b.png\"/></figure>Dark</p><p><strong>Coordinate the status bar style\nwith your app design.</strong> The\nvisual style of the status bar’s text and indicators is either light or dark,\nand can be set globally for your app or individually for different screens. A\ndark status bar works well above light-colored content and a light status bar\nworks well above dark-colored content.</p><p>将状态条风格和app设计相匹配。状态条文本和指示符的视觉风格是浅色的或者是深色的，并且可以为app全局设置或者为不同屏单独设计。一个暗的状态条在浅色内容上很好用，浅的状态条在深色内容上很好用。</p><p><strong>Obscure content under\nthe status bar.</strong> By\ndefault, the background of the status bar is transparent, allowing content\nbeneath to show through. Keep the status bar readable and don’t imply that\ncontent behind it is interactive. There are several common techniques for doing\nthis:</p><p>隐藏状态条下的内容。状态条的背景默认是透明的，使下面的内容能展示出来。保持状态条的可读性，并且不要暗示背后的内容是可交互的。有几个通用技巧：</p><p>·       \nUse a navigation bar in your app, which automatically displays a\nstatus bar background and ensures that content doesn’t appear under the status\nbar.</p><p>·       \n在app中使用导航条，能自动显示一个状态条背景，并且保证内容不会出现在状态条下面。</p><p>·       \nDisplay a custom image, such as a gradient or solid color,\nbehind the status bar.</p><p>·       \n在状态条后显示一个自定义图片，比如渐变或者纯色。</p><p>·       \nApply a blur to the content behind the status bar.</p><p>·       \n为状态条后的内容使用模糊。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2e2bc543f249ada17cfef5fb83c94ee5_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-2e2bc543f249ada17cfef5fb83c94ee5_b.png\"/></figure>Translucent</p><p><strong>Consider\ntemporarily hiding the status bar when displaying full-screen media.</strong> A status bar can be distracting when users are trying to focus\non media. Temporarily hide these elements to provide a more immersive experience.\nThe Photos app, for example, hides the status bar and other interface elements\nduring browsing of full-screen photos.</p><p>当全屏显示媒体文件时，考虑暂时隐藏状态条。当用户视图专注于媒体文件时，状态条会让人分心。暂时隐藏这些元素来提供一个更沉浸式的体验。例如，Photos照片，在浏览全屏照片时，隐藏状态栏或其他界面元素。</p><p><strong>Avoid permanently\nhiding the status bar.</strong> Without a\nstatus bar, people must leave your app to check the time or see if they have a\nWi-Fi connection. Let people redisplay a hidden status bar by using a simple,\ndiscoverable gesture. When browsing full-screen photos in the Photos app, a\nsingle tap shows the status bar again.</p><p>避免永久隐藏状态栏。没有状态栏时，人们必须离开app去查看时间或者看他们是否连上wifi。通过一个简单易发现的手势，让人们再次看到隐藏的状态条。当在Photos照片中浏览全屏照片时，简单的点击就能再次显示状态条。</p><p><strong>Communicate lengthy\nnetwork activity in the status bar.</strong> When your app uses the network, especially for lengthy\noperations, show the network activity status bar indicator so people know\nactivity is occurring. See<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/progress-indicators/%23network-activity-indicators\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Network Activity Indicators</a>.</p><p>在状态条中显示漫长的网络活动。当app用网时，特别是漫长的操作时，显示网络活动状态栏指示符，这样人们能知道活动正在进行。详情见【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/progress-indicators/%23network-activity-indicators\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Network Activity Indicators</a>.】</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uistatusbarstyle\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIStatusBarStyle</a>constant\nin <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiapplication\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIApplication</a> and the<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiviewcontroller/1621416-preferredstatusbarstyle\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">preferredStatusBarStyle</a> property in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiviewcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIViewController</a>.</p><p>详情见【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uistatusbarstyle\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIStatusBarStyle</a>constant\nin <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiapplication\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIApplication</a> and the<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiviewcontroller/1621416-preferredstatusbarstyle\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">preferredStatusBarStyle</a> property in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiviewcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIViewController</a>.】</p><h2><b>Toolbars工具条</b></h2><p>A toolbar appears at\nthe bottom of an app screen and contains buttons for performing actions\nrelevant to the current view or content within it. Toolbars are translucent,\nmay have a background tint, and often hide when people are unlikely to need\nthem. For example, in Safari, the toolbar hides when you begin scrolling the\npage since you are likely reading. You can show it again by tapping the bottom\nof the screen. Toolbars are also hidden when a keyboard is onscreen.</p><p>工具条在app屏幕的底端出现，包含与当前视图或者其中内容有关的操作按钮。工具条是透明的，可能有背景填充，并且经常在人们不需要时隐藏。例如，在Safari中，工具条在您开始滚动页面时隐藏，因为您可能在阅读。您也通过点击屏幕底部让它再显示。当键盘显示时工具条也会隐藏。</p><p><strong>Provide relevant\ntoolbar buttons.</strong> A toolbar\nshould contain frequently used commands that make sense in the current context.</p><p>提供相关的工具条按钮。工具条应该包含在当前情景下有意义的常用命令。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f7399d099c2b1473e3f6f4556ee1a25a_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;278&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"278\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-f7399d099c2b1473e3f6f4556ee1a25a_b.png\"/></figure><p><strong>Consider whether icons or\ntext-titled buttons are right for your app.</strong> Icons work well when you need more than three toolbar buttons.\nWhen you have three buttons or fewer, text can sometimes be clearer. In\nCalendar, for example, text is used because icons would be confusing. The use\nof text also allows the Inbox button to show a count of calendar and event\ninvitations.</p><p>考虑图标还是文本按钮适用于app。当您需要多于三个工具条按钮时很有用。当您有三个或更少的按钮时。有时候文本可能更清楚。例如，在Calender日历应用中，用了文本，因为图标可能让人困惑。文本的使用让收件箱按钮能显示日历和事件邀请的数目。</p><p><strong>Avoid using a segmented control in\na toolbar.</strong> Segmented\ncontrols let people switch contexts, whereas a toolbar is specific to the\ncurrent screen. If you need to provide a way to switch contexts, consider using\na tab bar instead. See<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-bars/tab-bars/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Tab Bars</a>.</p><p>避免在工具条上使用分区控件。分区控件让人们在情景间切换，而工具条是针对当前屏的。如果您需要提供一个切换情景的方式，考虑使用标签栏。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a50ea06129b22c170cffa3124755ef69_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"312\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;312&#39; height=&#39;277&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"312\" data-rawheight=\"277\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"312\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a50ea06129b22c170cffa3124755ef69_b.png\"/></figure>Give text-titled\nbuttons enough room.</strong> If your\ntoolbar includes multiple buttons, the text of those buttons may appear to run\ntogether, making the buttons indistinguishable. Add separation by inserting\nfixed space between the buttons. For implementation details, see the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibarbuttonsystemitem/uibarbuttonsystemitemfixedspace\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIBarButtonSystemItemFixedSpace</a> constant value in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibarbuttonitem\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIBarButtonItem</a>.</p><p>For implementation\ndetails, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitoolbar\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIToolbar</a>.</p><p>给文本按钮足够空间。如果您的工具条包含多个按钮，那些按钮的文本可能看上去挤在一起了，请让按钮之间看起来有区别。通过在按钮之间插入固定的空间来添加分割。详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibarbuttonsystemitem/uibarbuttonsystemitemfixedspace\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIBarButtonSystemItemFixedSpace</a> constant value in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uibarbuttonitem\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIBarButtonItem</a>.】</p><p>详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uitoolbar\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIToolbar</a>.】</p><p><strong>TIP</strong>It’s\nimportant to understand the difference between a toolbar and a tab bar, because\nboth types of bars appear at the bottom of an app screen. A toolbar contains\nbuttons for performing actions related to the current context, such as creating\nan item, deleting an item, adding an annotation, or taking a photo. A tab bar\nlets the user switch quickly between different sections of an app, for example,\nthe Alarm, Stopwatch, and Timer tabs in the Clock app. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-bars/tab-bars/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Tab\nBars</a>. Toolbars and tab bars never appear\ntogether in the same view.</p><p>理解工具条和标签栏之间的区别是很重要的，因为这两种条都在app屏幕低端出现。工具条包含与当前情景相关的操作按钮，比如创建项目，删除羡慕，添加注解，或者拍照。标签栏让用户在app的不同区域快速切换，比如，时钟app里的闹钟、秒表和计时器标签。详情查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-bars/tab-bars/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Tab Bars</a>】工具条和标签栏永远不要在同一视图里同时出现。</p>",

            "title": "iOS 10 人机界面指南：图形", 
            "content": "<h2><b>App Icon App图标</b></h2><p>Every app needs a beautiful and\nmemorable icon that attracts attention in the App Store and stands out on the\nHome screen. Your icon is the first opportunity to communicate, at a glance,\nyour app’s purpose. It also appears throughout the system, such as in Settings\nand search results.</p><p>每个app都需要一个漂亮难忘的图标，在App Store中引人注目，在主屏上脱颖而出。图标是第一个在一瞥中传达app目的的机会。图标在整个系统中都会出现，比如系统设置和搜索结果。  <strong>Embrace simplicity.</strong> Find a single element that captures the essence of your app and\nexpress that element in a simple, unique shape. Add details cautiously. If an\nicon’s content or shape is overly complex, the details can be hard to discern,\nespecially at smaller sizes.</p><p>崇尚简约。找到一个抓住app精髓的元素并且用简洁独特的形状表达这个元素。谨慎地添加细节。如果图标内容或者图形太复杂，这些细节可能难以辨认，特别是在小尺寸上。</p><p><strong>Provide a single focus point.</strong> Design an icon with a single, centered point that immediately\ncaptures attention and clearly identifies your app.</p><p>提供一个单独的焦点。用一个迅速吸引注意力、清晰表达app的单独中心点设计图标。</p><p><strong>Design a recognizable icon.</strong> People shouldn’t have to analyze the icon to figure out what it\nrepresents. For example, the Mail app icon uses an envelope, which is\nuniversally associated with mail. Take time to design a beautiful and engaging\nabstract icon that artistically represents your app’s purpose.</p><p>设计一个具有辨识度的图标。人们不应该去分析图标以弄清楚它代表什么。例如，Mail邮件app使用通常和邮件联系起来的信封作为图标。花点时间设计一个在艺术上代表app意图的，漂亮的吸引人的抽象图标。</p><p><strong>Keep the background simple and\navoid transparency.</strong> Make sure\nyour icon is opaque, and don’t clutter the background. Give it a simple\nbackground so it doesn’t overpower other app icons nearby. You don’t need to\nfill the entire icon with content.</p><p>背景保持简洁，避免半透明。确保图标不透明，不会和背景混杂。赋予其一个简洁的背景，这样它就不会在其他附近的app图标中显得太突兀。您不必将整个图标用内容填满。</p><p><strong>Use words only when they’re\nessential or part of a logo.</strong> An app’s\nname appears below its icon on the Home screen. Don’t include nonessential\nwords that repeat the name or tell people what to do with your app, like\n&#34;Watch&#34; or &#34;Play.&#34; If your design includes any text,\nemphasize words that relate to the actual content your app offers.</p><p>只有在文字很重要时或者是logo一部分时才使用。App的名字会在主屏图标下面出现。不要包含没意义重复名字或者告诉人们您的app是干嘛的文字，例如“Watch”或者“Play”。如果您的设计包含了文字，强调与您app提供的真正内容有关的文字。</p><p><strong>Don’t include photos, screenshots,\nor interface elements.</strong> Photographic\ndetails can be very hard to see at small sizes. Screenshots are too complex for\nan app icon and don’t generally help communicate your app’s purpose. Interface\nelements in an icon are misleading and confusing.</p><p>不要包含照片、截图或者界面元素。照片细节在小尺寸下很难看清。对于app图表来说截图太复杂了并且通常对于传到app意图没有帮助。图标中使用界面元素令人误解困惑。</p><p><strong>Don’t use replicas of Apple\nhardware products.</strong> Apple\nproducts are copyrighted and can’t be reproduced in your icons or images. In\ngeneral, avoid displaying replicas of devices, because hardware designs tend to\nchange frequently and can make your icon look dated.</p><p>不要使用Apple硬件产品的仿制品。Apple产品是有版权的并且不能在您的图标或者图片中被复制。总的来说，避免显示设备的复制品，因为硬件设计可能经常会改变，这会让您的icon看起来过时。</p><p><strong>Don’t place your app icon\nthroughout the interface.</strong> It can be\nconfusing to see an icon used for different purposes throughout an app.\nInstead, consider incorporating your icon’s color scheme. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/visual-design/color/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Color</a>.</p><p>不要在界面中到处放app图标。在一个app中看到一个图标被用作各种用途是很让人费解的。反而应该考虑结合图标配色。</p><p><strong>Test your icon against different\nwallpapers.</strong> You can’t\npredict which wallpaper people will choose for their Home screen, so don’t just\ntest your app against a light or dark color. See how it looks over different\nphotos. Try it on an actual device with a dynamic background that changes\nperspective as the device moves.</p><p>在不同壁纸环境下测试您的图标。您无法预料人们会为主屏选择什么壁纸，所以不要只在浅色或者深色环境下测试app。看看它在不同的照片之上看起来如何。在具有随着设备移动而改变角度的动态壁纸的真实设备上测试它。</p><p><strong>Keep icon corners square.</strong> The system applies a mask that rounds icon corners\nautomatically.</p><p>图标边角应该是方的。系统会自动遮罩使角变圆。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a9cab0df6d0de63e886733b45d6ce588_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"576\" data-rawheight=\"162\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"576\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a9cab0df6d0de63e886733b45d6ce588_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;576&#39; height=&#39;162&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"576\" data-rawheight=\"162\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"576\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a9cab0df6d0de63e886733b45d6ce588_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-a9cab0df6d0de63e886733b45d6ce588_b.png\"/></figure><br/><h3>App\nIcon Sizes App图标尺寸</h3><p>Every app must supply both small and\nlarge app icons. The small icons are used on the Home screen and throughout the\nsystem once your app is installed. The large icon is used by the App Store.</p><p>每个app必须使用大小两个app图标。小图标用于主屏和整个系统中，当您的app一安装啊。大图标用于App Store。</p><p><strong>Provide different sized small\nicons for different devices.</strong> Make sure\nthat your app icon looks great on all the devices you support.</p><p>为不同设备提供不同的小图标。确保您的app图标在所有支持设备上都看起来很棒。</p><p><strong>Mimic your small app icon with\nyour large app icon.</strong> Although\nthe large icon is used differently than the small one, it’s still your app\nicon. It should generally match the smaller version in appearance, although it\ncan be subtly richer and more detailed since there are no visual effects\napplied to it.</p><p>小图标跟大图标得差不多。尽管大图标跟小图标用途不一样，它还是您的app图标。它应该在外观上跟小图标搭配，尽管它可能更丰富或者更精细，因为没有视觉效果影响它。</p><h3>Spotlight and Settings Icons</h3><h3>Spotlight搜索和系统设置图标</h3><p>Every app should provide a small icon\nthat iOS can display when the app name matches a term in a Spotlight search.\nAdditionally, apps with settings should provide a small icon to display in the\nbuilt-in Settings app. Both icons should clearly identify your app—ideally,\nthey should match your app icon. If you don’t provide these icons, iOS might\nshrink your main app icon for display in these locations.</p><p>每个app应该提供用于显示在Spotlight搜索结果的小图标。除此之外，需要设置的app还应该提供一个用于显示在系统设置的小图标。这两个图标都得清晰地代表您的app，理想情况下，他们得与app图标相匹配。如果您不提供这些图标，iOS会直接把主屏app图标缩小用于这些地方的显示。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-895ee9e328f633a4c854622a4a69e4b8_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"100\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-895ee9e328f633a4c854622a4a69e4b8_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;100&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"100\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-895ee9e328f633a4c854622a4a69e4b8_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-895ee9e328f633a4c854622a4a69e4b8_b.png\"/></figure><p><strong>Don’t add an overlay or border to\nyour Settings icon.</strong> iOS\nautomatically adds a 1-pixel stroke to all icons so that they look good on the\nwhite background of Settings.</p><p>不要在系统设置图标上添加叠加或者描边。iOS会自动给所有图标添加一像素的描边，这样他们在系统设置的白背景下看起来很棒。</p><p><strong>TIP</strong>If\nyour app creates custom documents, you don&#39;t need to design document icons\nbecause iOS uses your app icon to create document icons automatically.</p><p>如果您的app会创建文件，您不用设计文件的图标，因为iOS会用您的app图标作为文件图标。</p><h2><b>Custom Icons自定义图标</b></h2><p>If your app includes tasks or modes\nthat can’t be represented by a system icon, or if the system icons don’t match\nyour app’s style, you can create your own icons. A custom icon, sometimes\ncalled a template, discards color information and uses a mask to produce the\nappearance you see onscreen in a navigation bar, tab bar, toolbar, or Home\nscreen quick action.</p><p>如果您的app包含系统图标不能表示的任务或者模块，或者系统图标和您的app风格不搭，您可以创造自己的图标。一个自定义图标，有时叫做template，丢弃颜色信息并且使用遮罩来产生您在屏幕上导航条，切换条，工具条或者主屏快速启动看到的那种效果。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9d7eaf777f4aaa7764673390b173ed4c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"358\" data-rawheight=\"50\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"358\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;358&#39; height=&#39;50&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"358\" data-rawheight=\"50\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"358\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9d7eaf777f4aaa7764673390b173ed4c_b.png\"/></figure>Create simple, recognizable\ndesigns.</strong> Too many\ndetails can make an icon appear sloppy or unreadable. Strive for a design most\npeople will interpret correctly and won’t find offensive.</p><p>创建简洁，可识别的设计。太多细节会让图标看起来太松散，不可读。争取做出大多数人都能准确识别而且不会感觉冒犯的设计。</p><p><strong>Design a solid color icon with\ntransparency, antialiasing, and no drop shadow.</strong> iOS ignores all color information, so there’s no need to use\nmore than one fill color. Allow transparency to define the shape of the icon.</p><p>设计一个带有透明度、抗锯齿的纯色图标，并且没有阴影。iOS忽视所有颜色信息，所以不需要使用一个以上的颜色。允许透明度以限定图标的形状。</p><p><strong>Distinguish your custom icon from\nthe system icons.</strong> Your icon\nshouldn’t be easily mistaken for one of the system-provided icons. If you want\nyour icon to look like it&#39;s related to the iOS icon family, use a very thin\nstroke to draw it. A 1pt stroke (2px for @2x resolution) works well for most\nicons.</p><p>将您的自定义图标和系统图标区分开。您的图标不应该被误认为一个系统图标。如果您想让您的图标看起来属于iOS图标家族，使用非常细的笔触去画。1pt的画笔对于大多数图标效果都很好。（对于@2X分辨率来说是2px）</p><p><strong>Keep your icons consistent.</strong> Whether you use only custom icons or mix custom and system\nicons, all icons in your app should be the same in terms of size, level of\ndetail, perspective, and stroke weight.</p><p>保持图标一致性。无论您只是用自定义图标还是将系统图标和自定义图标混用，app中的所有图标在尺寸，精细度，透视，粗细方面都应该一样。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-340106cb6054dead00e807770e36005e_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"128\" data-rawheight=\"88\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"128\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;128&#39; height=&#39;88&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"128\" data-rawheight=\"88\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"128\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-340106cb6054dead00e807770e36005e_b.png\"/></figure>Provide\ntwo versions of custom tab bar icons.</strong> Provide icons for both the selected and unselected states. The\nselected icon is often a filled-in version of the unselected icon, but some\ndesigns call for variations to this approach. For example, Apple apps sometimes\ninvert icon interiors, increase or reduce strokes, and enclose the icon within\na shape, such as a circle.</p><p>提供两个版本的自定义标签栏图标。提供选中和未选中状态的图标。选中的图标通常是未选中图标的填充版，但是有些设计需要变化。比如，Apple app有时候翻转图标内部，增加或者减少描边，并且将图标括在一个形状中，比如圆形。</p><p><strong>Don’t use text in a custom tab bar\nicon.</strong> If you\nneed to show text, display a title beneath the tab and adjust its placement\naccordingly.</p><p>在自定义标签栏图标中不要使用文本。如果您需要展示文本，在标签下方显示一个标题并且相应地调整位置。</p><p><strong>Don’t use replicas of Apple\nhardware products.</strong> Apple\nproducts are copyrighted and can’t be reproduced in your icons or images. In\ngeneral, avoid displaying replicas of devices because hardware designs tend to\nchange frequently and can make your icon look dated.</p><p>不要使用Apple硬件产品的仿制品。Apple产品是有版权的并且不能在您的图标或者图片中被复制。总的来说，避免显示设备的复制品，因为硬件设计可能经常会改变，这会让您的icon看起来过时。</p><p><strong>Provide alternative text labels\nfor icons.</strong> Alternative\ntext labels aren’t visible onscreen, but they let VoiceOver audibly describe\nwhat&#39;s onscreen, making navigation easier for people with visual impairments.</p><p>为图标提供可替换标签。可替换标签在屏幕上不可见，但是能被VoiceOver读出来，让视障人士可以轻松导航。</p><h3>Custom Icon Sizes自定义图标尺寸</h3><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c53be9b1c141761b64ad903e0199b56_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"174\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c53be9b1c141761b64ad903e0199b56_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;174&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"174\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c53be9b1c141761b64ad903e0199b56_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-1c53be9b1c141761b64ad903e0199b56_b.png\"/></figure><p><b> Image Size and Resolution</b></p><p><b>图片尺寸和分辨率</b></p><p>iOS uses a coordinate system to place\ncontent onscreen. This coordinate system is based on measurements in points,\nwhich map to pixels in the display. On a standard-resolution screen, one point\n(1/72 of an inch) is equal to one pixel. High-resolution screens have a higher\npixel density. Because there are more pixels in the same amount of physical\nspace, there are more pixels per point. As a result, high-resolution displays\nrequire images with more pixels.</p><p>iOS使用写作系统来放置屏幕内容。这个协作系统基于点的测量，能映射到显示器上的像素。在一个标准分辨率的屏幕上，一点（1/72 英寸）等于一像素。高分辨率的屏幕有更高的像素密度。因为在相同大小的物理区域他们有更多像素，每点有更多像素。因此，高分辨率的显示器需要更多像素的图片。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-17de3ffc5831c9fa804eabc9225812c4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"614\" data-rawheight=\"225\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"614\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-17de3ffc5831c9fa804eabc9225812c4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;614&#39; height=&#39;225&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"614\" data-rawheight=\"225\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"614\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-17de3ffc5831c9fa804eabc9225812c4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-17de3ffc5831c9fa804eabc9225812c4_b.png\"/></figure>You must supply high-resolution images\nfor all artwork in your app, for all devices your app supports. Depending on the\ndevice, you accomplish this by multiplying the number of pixels in each image\nby a specific scale factor.</p><p>您必须为app中所有图形提供高分辨率图片，为所有支持的设备。取决于设备，您通过特定的比例乘以每张图片的像素数来实现。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c0e3889fd2af75c4b38f4317cd2eeb2c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"81\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c0e3889fd2af75c4b38f4317cd2eeb2c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;81&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"81\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c0e3889fd2af75c4b38f4317cd2eeb2c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-c0e3889fd2af75c4b38f4317cd2eeb2c_b.png\"/></figure>A standard resolution image has a scale\nfactor of 1.0 and is referred to as an @1x image. High resolution images have a\nscale factor of 2.0 or 3.0 and are referred to as @2x and @3x images. Suppose\nyou have a standard resolution @1x image that’s 100px by 100px, for example.\nThe @2x version of this image would be 200px by 200px. The @3x version would be\n300px by 300px.</p><p>标准分辨率图片的比例是1.0，被称作@1x图片。高分辨图片比例是2.0或3.0，被称作@2x图片和@3x图片。假设您有一张标准分辨率@1x图片，是100像素X100像素的，@2x版本就是200像素X200像素的，@3x版本就是300像素X300像素的。</p><h2><b>Launch Screen启动页</b></h2><p>A launch screen appears instantly when\nyour app starts up. The launch screen is quickly replaced with the first screen\nof your app, giving the impression that your app is fast and responsive. The\nlaunch screen isn’t an opportunity for artistic expression. It’s solely\nintended to enhance the perception of your app as quick to launch and\nimmediately ready for use. Every app must supply a launch screen.</p><p>启动页在app启动是立刻出现。启动页很快被app第一屏取代，给出app快速回应的印象。启动页不是一个用于艺术表达的机会。它只是意在增强app快速启动，立刻能用的感觉。每个app必须使用启动页。</p><p>Launch screen                                         First\nscreen</p><p>Because device screen sizes vary,\nlaunch screen sizes vary too. To accommodate this, you can provide a launch\nscreen as an Xcode storyboard or as a set of static images for the devices your\napp supports. Using an Xcode storyboard is the recommended approach, as\nstoryboards are flexible and adaptable. You can use a single storyboard to\nmanage all of your launch screens. To learn about implementing adaptable\ninterfaces, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/AutolayoutPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Auto Layout Guide</a>.</p><p>因为设备屏幕变化，启动页尺寸也会变化。为了适应，您可以为app支持的设备提供启动页作为Xcode故事版或者作为一系列静态图片。使用Xcode故事版是推荐方式，因为故事版灵活可适应。您可以使用一个单独的故事版来管理所有的启动屏。为了了解实践可适应界面，详情请查看【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/AutolayoutPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Auto Layout Guide</a>.】</p><p><strong>Design a launch screen that’s\nnearly identical to the first screen of your app.</strong> If you include elements that look different when the app\nfinishes launching, people can experience an unpleasant flash between the\nlaunch screen and the first screen of the app.</p><p>设计一个跟第一屏差不多感觉得启动页。如果当app结束启动时包括看起来不一样的元素，人们可能在启动页和第一屏之间体验到不舒服的跳跃。</p><p><strong>Avoid including text on your\nlaunch screen.</strong> Because\nlaunch screens are static, any displayed text won’t be localized.</p><p>在启动页上避免包含文本。因为启动页是静止的，任何显示的文本不会是本地化的。</p><p><strong>Downplay launch.</strong> People are likely to switch apps frequently, so design a launch\nscreen that doesn’t draw attention to the app launching experience.</p><p>淡化启动。人们可能在app之间频繁切换，所以设计一个不会吸引人注意到启动体验的启动页。</p><p><strong>Don’t advertise.</strong> The launch screen isn’t a branding opportunity. Don’t design an\nentry experience that looks like a splash screen or an &#34;About&#34;\nwindow. Don’t include logos or other branding elements unless they’re a static\npart of your app’s first screen.</p><p>不要打广告。启动页不是品牌推广的机会。不要设计像闪屏的进入体验或者介绍页。不要包括logo或者其他推广元素，除非他们是app第一屏的静态元素。</p><h3>Static Launch Screen Images</h3><p>静止的启动页图片</p><p>It’s best to use an Xcode storyboard\nfor your launch screen, but you can provide a set of static images if\nnecessary. Create static images in different sizes for different devices, and\nbe sure to include the status bar region.</p><p>最好用Xcode故事版作为启动页，但是必要时您可以提供一系列静止图片。为不同设备创造不同尺寸的静止图片，确认包含状态条区域。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-196b7219e8fe003832e090457f45a7a1_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"150\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-196b7219e8fe003832e090457f45a7a1_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;150&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"150\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-196b7219e8fe003832e090457f45a7a1_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-196b7219e8fe003832e090457f45a7a1_b.png\"/></figure><h2><b>System Icons系统图标</b></h2><p>iOS provides lots of small\nicons—representing common tasks and types of content—for use in navigation\nbars, tab bars, toolbars, and Home screen quick actions. It’s a good idea to\nuse these built-in icons as much as possible because they&#39;re familiar to\npeople.</p><p>iOS提供很多小图标，代表常见的任务和内容类型，用于导航条，标签栏，工具条，主屏快速动作。最好使用这些内置图标，因为人们对这些图标很熟悉。</p><p><strong>Provide alternative text labels\nfor icons.</strong> Alternative\ntext labels aren’t visible onscreen, but they let VoiceOver audibly describe\nwhat&#39;s onscreen, making navigation easier for people with visual impairments.</p><p>为图标提供可替换标签。可替换标签在屏幕上不可见，但是能被VoiceOver读出来，让视障人士可以轻松导航。</p><h3>Navigation Bar and Toolbar Icons导航条工具栏图标</h3><p><strong>TIP </strong>You\ncan use text instead of icons to represent items in a navigation bar or\ntoolbar. For example, Calendar uses “Today,” “Calendars,” and “Inbox” in the\ntoolbar. You can also use a fixed space element to provide padding between\nnavigation and toolbar icons.</p><p>您可以使用文本而不是图标来表示导航条或者工具条里的项目。例如，日历中用“今天”“日历”和“收件箱”在工具条里。您也可以用一个固定的空元素来填充导航和工具条图标</p><br/><p><b>Button name</b></p><p><b>Function</b></p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-5737daba98624757f1d30e6c3edd63d5_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"19\" data-rawheight=\"27\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"19\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;19&#39; height=&#39;27&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"19\" data-rawheight=\"27\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"19\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-5737daba98624757f1d30e6c3edd63d5_b.png\"/></figure>Action动作</p><p>Shows a modal view containing share\n  extensions, action extensions, and tasks, such as Copy, Favorite, or Find,\n  that are useful in the current context.显示一个模态视图，包含分享扩展，动作扩展，以及任务，例如拷贝，收藏或者寻找等在当前情境下有用的。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9ee4a0b91ecdd1ccd0afa6e0ab0ae86c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"15\" data-rawheight=\"15\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"15\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;15&#39; height=&#39;15&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"15\" data-rawheight=\"15\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"15\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9ee4a0b91ecdd1ccd0afa6e0ab0ae86c_b.png\"/></figure>Add添加</p><p>Creates a new item.添加新项目</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b79df9a2a9c986e02f7712f305171ca3_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"25\" data-rawheight=\"24\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"25\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;25&#39; height=&#39;24&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"25\" data-rawheight=\"24\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"25\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-b79df9a2a9c986e02f7712f305171ca3_b.png\"/></figure>Bookmarks书签</p><p>Shows app-specific bookmarks.显示app中的书签</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-84e1cae4ebbfcc5b27f777ce24775240_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"25\" data-rawheight=\"19\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"25\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;25&#39; height=&#39;19&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"25\" data-rawheight=\"19\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"25\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-84e1cae4ebbfcc5b27f777ce24775240_b.png\"/></figure>Camera相机</p><p>Takes a photo or video, or shows the\n  Photo Library.拍照片或者拍视频，或者显示照片库</p><p>Cancel</p><p>Cancel取消</p><p>Closes the current view or ends edit mode\n  without saving changes.关闭当前视图或者不保存更改就结束编辑模式</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c811602779ab55278567938b16b766f9_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"23\" data-rawheight=\"23\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"23\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;23&#39; height=&#39;23&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"23\" data-rawheight=\"23\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"23\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-c811602779ab55278567938b16b766f9_b.png\"/></figure>Compose创作</p><p>Opens a new view in edit mode.在编辑模式中打开一个新视图</p><p>Done</p><p>Done完成</p><p>Saves the state and closes the current\n  view, or exits edit mode.存储状态并且关闭当前视图，或者离开编辑状态。</p><p>Edit</p><p>Edit编辑</p><p>Enters edit mode in the current context.在当前情境中进入编辑模式</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-40d2b406ce6139b26d761554ddef4634_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"24\" data-rawheight=\"15\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"24\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;24&#39; height=&#39;15&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"24\" data-rawheight=\"15\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"24\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-40d2b406ce6139b26d761554ddef4634_b.png\"/></figure>Fast Forward快进</p><p>Fast-forwards through media playback or\n  slides.媒体或者幻灯片快进</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-89f50df00daacc5d77c8d97d9a5f4a09_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"21\" data-rawheight=\"18\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"21\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;21&#39; height=&#39;18&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"21\" data-rawheight=\"18\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"21\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-89f50df00daacc5d77c8d97d9a5f4a09_b.png\"/></figure>Organize组织</p><p>Moves an item to a new destination, such\n  as a folder.将项目移动到新目的地，比如文件夹</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4881e667ee6142e92af21d879cfa05a7_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"15\" data-rawheight=\"19\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"15\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;15&#39; height=&#39;19&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"15\" data-rawheight=\"19\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"15\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-4881e667ee6142e92af21d879cfa05a7_b.png\"/></figure>Pause暂停</p><p>Pauses media playback or slides. Always\n  store the current location when pausing, so playback can resume later.暂停媒体或者幻灯片播放。暂停时总是存储当前位置，之后就可以继续播放了。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e8e9bc304bce9d71938d015c22e69eee_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"17\" data-rawheight=\"19\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"17\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;17&#39; height=&#39;19&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"17\" data-rawheight=\"19\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"17\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-e8e9bc304bce9d71938d015c22e69eee_b.png\"/></figure>Play播放</p><p>Begins or resumes media playback or\n  slides.开始或继续媒体或幻灯片播放</p><p>Redo</p><p>Redo重做</p><p>Redoes the last action that was undone.重做上一个被撤销的动作</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6404df4a815bcc4b5073a34600226bfd_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"18\" data-rawheight=\"22\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"18\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;18&#39; height=&#39;22&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"18\" data-rawheight=\"22\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"18\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-6404df4a815bcc4b5073a34600226bfd_b.png\"/></figure>Refresh刷新</p><p>Refreshes content. Use this icon\n  sparingly, as your app should refresh content automatically whenever\n  possible.刷新内容。慎用此图标，因为app应该尽可能自动刷新内容。</p><p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-9bfa132ec6d86031aae905a77a65d74c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"25\" data-rawheight=\"19\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"25\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39;
