            "upvote": 3, 
            "title": "iOS 10 人机界面指南：视觉设计", 
            "content": "<h2><b>Animation动画</b></h2><p>Beautiful, subtle animation throughout\niOS builds a visual sense of connection between people and content onscreen.\nWhen used appropriately, animation can convey status, provide feedback, enhance\nthe sense of direct manipulation, and help users visualize the results of their\nactions.</p><p>遍布iOS的美丽精妙的动画在人和屏幕内容之间创造了视觉连接。适当使用时，动画能传达状态，提供反馈，增强直接操作的感觉，并且帮助用户可视化操作结果。</p><p><strong>Use animation and motion effects\njudiciously.</strong> Don’t use\nanimation for the sake of using animation. Excessive or gratuitous animation\ncan make people feel disconnected or distracted, especially in apps that don’t\nprovide an immersive experience. iOS uses motion effects, such as a parallax\neffect, to create the perception of depth on the Home screen and in other\nareas. These effects can increase understanding and enjoyment, but overusing\nthem can make an app feel disorienting and difficult to control. If you\nimplement motion effects, always test the results to make sure they work well.</p><p>明智使用动画和动效。不要为了用动画而用动画。过多的没必要的动画会让人感觉不连贯，分心，特别是在非沉浸式体验的app中。iOS使用动效，例如视差效果，来在主屏和其他区域创建深度感。这些效果，能增加理解和乐趣，但是滥用动效会让人感觉app令人困惑，难以控制。如果您使用动效，请始终测试结果，来确认他们运行良好。</p><p><strong>Strive for realism and\ncredibility.</strong> People\ntend to accept artistic license, but they can feel disoriented when movement\ndoesn’t make sense or appears to defy physical laws. If someone reveals a view\nby sliding it down from the top of the screen, for example, they should be able\ndismiss the view by sliding it back up.</p><p>力争真实可信。人们趋向于接受艺术创作，但是当动作没有意义或者看起来违背物理定律时，他们可能感觉困惑。例如，如果有人通过从屏幕顶部向下滑动显示一个视图，那他们应该通过把它划上去来离开视图。</p><p><strong>Use consistent animation.</strong> A familiar, flowing experience keeps users engaged. They&#39;re\naccustomed to the subtle animation used throughout iOS, such as smooth\ntransitions, fluid changes in device orientation, and physics-based scrolling.\nUnless you’re creating an immersive experience, such as a game, custom\nanimation should be comparable to the built-in animations.</p><p>使用一致的动画。一个贴心的，流畅的体验能够保持用户活跃度。他们对于iOS中的精妙动画很熟悉，例如顺滑的过渡，流畅的设备方向改变，以及基于物理的滚动。除非您在创造沉浸式体验，比如游戏，个性化动画应该与系统动画相当。</p><p><strong>Make animations optional.</strong> When the option to reduce motion is enabled in accessibility\npreferences, your app should minimize or eliminate application animations.</p><p>动画应该是可选项。当无障碍偏好设置中减少动画的选项被打开，您的app应该减少甚至消除动画。</p><h2><b>Branding品牌传播</b></h2><p>Successful branding involves more than\njust adding brand assets to your app. Great apps express unique brand identity\nthrough smart font, color, and image decisions. Provide enough branding to give\npeople context in your app, but not so much that it becomes a distraction.</p><p>成功的品牌传播不只是将品牌资产添加到app。好的app通过字体、颜色、图片传达独特的品牌识别。在app中提供充足的品牌传播来给人们情景，但是不要做得太过，以免成为干扰。</p><p><strong>Incorporate refined, unobtrusive\nbranding.</strong> People\nuse your app to be entertained, get information, or get things done, not to\nwatch an advertisement. For the best experience, subtly incorporate your brand\nthrough your app’s design. Using colors from your app icon throughout your\ninterface is one great way to provide context in your app.</p><p>整合精致的不显眼的品牌传播。人们用您的app获得娱乐，获取信息，或者做事，而不是看广告。为了最好的体验，在app设计中巧妙地结合您的品牌。在整个界面中使用app图标的颜色是在app中提供情境的好方法。</p><p><strong>Don’t let branding get in the way\nof great app design.</strong> Above\nall, make your app feel like an iOS app. Ensure that it&#39;s intuitive, easy to\nnavigate, easy to use, and focuses on content. Even if your app is available on\nother platforms, avoid diluting your design by focusing too much on consistent\nbranding.</p><p>不要让品牌传播阻碍app设计。最重要的是，让您的app看起来像iOS app。确保它是直观的，容易导航的，易用的，聚焦在内容的。即使app在其他平台上也能获得，要避免在品牌传播上投放太多注意力，冲淡设计。</p><p><strong>Defer to content over branding.</strong> Showing a persistent bar at the top of the screen that does nothing\nbut display brand assets means there’s less room for viewing content. Instead,\nconsider less intrusive ways to implement branding, such as using a custom\ncolor scheme or font, or subtly customizing the background.</p><p>内容优先，品牌传播是次要的。一直在屏幕顶端显示一条没用的品牌资产，意味着查看内容的空间减小了。相反，考虑用打扰性更小的方式来实践品牌传播，例如使用定制的配色或者字体，或精妙定制的背景。</p><p><strong>Resist the temptation to display\nyour logo throughout your app.</strong> Avoid displaying a logo throughout your app unless it’s\nnecessary for providing context. This is especially important in navigation\nbars, where a title is more helpful.</p><p>拒绝在整个app中显示logo的诱惑。避免在APP中到处显示logo，除非这对于提供情景是必须的。特别是在导航条中，标题更有用。</p><p><strong>Adhere to Apple&#39;s trademark\nguidelines.</strong> Apple\nTrademarks should not appear in your app name or imagery. See<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.apple.com/legal/intellectual-property/trademark/appletmlist.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Trademark List</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.apple.com/legal/intellectual-property/guidelinesfor3rdparties.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Guidelines for Using\nApple Trademarks</a>.</p><p>用Apple的商标。Apple商标不应该出现在app名字或者图像中。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.apple.com/legal/intellectual-property/trademark/appletmlist.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Apple Trademark List</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.apple.com/legal/intellectual-property/guidelinesfor3rdparties.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Guidelines for Using\nApple Trademarks</a>.】</p><p><strong>TIP</strong>The\nApp Store offers more opportunities to highlight your brand. For guidance, see\nabout <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/app-store/marketing/guidelines/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App\nStore Marketing Guidelines</a>.</p><p>App Store为宣传您的品牌提供了更多机会。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/app-store/marketing/guidelines/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App\nStore Marketing Guidelines</a>.】</p><h2><b>Color色彩</b></h2><p>In iOS, color can indicate\ninteractivity, impart vitality, and provide visual continuity. Look to the\nsystem’s color scheme for guidance when picking app tint colors that look great\nindividually and in combination, on both light and dark backgrounds.</p><p>在iOS中，色彩能说明交互性，传递活力，提供视觉连续性。当挑选单独看着好，合起来看也好，浅色和深色背景上看起来也好的app颜色时，请参考系统配色。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b29e5c7e7a61fa440f79c544b2d0b472_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"771\" data-rawheight=\"132\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"771\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b29e5c7e7a61fa440f79c544b2d0b472_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;771&#39; height=&#39;132&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"771\" data-rawheight=\"132\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"771\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b29e5c7e7a61fa440f79c544b2d0b472_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-b29e5c7e7a61fa440f79c544b2d0b472_b.png\"/></figure><p><strong>Use complementary colors\nthroughout your app.</strong> The\ncolors in your app should work well together, not conflict or distract. If\npastels are essential to your app’s style, for example, use a coordinating set\nof pastels.</p><p>在app中使用互补色。这些颜色在app中应该很搭配，不冲突，不让人分心。如果粉彩对于您app的风格很重要，使用一组协调的粉彩。</p><p><strong>Consider choosing a key color to\nindicate interactivity throughout your app.</strong> In Notes, interactive elements are yellow. In Calendar,\ninteractive elements are red. If you define a key color that denotes\ninteractivity, make sure other colors don’t compete with it.</p><p>考虑在整个app中选择一种关键色说明交互性。在备忘录中，交互元素是黄色的。在日历中，交互元素是红的。如果您定义一种关键色代表交互性，确认其他的颜色不会与之冲突。</p><p><strong>In general, choose a limited color\npalette that coordinates with your app logo.</strong> Subtle use of color is a great way to communicate your brand.</p><p>总的来说，选择一个跟您applogo协调的调色盘。精妙使用颜色是传播品牌的好方法。</p><p><strong>Apply color profiles to your\nimages.</strong> The\ndefault color space on iOS is Standard RGB (sRGB). To ensure that colors are\ncorrectly matched to this color space, make sure your images include embedded\ncolor profiles.</p><p>图片需要带有颜色配置文件。iOS的默认颜色空间是sRGB。为了确保颜色正确匹配sRGB，确认您的图片包含嵌入的颜色配置文件。</p><p><strong>Use wide color to enhance the\nvisual experience on compatible devices.</strong> Wide color displays support a P3 color space that can produce\nricher, more saturated colors than sRGB. When the experience calls for vivid\nimagery, prepare images using the Display P3 color profile at 16 bits per\npixel. For best results, these images should be saved as 16-bit .png files with\nthe Display P3 profile embedded.</p><p>使用广色域以增强兼容设备上的视觉体验。支持P3颜色空间的广色域显示器能产生比sRGB更丰富更饱满的颜色。当体验需要栩栩如生的图片时，准备使用Display\nP3颜色配置文件的16位彩色图片。这些图片最好被存储为16位彩色png，内嵌Display P3颜色配置文件。</p><p><strong>TIP</strong>On\nMacs with wide color displays, you can use the system color picker to select\nand preview P3 colors, and to compare them with sRGB colors.</p><p>在带有广色域显示器的Mac上，您能使用系统拾色器来选择和预览P3颜色，与sRGB颜色相比较。</p><p><strong>Avoid using the same color for\ninteractive and noninteractive elements.</strong> If interactive and noninteractive elements have the same color,\nit’s hard for people to know where to tap. Consider how translucency affects\ncolors. Colors can appear different when placed behind a translucent element,\nor when applied to a translucent element, such as a toolbar.</p><p>避免为可交互元素及不可交互元素使用同一颜色。如果可交互元素和不可交互元素使用同一颜色，用户就不知道往哪点了。半透明会如何影响色彩。在半透明元素后面，颜色会看起来不一样。或者是放在一个半透明元素上，比如工具条。</p><p><strong>Test your app’s color scheme under\na variety of lighting conditions.</strong> Lighting varies significantly both indoors and outdoors, based\non room ambiance, time of day, the weather, and more. Colors you see on your\ncomputer won’t always look the same when your app is used in the real world.\nAlways preview your app under multiple lighting conditions, including outdoors\non a sunny day, to see how colors appear. If necessary, adjust colors to\nprovide the best possible viewing experience in the majority of use cases.</p><p>在不同的光照条件下测试app配色。室内外的光照在室内氛围、时间、天气等诸多元素的作用下，变化非常大。当您在现实世界使用app时，在您电脑上看到的颜色不会总是看起来一样。总是在不同光照条件下预览您的app，包括晴天的室外，看这些颜色看起来如何。必要时，将颜色调整为在大多数使用情况下表现出色。</p><p><strong>Consider how the True Tone display\naffects color.</strong> The True\nTone display uses ambient light sensors to automatically adjust the white point\nof the display to adapt to the lighting conditions of the current environment.\nApps that focus primarily on reading, photos, video, and gaming can strengthen\nor weaken this effect by specifying a white point adaptivity style. For\nimplementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Reference/InfoPlistKeyReference/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Information Property\nList Key Reference</a>.</p><p>考虑True Tone显示器会如何影响颜色。True Tone显示器使用环境光传感器，来自动调节显示器上的白点，以适应当前环境下的光照条件。主要用于阅读，照片，视频和游戏的app可以通过特定一个白点适应模式来加强或者减弱这种效果。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/General/Reference/InfoPlistKeyReference/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Information Property\nList Key Reference</a>.】</p><p>Play</p><p><strong>Be aware of colorblindness and how\ndifferent cultures perceive color.</strong> People see colors differently. Many colorblind people, for\nexample, find it difficult to distinguish red from green (and either color from\ngray), or blue from orange. Avoid using these color combinations as the only\nway to distinguish between two states or values. For example, instead of using\nred and green circles to indicate offline and online, use a red square and a\ngreen circle. Some image-editing software includes tools that can help you\nproof for colorblindness. Also consider how your use of color might be\nperceived in other countries and cultures. In some cultures, for example, red\nis used to communicate danger. In others, red has positive connotations. Make\nsure the colors in your app send the appropriate message.</p><p>注意色盲人士和不同的文化如何理解颜色。人们对颜色的看法是不同的。比如，很多色盲人士，很难区别红绿色（以及灰色），或者蓝橙色。避免使用这些颜色组合作为去分两种状态的唯一途径。比如，用一个红方块和一个绿圆圈区分下线上线状态，而不是红圆圈和绿圆圈。一些图片编辑软件包含确诊色盲的工具。也要考虑您使用的颜色在其他国家其他文化中被如何看待。比如，在一些文化中，红色被视为危险。在其他文化中，红色有积极的意思。确认您app中的颜色传达了恰当的信息。</p><p><strong>Use sufficient color contrast\nratios.</strong> Insufficient\ncontrast in your app makes content hard to read for everyone. Icons and text\nmight blend with the background, for example. An online color contrast calculator\ncan help you accurately analyze the color contrast in your app, to ensure that\nit meets optimal standards. Strive for a minimum contrast ratio of 4.5:1,\nalthough 7:1 is preferred because it meets more stringent accessibility\nstandards.</p><p>色彩对比度要足。App中对比度不足会让内容难以阅读。比如，图标和文本会和背景混在一起。在线颜色对比度计算器能帮您精确分析app中的色彩对比，来确保符合视觉标准。至少要达到4.5：1的对比度，7:1更好，因为这能满足更严格的无障碍标准。</p><h2><b>Layout布局</b></h2><p>People generally want the ability to\nuse their favorite apps on all of their devices and in any orientation. In iOS,\ninterface elements and layouts can be configured to automatically change shape\nand size on different devices, during multitasking on iPad, in split view, and\nwhen the screen is rotated. It’s essential that you plan ahead and design an\napp that provides a great experience in any context.</p><p>人们通常希望能够在所有设备任何方向上使用它们最爱的app。在iOS中，在不同设备上，在iPad多任务状态下，在Split View，在屏幕被旋转时，界面元素和布局能重新布局以自动改变形状和尺寸。提前规划并且设计在任何情境下都提供良好体验的app是很重要的。</p><p><strong>Maintain focus on the current\ncontent during context changes.</strong> Content is your highest priority. Changing focus when the environment\nchanges can be disorienting, frustrating, and make people feel like they’ve\nlost control of the app.</p><p>情景变幻时，保持聚焦当前内容。内容是最重要的。当情景改变时焦点也改变，这会让人困惑，沮丧，让人感觉他们对app失去控制。</p><p><strong>Ensure primary content is clear at\nits default size.</strong> People\nshouldn’t have to scroll horizontally to read important text, or zoom to see\nprimary images, unless they choose to change the size.</p><p>确保基本内容在默认尺寸下清晰可读。人们不应该横向滚动来阅读重要的文本，或者放大去看基本图片，除非他们选择改变尺寸。</p><p><strong>Maintain an overall consistent\nappearance throughout your app.</strong> In general, elements with similar functions should look similar.</p><p>在整个app中保持全局一致性。总的来说，相似功能的元素应该看起来差不多。</p><p><strong>Use visual weight and balance to\ndenote importance.</strong> Large\nitems catch the eye and appear more important than smaller ones. Larger items\nare also easier to tap, which is especially important when an app is used in\ndistracting surroundings, such as in the kitchen or a gym. In general, place\nprincipal items in the upper half of the screen and—in a left-to-right reading\ncontext—near the left side of the screen.</p><p>使用视觉重量和平衡来表达重要性。大的物体看起来更吸引眼球而且看起来比小东西更重要。大项目更容易点击，特别是当app用于令人分心的环境，比如在厨房或者健身房。总的来说，把重要的项目放在屏幕左上部分（在从左至右的阅读顺序中）</p><p><strong>Use alignment to ease scanning and\nto communicate organization and hierarchy.</strong> Alignment makes an app look neat and organized, helps people\nfocus while scrolling, and makes it easier to find information. Indentation and\nalignment can also indicate how groups of content are related.</p><p>使用对齐来使浏览更容易并且传达组织和阶层。对齐让app看起来整洁有组织，帮助人们在滚动浏览时聚焦，并且让找到信息更容易。缩进和对齐也能说明内容组之间时如何联系的。</p><p><strong>Avoid gratuitous layout changes.</strong> Just because someone rotates a device doesn’t mean the entire\nlayout needs to change. For example, if your app shows a grid of images in\nportrait mode, it doesn’t have to present the same images as a list in\nlandscape mode. Instead, it might simply adjust the dimensions of the grid. Try\nto maintain a comparable experience in all contexts.</p><p>避免无意义的布局更改。只是因为某人转动了设备，不意味着整个布局需要改变。例如，如果您的app在纵向模式下显示图片网格，它不必在横向模式下显示同样图片网格。相反，它可以简单调整网格的尺寸。尽量在所有情境下保持可比的体验。</p><p><strong>If possible, support both portrait\nand landscape orientations.</strong> People\nprefer to use apps in different orientations, so it’s best when you can fulfill\nthat expectation.</p><p>如果可能的话，支持纵向模式和横向模式。人们更喜欢在不同方向使用app，所以最好您能符合他们的期望。</p><p><strong>If your app supports only one\norientation, support both variants.</strong> If it’s essential that your app run in a single orientation,\nmake sure it supports both orientation variants. For example, if your app only\nruns in landscape mode, it should be usable regardless of whether the Home\nbutton is on the left or the right. If the device is rotated 180 degrees while\nusing your app, your app should respond by rotating its content 180 degrees. If\nyour app doesn&#39;t rotate automatically when someone holds the device wrong,\nthey&#39;ll know instinctively to rotate it. You don&#39;t need to tell them.</p><p>如果app只支持一种方向，那就支持变种情况。如果app只在一个方向运行是很重要的，确认它能支持各种该方向的变种。比如，如果app只在横向运行，那么无论Home键在左边还是在右边都可用。如果在使用app时设备被旋转180度，您的app应该把内容也旋转180度。如果app在某人错误地握持设备时没有自动旋转，他们就直接知道该转一下了。您不必告诉他们。</p><p><strong>Customize your app’s response to\nrotation according to context.</strong> A game that lets people move a character by rotating the device,\nfor example, probably shouldn’t switch orientations during gameplay. It could,\nhowever, display menus and intro sequences based on the current orientation.</p><p>根据情景个性化定制app对于旋转的反应。比如，一个通过旋转设备来移动游戏角色的游戏，在游戏期间可能不要切换方向。然而，它可以基于当前方向显示菜单和介绍。</p><p><strong>Provide ample spacing for\ninteractive elements.</strong> Try to\nmaintain a minimum tappable area of 44pt x 44pt for all controls.</p><p>为交互元素提供足够空间。尽量为所有空间保持最小44ptX44pt的可点击空间。</p><p><strong>Be prepared for text size changes.</strong> People expect most apps to respond appropriately when they\nchoose a different text size in Settings. To accommodate some text-size\nchanges, you might need to adjust the layout. For more information about text\nusage in your app, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/visual-design/typography/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Typography</a>.</p><p>准备好文字尺寸的更改。当人们在系统设置中选择不同字号时，人们期待大多数app能恰当回应。为了兼容字号更改，您可能需要调整布局。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/visual-design/typography/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Typography</a>.】</p><p>For implementation details on\nadaptivity, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/AutolayoutPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Auto Layout Guide</a>.</p><p>关于实践可适应性，详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/AutolayoutPG/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Auto Layout Guide</a>】</p><h2><b>Typography字体</b></h2><p>San Francisco is the system font on\niOS. There are two variants of this font: SF UI Text for text 19 points or\nsmaller, and SF UI Display for text 20 points or larger. When you use the\nsystem font for text in labels and other interface elements, iOS automatically\napplies the most appropriate text style of the font based on the point size. It\nalso switches fonts automatically as needed and respects accessibility\nsettings. Download the San Francisco fonts in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/resources/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Resources</a>.</p><p>San Francisco是iOS的系统字体。这个字体有俩变种:SF UI\nText,用于19点或更小的文字；SF UI Display，用于20点或更大的文字。当您在标签和其他界面元素中使用系统文字，iOS自动基于点尺寸实施最合适的字体风格。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-aa95fe81f3abaf27c0c13683bfeb700f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"556\" data-rawheight=\"133\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"556\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-aa95fe81f3abaf27c0c13683bfeb700f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;556&#39; height=&#39;133&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"556\" data-rawheight=\"133\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"556\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-aa95fe81f3abaf27c0c13683bfeb700f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-aa95fe81f3abaf27c0c13683bfeb700f_b.png\"/></figure><p>iOS uses San\nFrancisco as the system font for Latin, Greek and Cyrillic alphabets, and a\nvariety of other typefaces for other scripts.</p><p><strong>Emphasize important information.</strong> Use font weight, size, and color to highlight the most important\ninformation in your app.</p><p>强调重要信息。使用字重，字号，颜色来强调app中最重要的信息。</p><p><strong>If possible, use a single font.</strong> Mixing several different fonts can make your app seem fragmented\nand sloppy. Consider using one font and just a few styles and sizes.</p><p>可能的话尽量只用一种字体。混合多种字体会让app看起来碎片又松散。考虑使用一种字体和一两种风格、字号。</p><p><strong>Use built-in text styles whenever\npossible.</strong> The\nbuilt-in text styles let you express content in ways that are visually\ndistinct, while retaining optimal legibility. These styles are based on the\nsystem fonts and allow you to take advantage of key typographic features, such\nas Dynamic Type, which automatically adjusts tracking and leading for every\nfont size. iOS includes the following text styles:</p><p>尽量使用系统内置的文本风格。系统内置文本风格能视觉清晰地展示内容，同时保持最佳可读性。这些风格基于系统字体，并且允许您利用重要的字体特性，比如动态字体，能为每个字号自动调节字符间距和行间距。iOS包含以下文本风格：</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fa957ff11d380add6124d734d9b04c10_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"112\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fa957ff11d380add6124d734d9b04c10_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;112&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"112\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fa957ff11d380add6124d734d9b04c10_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-fa957ff11d380add6124d734d9b04c10_b.png\"/></figure><p><strong>Make sure custom fonts are\nlegible.</strong> Custom\ntypefaces are supported on iOS, but are often tough to read. Unless your app\nhas a compelling need for a custom font, such as for branding purposes or to\ncreate an immersive gaming experience, stick with the system fonts. If you do\nuse a custom font, make sure it’s readable.</p><p>确保自定义字体是可读的。iOS支持自定义字体，但是他们经常难以阅读。除非您的app迫切需要自定义字体，比如为了品牌传播或者创建沉浸式的游戏体验，最好还是用系统字体吧。如果您使用自定义字体，确保它的可读性。</p><p><strong>Implement accessibility features\nfor custom fonts.</strong> System\nfonts automatically react to accessibility features, such as when bold text is\nenabled. Apps using custom fonts should implement the same behavior by checking\nwhether accessibility features are enabled and registering for notifications\nwhen they change. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/interaction/accessibility/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Accessibility</a>.</p><p>对自定义字体使用无障碍特性。系统字体自动对无障碍特性做出反应，比如加粗文字。使用自定义字体的app应该通过查看无障碍特性是否开启，来实行同样的行为，并且在改变时注册通知。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/interaction/accessibility/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Accessibility</a>.】</p><h3>Dynamic Type Sizes动态字体字号</h3><p>Both variants of the SF UI\ntypeface were designed to be highly legible at both small and large sizes.\nDynamic Type provides additional flexibility by letting readers choose their\npreferred text size.</p><p>SF UI字体的两个变种都被设计为具有高度可读性，无论大小字号。动态字体通过让读者选择喜欢的字号来提供更高的灵活性。</p><p><strong><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-10b2f2504fb1aed9b8cf7d77f56cc9ff_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"299\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-10b2f2504fb1aed9b8cf7d77f56cc9ff_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;299&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"299\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-10b2f2504fb1aed9b8cf7d77f56cc9ff_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-10b2f2504fb1aed9b8cf7d77f56cc9ff_b.png\"/></figure><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e59d4d81a47c255502b8ee7d82ba5b5f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"313\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-e59d4d81a47c255502b8ee7d82ba5b5f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;301&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"301\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8f7a9ae1c220e7113b40d2852241cc24_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-8f7a9ae1c220e7113b40d2852241cc24_b.png\"/></figure><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-58d570936fd0feeffc6faaf2d542186b_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"289\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-58d570936fd0feeffc6faaf2d542186b_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;289&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"289\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-58d570936fd0feeffc6faaf2d542186b_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-58d570936fd0feeffc6faaf2d542186b_b.png\"/></figure>Prioritize content when responding\nto text-size changes.</strong> Not all content\nis equally important. When someone chooses a larger size, they want to make the\ncontent they care about easier to read; they don’t always want every word on\nthe screen to be larger.</p><p>在回应字号更改时，区分内容优先级。不是所有的内容都一样重要。如果某人选择更大的字号，他们想让他们关心的内容更易读，而不是想让屏幕上的每一个字都变大。</p><p>Download a dynamic type size table in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/resources/%23dynamic-type-sizes\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Resources</a>.</p><p>在【 <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/resources/%23dynamic-type-sizes\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Resources</a>.】中下载动态字体表格</p><h3>Font Usage and Tracking字体用法和字符间距</h3><p><strong>Use the correct font variant in\ninterface mockups.</strong> Use SF UI\nText for text 19 points or smaller. Use SF UI Display for text 20 points or\nlarger. Adjust tracking—the spacing between letters—appropriately, as follows:</p><p>在界面模型中使用正确的字体变种。对于19点及更小的文字使用SF UI Text，对于20点及更大的文字使用SF UI Display。恰当调整字符间距。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bad571af86bd186ee28de2e1b2022336_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"340\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bad571af86bd186ee28de2e1b2022336_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;340&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"340\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bad571af86bd186ee28de2e1b2022336_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-bad571af86bd186ee28de2e1b2022336_b.png\"/></figure><br/><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ecdab0611a03cf6683855f567e5870d_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"259\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ecdab0611a03cf6683855f567e5870d_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;554&#39; height=&#39;259&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"554\" data-rawheight=\"259\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"554\" data-original=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ecdab0611a03cf6683855f567e5870d_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-1ecdab0611a03cf6683855f567e5870d_b.png\"/></figure>",

            "userLink": "https://www.zhihu.com/people/55ad36e0c5bc228f82bb1c0030fc3dfd", 
            "upvote": 1, 
            "title": "iOS 10 人机界面指南：特性", 
            "content": "<p><b>Multitasking多任务</b></p><p>Multitasking lets you quickly switch from one app to another at any time through a multitasking interface on an iOS device, or by using a multifinger gesture on an iPad. On iPad, multitasking also lets you use two apps at once in Slide Over, Split View, or Picture in Picture mode. Slide Over is accessed by swiping from the right side of the screen to temporarily use a second app without leaving the context of the current app, such as to quickly view your Mail inbox while you’re using Safari. Split View lets you use two side-by-side apps at the same time, and Picture in Picture lets you watch a video while working in another app.</p><p>多任务特性使得您可以在任何时候通过iOS设备上的多任务界面在app之间切换，或者在iPad上使用一个多指手势。在iPad上，多任务特性也能让您在Slide Over, Split View, 或者Picture in Picture 模式中同时使用两个app。Slide Over通过从屏幕右边滑动来暂时使用第二个app，不用离开当前app的场景，比如在使用Safari时快速查看邮箱收件箱。Spilt View让您可以同时使用两个各占屏幕一半的app，画中画模式让您能在使用另一个app时观看视频。</p><p>Designing an app that thrives in a multitasking environment hinges on your app harmoniously coexisting with other apps on the device. This means your app shouldn’t use too much CPU, memory, screen space, or other system resources. It should respond well to sudden interruptions and audio from other apps, transition to and from the background quickly and smoothly, and behave responsibly when operating in the background.<br/></p><p>设计在多任务环境中茁壮成长的app取决于这个app能与其他在设备上的app和谐共处。就是说这个app不能占用太多CPU，内存，屏幕空间或者其他系统资源，它应该对于突然地打断以及来自其他app的声音反映良好，能快速顺滑地从后台来去自如，并且在后台运行时也表现得很靠谱。</p><p><b>Be prepared for interruptions, and be ready to  resume.</b> Your app can be interrupted at any time. When an interruption occurs, your app should save the current state quickly and precisely so people can seamlessly continue where they left off when they return. For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/iPhone/Conceptual/iPhoneOSProgrammingGuide/StrategiesforImplementingYourApp/StrategiesforImplementingYourApp.html%23//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40007072-CH5-SW2\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Preserving Your App’s Visual Appearance Across Launches</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/iPhone/Conceptual/iPhoneOSProgrammingGuide/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">App Programming Guide for iOS</a>.<br/></p><p>准备好被打断，准备好继续。您的app随时可能被打断。当打断发生时，您的app应该快速精确地保存当前状态，这样人们可以在返回时无缝从他们离开的地方继续。</p><p><b>Make sure your interface works with a double-high status bar.</b> Certain features, such as in-progress phone calls, audio recording, and tethering display an additional status bar at the top of the screen. In unprepared apps, this added height can cause layout problems by covering or pushing down other interface elements. Test your app with these features enabled to ensure that your interface responds appropriately and still looks great.</p><p>确认界面在出现双倍高度状态条时运行正常。某些功能，比如打电话，录音，分享热点会在屏幕最上面显示附加的状态条。在没准备好的app中，这个增加的高度可能会引起布局问题，遮挡或者将其他界面元素往下推。用这些功能测试您的app，让界面在这些状态下恰当回应并且仍然看起来很棒。</p><p><b>Pause activity that requires attention or active participation.</b> If your app is a game or a media-viewing app, for example, make sure people don’t miss anything when they switch to another app. When they switch back, let them continue as if they’d never left.<br/></p><p>暂停需要注意力或者主动参与的活动。比如，如果您的app是个游戏或者播放媒体的，确认人们在切换到其他app时没有错过任何东西。当他们切换回来，让他们像从没离开过一样继续。</p><p><b>Respond appropriately to external audio.</b> Occasionally, your app’s audio may be interrupted by audio from another app or the system itself. For example, an incoming phone call or a music playlist initiated by Siri may interrupt your app’s audio. When situations like these occur, your app’s response should meet people’s expectations. For primary audio interruptions, such as playing music, podcasts, or audiobooks, your app should pause its audio indefinitely. For shorter interruptions, such as GPS directional notifications, your app should temporarily lower its audio volume or pause its audio and resume when the interruption ends. For additional guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/interaction/audio/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Audio</a>.<br/></p><p>对于外部音频恰当反应。有时候，app音频会被其他app的音频或者系统本身打断。比如，来点或者Siri触发的音乐播放列表可能会打断app的音频。当这种情况发生时，app的反应要符合人的预期。对于基本的音频打断，比如播放音乐、podcast、有声书，app应该无限期停止音频。对于短暂的打断，比如GPS方位通知，app应该暂时调低音量或者暂停音频，然后当打断结束时继续。</p><p><b>Finish user-initiated tasks in the background.</b> When someone starts a task, they expect it to finish even if they switch away from your app. If your app is in the middle of performing a task that doesn’t need additional input, complete it in the background before suspending.</p><p>在后台结束用户发起的任务。当某人开始一个任务，他们期望即使从app切出也能完成。如果app正在进行一个不需要再输入的任务，在暂停之前在后台完成它。</p><p><b>Use notifications sparingly.</b> Your app can arrange for notifications to be sent at specific times, whether your app is suspended, running in the background, or not running at all. Notifications are fine for communicating important information, but avoid pestering people with too many. For example, don’t show a notification every time your app finishes a task in the background. Instead, let people check on tasks by returning to your app. For additional guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/features/notifications/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Notifications</a>.</p><p>For iPad-specific implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/WindowsViews/Conceptual/AdoptingMultitaskingOniPad/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Adopting Multitasking Enhancements on iPad</a>.</p><p>慎用通知。app可以安排在特定时候发通知，无论app暂停了、在后台运行或者根本没运行。通知对于交流重要信息很有用，但是不要用太多通知纠缠用户。例如，app不要每次一在后台完成个任务就发个通知。相反，要让用户回app查看任务。</p><p>iPad特定的详情，请查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/WindowsViews/Conceptual/AdoptingMultitaskingOniPad/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Adopting Multitasking Enhancements on iPad</a>.】</p><p><b>Notifications通知</b><br/></p><p>Apps can use notifications to provide timely and important information anytime, whether the device is locked or in use. For example, notifications may occur when a message has arrived, an event is about to occur, new data is available, or the status of something has changed. People see notifications on the lock screen, at the top of the screen while using the device, and in Notification Center, which is opened by swiping down from the top edge of the screen. Each notification includes the app name, a small app icon, and a message. Notifications may also be accompanied by a sound, and may cause a badge to appear or update on the corresponding app’s icon.</p><p>无论设备锁了没，app可以用通知提供及时的重要信息。例如，通知可以在消息来了、某个事件即将发生、新数据可以获得，或者某物的状态改变时出现。人们能在锁屏上看到通知，使用设备时在屏幕上方看到通知，在从屏幕顶端下拉出现的通知中心看到。每个通知包含app名称，一个小图标，并且可能引起一个提示数字出现或者相应app图标的更新。</p><p>The behavior of notifications is managed in Settings on an app-by-app basis. For any app that supports notifications, you can enable or disable the feature entirely. You can also enable visibility in Notification Center and on the lock screen, enable app icon badging, and choose one of these notification styles:</p><p>在系统设置中可以管理每个app的通知行为。对于每个支持通知的app，您可以开启或彻底关闭该功能。您也可以让通知在通知中心和锁屏上可见，允许app图标徽章，并且选择一种通知风格：</p><p><i>\t•\tBanner.</i> Appears at the top of the screen for a few seconds while the device is in use, then disappears.</p><p>横幅。当设备在使用中时，在屏幕顶端出现几秒钟，然后消失。</p><p><i>\t•\tAlert.</i> Appears at the top of the screen while the device is in use and stays there until manually dismissed.</p><p>提醒。当设备在使用中时，在屏幕顶端出现并停留，直到手动取消。</p><p>Tapping a notification when the device is unlocked, or swiping it to the side when the device is locked, dismisses the notification, removes it from Notification Center, opens the corresponding app, and shows related information. Tapping a new email notification on an unlocked device, for example, opens Mail and shows the new message.</p><p>当设备没锁时点击通知，或者当设备锁屏时滑动通知，关闭通知，从通知中心移除，打开对应的app，并且显示相关信息。例如，在没锁的设备上点击新邮件通知，打开Mail邮件然后显示新邮件。</p><p> On an unlocked device, swiping a notification up or letting it disappear dismisses the notification and may remove it from Notification Center.</p><p>Applying pressure to a notification using 3D Touch or, on an unlocked device, swiping a notification down, opens an expanded detail view. This view is customizable and can include up to four buttons for taking action. A to-do list app, for example, might deliver a task notification with a detail view that includes actions for deferring the task and marking it as complete. An Calendar event notification provides a Snooze action that briefly delays the event&#39;s alarm.</p><p>在没锁的设备上，将通知上划或者让它消失会关闭通知，而且将其从通知中心移除。在没锁设备上，使用3D Touch按压通知或者将通知下划，会打开一个扩展详情视图。这个视图可以定制，最多能包含四个动作按钮。例如，一个提醒事项app，可能推送一个任务通知，它的详情视图带有推迟任务和标记为已完成动作。一个日历事项通知提供推迟动作，能略略推迟事件闹钟。</p><p><b>TIP</b></p><p>Notifications can be local or remote. Local notifications originate and are delivered on the same device. A to-do list app might use local notifications to alert someone about an upcoming meeting or due date. Remote notifications, also called push notifications, come from a server. A multiplayer game might use remote notifications to let players know when it’s their move.</p><p>People must explicitly opt into receiving notifications from every app that supports them—they’re asked to do so the first time they use the app. If someone opts out, they can always visit Settings to opt in.</p><p>通知可能是本地的或远程的。本地通知在同一设备上产生并推送。一个提醒事项app会使用本地通知来提醒某人关于即将到来的会议或约会。远程通知，也叫做推送通知，来自于服务器。一个多人对战游戏会使用远程通知让玩家知道该他们走了。人们必须为每个支持通知功能的app明确选择接受通知，他们会在首次使用app时被要求这样做。如果有人拒绝，他们可以查看系统设置来打开通知。</p><p><b>Provide useful, informative notifications.</b> People enable notifications to get quick updates, so focus on providing information of value. Use complete sentences, sentence case, proper punctuation, and don’t truncate your message—the system does this automatically, if necessary. Avoid telling people to open your app, navigate to specific screens, tap specific buttons, and perform other tasks that are hard to remember once the notification is dismissed.</p><p>提供有用的有信息含量的通知。人们打开通知是为了获得快速更新，所以请专注于提供有价值的信息。使用完整的句子，首字母大写，恰当的时机，并且不要截短信息——如果有必要，系统会自动截短的。避免让用户打开app，到某个特定界面，点击特定按钮，或者做其他难记的任务，以防通知被错过。</p><p><b>Don’t send multiple notifications for the same thing, even if the user hasn&#39;t responded.</b> People attend to notifications at their convenience. If you send multiple notifications for the same thing, you fill up Notification Center, and users may turn off notifications from your app.</p><p>不要因为同一件事发好几个通知，即使用户没回应。人们趋向于随他们的意去查看通知。如果您因为同一个事发好几个通知，您的通知就会充满通知中心，用户就会把您app的通知关掉。</p><p><b>Don’t include your app name or icon.</b> The system automatically shows this information at the top of each notification.</p><p>不用在通知中包括app名称或者图标。系统会自动显示。</p><p><b>Use badging to supplement notifications, not to denote critical information.</b> Keep in mind that badging of your app can be turned off. If your app relies on badging to communicate important information, you run the risk of people missing it.</p><p>提示数字只是作为补充，不能说明重要信息。要记得app的提示数字是能关掉的，如果您依赖提示数字去传递重要信息，那人们很可能遗漏掉。</p><p><b>Keep badges up to date.</b> Update your app’s badge as soon as the corresponding information is read. You don’t want people to think there’s new information available, only to find that they’ve already seen it. Note that reducing a badge’s count to zero removes all related notifications from Notification Center.</p><p>提示数字要实时更新。相应信息阅读完毕就立刻更新提示数字。不要让人觉得还有可读信息，结果发现他们都读过了。注意提示数字降为0时，所有相关通知都会从通知中心删除。</p><p><b>Provide a sound to supplement your notifications.</b> Sound is a great way to get someone&#39;s attention when they’re not looking at the screen. A to-do list app might play an alert sound, for example, when it’s time to perform an important task. Your app can use a custom sound or a built-in alert sound for this. If you use a custom sound, make sure it’s short, distinctive, and professionally produced. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/NetworkingInternet/Conceptual/RemoteNotificationsPG/Chapters/IPhoneOSClientImp.html%23//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40008194-CH103-SW6\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Preparing Custom Alert Sounds</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/NetworkingInternet/Conceptual/RemoteNotificationsPG/Chapters/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Local and Remote Notification Programming Guide</a>. Keep in mind that people can optionally disable notification alert sounds. They can also enable a vibration that accompanies the sound—this must be manually enabled and can’t be enabled programmatically by your app.</p><p>用音效补充通知。当人们没看屏幕时，音效是引人注意的好方法。比如，一个提醒事项app可能发出提醒音效，当要做重要任务时。App可以使用自定义音效或者系统内置的音效。如果使用自定义音效，请确保它是短促，独特，经过专业制作的。详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/NetworkingInternet/Conceptual/RemoteNotificationsPG/Chapters/IPhoneOSClientImp.html%23//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40008194-CH103-SW6\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Preparing Custom Alert Sounds</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/NetworkingInternet/Conceptual/RemoteNotificationsPG/Chapters/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Local and Remote Notification Programming Guide</a>】要记得人们可以关掉通知提醒音效。他们也可以开启音效+振动，这必须是手动添加的，不能通过app自动开启。</p><p><b>Consider providing a detail view.</b> A notification detail view provides more information about a notification, as well as the ability to take immediate action without leaving the current context to open your app. This view should include useful information, be recognizable, and feel like a natural extension of your app. It can contain photos, videos, and other content, and can be dynamically updated while displayed. For example, a ridesharing app could display a map here that shows a car approaching your current location.</p><p>考虑提供详情视图。通知详情视图提供关于该通知的更多信息，以及不用离开当前情景去打开app就能立刻采取行动。这个视图应该包括有用的信息，具有辨识性，看起来像是app的自然延伸。它可以包括照片，视频，以及其他内容，并且在显示时可以动态更新。例如，一个共享乘车app可以显示一个地图，地图上显示车正在靠近您的当前位置。</p><p><b>Provide intuitive, beneficial actions.</b> A notification detail view can include up to four action buttons. These buttons should be for performing common, time-saving tasks that eliminate the need to open your app. Use short, title-case names that clearly describe the action results. A notification detail view can also display an onscreen keyboard for collecting information needed to take action. For example, a messaging app might let people respond directly from a new message notification.</p><p>提供直接的，有用的动作。通知详情视图可以包括最多四个动作按钮。这些按钮应该能实现常用的 节省时间的任务，减少打开app的需求。使用简短，首字母大写的名称来清晰描述动作结果。通知详情视图也可以在屏幕上显示键盘，以收集用于行动的信息。例如，短信app可能让人们直接在新短信通知里回复。</p><p><b>Avoid providing destructive actions.</b> Think carefully before providing destructive actions in a notification detail view. If you must provide them, make sure people have enough context to avoid unintended consequences. Actions identified as destructive appear in red.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/NetworkingInternet/Conceptual/RemoteNotificationsPG/Chapters/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Local and Remote Notification Programming Guide</a>.</p><p>避免提供破坏性动作。在通知详情视图中提供破坏性动作之前要慎重考虑。如果您必须提供他们，确保人们有足够的情景认知来避免意想不到的后果。破坏性动作要显示为红色。</p><p><b>Printing打印</b><br/></p><p> Your app can take advantage of the system’s built-in AirPrint technology to enable wireless printing of images, PDFs, and other content to compatible printers. While viewing printable content in an AirPrint-enabled app, people typically tap an action button in a navigation bar or toolbar and then tap a Print action to display a printer view. This view provides a list of available printers and any customizable options, such as the number of copies and page range, and provides a button to initiate printing.</p><p>App可以利用系统内置的AirPrint技术在兼容的打印机上实现无线打印图片、PDF及其他内容。当在可以使用AirPrint的app中浏览打印内容时，人们通常点击导航条上的动作按钮然后点击打印来显示打印视图。这个视图提供可用打印机列表以及个性化设置，例如打印数量，页数范围，并且提供开始打印的按钮。</p><p><b>Make printing discoverable.</b> Enable printing through the system-provided Action button if your app has a toolbar or navigation bar. Users are familiar with this button and use it to print in other apps. If your app doesn’t have a toolbar or navigation bar, design a custom print button instead.</p><p>让打印容易发现。如果app有工具条或者导航条，通过系统提供的动作按钮实现打印功能。用户对这个按钮很熟悉，在其他app中也用它来打印。如果app没有工具条或者导航条，那就设计一个个性化的打印按钮。</p><p><b>Enable printing only when it&#39;s possible to print.</b> If there’s nothing onscreen to print or no printers are available, don’t show a Print action when someone taps the Action button. If your app implements a custom print button, disable or hide it when printing isn’t possible.</p><p>只在能打印时允许打印功能。如果屏幕上什么都没有或者没有可用的打印机，当某人点击动作按钮时，不要显示打印动作。如果app用个性化的打印按钮，当不能打印时，让它不可用或者隐藏起来。</p><p><b>Provide printing options that add value.</b> Think about the options people might want to specify when they print your content. Consider options for selecting a page range and requesting multiple copies. Enable additional options, such as front and back printing, if it makes sense and the printer supports them.</p><p>提供有价值的打印选项。思考人们在打印时特殊考虑的事。考虑选择页面范围和多份打印的选项。如果有意义并且打印机支持，实现附加功能，例如双面打印。</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/2DDrawing/Conceptual/DrawingPrintingiOS/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Drawing and Printing Guide for iOS</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiprintinteractioncontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPrintInteractionController</a>.</p><p>详情请见【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/2DDrawing/Conceptual/DrawingPrintingiOS/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Drawing and Printing Guide for iOS</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiprintinteractioncontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPrintInteractionController</a>.】</p><p><b>Quick Look</b><br/></p><p>Within your app, Quick Look lets people preview Keynote, Numbers, Pages, and PDF documents, as well as images and other types of files, even if your app doesn&#39;t support those file formats. Mail uses Quick Look for viewing attachments. After downloading an attachment, Mail shows the attachment’s icon and file name within the message. Tapping the icon displays a preview of the attachment.</p><p>在app中，Quick Look让人们能预览Keynote，Numbers，Pages以及PDF文件，图片及其他文件类型，即使您的app不支持那些文件格式。邮件Mail使用Quick Look预览附件。下载附件之后，邮件Mail在邮件中显示附件的图标和文件名。点击图标显示附件预览。</p><p><b>Present previews appropriately for the current context.</b> On iPhone, if your app has a navigation bar, slide the preview into place like any other view in your app’s hierarchy. On iPads, or if your app doesn’t have its own navigation bar, open the preview in a full-screen modal view that includes a navigation bar. With both methods, the navigation bar includes a button for exiting Quick Look, as well as preview-specific buttons for performing actions such as sharing and markup. If your app includes a toolbar, any preview-specific buttons appear here instead of in the navigation bar.</p><p>为当前情景恰当地显示预览。在iPhone上，如果app有导航条，让预览像app阶层中的其他视图一样滑入显示。在iPad上，或者app没有导航条，用带有导航条的模态视图全屏显示预览。在这两种方式里，导航条包含一个用于离开Quick Look的按钮，还有一个用于实现预览中特定功能的按钮，比如分享和标记。如果app有工具条，任何预览特定功能按钮在此处出现，而不是在导航条上。</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/FileManagement/Conceptual/DocumentInteraction_TopicsForIOS/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Document Interaction Programming Topics for iOS</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/quicklook\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Quick Look</a>.</p><p><b>Siri</b><br/></p><p>Your app can integrate with Siri to perform certain tasks in response to spoken commands and questions from users.</p><p>App可以整合Siri来实现某种回应语音命令、回答用户问题的任务</p><ul><li><b>Audio and video calling apps.</b> Initiate calls and search the call history.</li><li><b>音频视屏电话</b><b>app</b><b>。</b>启动通话并且搜索通话记录。</li><li><b>Messaging apps.</b> Send messages and read received messages.</li><li><b>信息</b><b>app</b><b>。</b>发送信息，播报收到的信息。</li><li><b>Apps that offer payment services.</b> Send and request payments.</li><li><b>支付</b><b>app</b><b>。</b>发送支付请求。</li><li><b>Apps that manage photos.</b> Search for and display photos.</li><li><b>照片管理</b><b>app</b><b>。搜索和显示照片。</b></li><li><b>Apps that offer transportation services.</b> Book rides and provide ride status information.</li><li><b>提供交通服务的</b><b>app</b><b>。预定行程，提供行程状态信息。</b></li><li><b>Apps that offer fitness activities.</b> Start, pause, resume, end, and cancel workouts.</li><li><b>提供健身活动的</b><b>app</b><b>。</b>开始，暂停，继续，停止，取消健身。</li><li><b>Automotive vendors that integrate with CarPlay.</b>Change the car’s audio source, climate, defroster settings, seat temperature, and radio station.</li><li><b>整合</b><b>CarPlay</b><b>的汽车供应商。</b>改变汽车音源，空调，除霜设置，座椅温度，广播电台。</li></ul><br/><p>Siri handles the language processing and semantic analysis needed to turn spoken requests into actionable instructions your app can handle. Your app is responsible for defining the tasks it supports, validating the information received, providing information for Siri to present, and taking action.</p><p>Siri处理语言处理和语义分析，以将口语要求转化为app能处理的指令。App有责任定义支持的任务，验证收到的信息，为Siri提供显示的信息，并且做出行动。</p><p>While validating information, if something is missing or unclear, your app can instruct Siri to present choices, ask for confirmation, or request more information. At Siri’s discretion, certain tasks such as sending messages and making payments always require confirmation before the app can perform the task.<br/></p><p>验证信息时，如果某些事漏掉了或者不清楚，app可以让Siri显示选项，请求确认或者要求更多信息。处于谨慎，例如发送信息和支付之类的任务，在实时动作之前总是需要确认。</p><p>Information from your app’s response is spoken by Siri and appears in the Siri interface. If appropriate, your app can provide custom content for Siri to display. A fitness app, for example, might provide custom workout information.</p><p>从app获得的回应信息通过Siri之口说出并且显示在Siri界面上。如果合适，app可以为Siri提供定制内容。例如，一个健身app，可以提供定制的锻炼信息。</p><p><b>Strive for a voice-driven experience that doesn’t require touching or looking at the screen.</b> People don’t always look at the screen when using Siri. They may interact with Siri through a headset, through their car, or from across the room. To the extent possible, let users complete tasks without unlocking their phone.</p><p>争取创建不需要触控或者看屏幕的语音体验。人们在使用Siri时不会总看屏幕。他们可能通过耳机、通过车或者房间另一端与Siri交互。尽可能让用户不用解锁iPhone就能完成任务。</p><p><b>Respond quickly and minimize interaction.</b> People use Siri for convenience, so don&#39;t make them wait for a response. Your app should validate information and take action as quickly as possible after receiving a request. When clarification or additional information is needed, present efficient, focused choices that reduce the possibility of additional prompting.</p><p>快速回应，最少化交互步骤。人们为了方便才使用Siri，所有不要让他们等回应。App在收到请求之后应该尽快确认信息，采取信息。当需要确认或者附加信息时，呈现高效集中的选项，减少更多提示的可能。</p><p><b>Take people directly to content.</b> Transitions from Siri to your app should go directly to the expected destination. Don’t show intermediary screens or messages that get in the way or slow people down.</p><p>直接将人带到内容面签。从Siri过渡到app，应该直接到预期的终点。不要显示中间屏或者信息，那会阻碍使用，减慢操作。</p><p><b>Be relevant, accurate, and appropriate.</b> Your app’s response should always be relevant to the current request and should accurately reflect people’s expectations. Never include content that might be considered offensive or demeaning.</p><p>切题，准确，恰当。对于当前要求，app的回应应该总是切题的，并且应该准确反映人们的期望。用于不要包含可能被视作冒犯或者贬低的内容。</p><p><b>Default to the safest and least expensive option.</b> A response should never be deceiving or misrepresent information, especially when it has financial impact. For a purchase with multiple pricing levels, don’t default to the most expensive. At the point where a user is making a payment, don’t charge extra fees without informing them.</p><p>默认最安全最便宜的选项。回应永远不能是欺骗的歪曲的信息，特别涉及到钱的方面。比如有多个价格的购买行为，不要默认选择最贵的。当用户支付时，不要不通知就收其他费用。</p><p><b>Increase accuracy with custom vocabulary.</b> Your app can help Siri learn more about the actions your app performs by defining specific terms people might use in requests, such as contact names, photo tags, photo album names, ride options, and workout names. These terms should be nongeneric, unique to your app, and terms people might actually use when making a request. The vocabulary you provide should never include other app names, terms that are obviously connected with other apps, inappropriate language, or reserved phrases, such as “Hey Siri.” Note that any terms you define are used by Siri to help resolve requests, but aren’t guaranteed to be recognized.</p><p>通过自定义词语增加准确性。App可以通过定义人们在发出请求时特定的项目，例如联系人姓名，照片标签，相簿名字，行程选项，锻炼项目名字，帮助Siri了解更多app中实现的动作。这些项目应该是不通用的，只在您的app中使用的，人们发出指令时真的会用到的。您提供的词汇应该不是其他app的名字，或者明显与其他app有关的，不恰当的语言，或者预置短语，比如“Hi Siri”。注意，这些您定义的项目用于帮助Siri解决指令，但是不保证会被识别。</p><p><b>Provide example requests.</b> Provide Siri with example phrases to show in the guide that appears when you tap the Help button in the Siri interface. Use these phrases to teach people the easiest and most efficient way to use Siri with your app.</p><p>提供请求示例。给Siri提供示例短语，当您点击Siri界面上的帮助键时会显示出指南。通过这些短语，用最简单最有效的方式教人们学习如何在app中使用Siri。</p><p><b>Make sure your custom interface integrates well with Siri.</b> It’s fine to use your app’s colors, imagery, and other design elements to communicate your brand, but any custom interface elements should still feel like they belongs in Siri.</p><p>确认您的个性化界面与Siri整合得很好。使用您的app主题色，图片以及其他设计元素来传达您的品牌，这是好的。但是任何定制的界面元素得看起来仍然属于Siri。</p><p><b>Don’t include your app name or icon in your custom interface.</b> The system automatically shows this information.</p><p>在个性化界面中不要出现app名字或者图标。系统会自动显示这些信息。</p><p><b>Don’t advertise.</b> Your app’s Siri experience should never include advertisements, marketing, or in-app purchase sales pitches.</p><p>不要做广告。App的Siri体验永远不要包含广告，市场推广或者内购推销。</p><p><b>Don’t attempt to mimic or manipulate Siri.</b> Your app should never impersonate Siri, attempt to reproduce the functionality Siri provides, or provide a response that appears to come from Apple.</p><p>不要试图模仿或者操控Siri。您的app永远不要模仿Siri，试图复制Siri提供的功能，或者提供一个看起来好像来自Aple的回应。</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Intents/Conceptual/SiriIntegrationGuide/index.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">SiriKit Programming Guide</a>.</p>",
