            "content": "<p><b>Gestures</b></p><p>People interact with an iOS device by performing gestures on the touchscreen. These gestures elicit a close personal connection with content and enhance the sense of direct manipulation of onscreen objects. People generally expect the following standard gestures to work the same across the system and in every app.</p><p>人们通过在屏幕上使用手势与iOS设备交互。这些手势引出与内容个人紧密联系，并且加强对屏幕上物体的直接操作感。人们通常希望以下这些标准手势在整个系统以及每个app中都起到一样的效果。</p><p><b>Tap.</b> Activates a control or selects an item.<br/></p><p>点击。激活控件或者选中项目。</p><p><b>Drag.</b> Moves an element from side-to-side or drags an element across the screen.<br/></p><p>拖拽。将元素从一边移动到另一边或者在整个屏幕上拖拽元素。</p><p><b>Flick.</b> Scrolls or pans quickly.<br/></p><p>轻扫。滚动或者快速平移。</p><p><b>Swipe.</b> When performed with one finger, returns to the previous screen, reveals the hidden view in a split view controller, reveals the Delete button in a table-view row, or reveals actions in a peek. When performed with four fingers on an iPad, switches between apps.<br/></p><p>滑动。单指操作时，作用是返回上一屏，在分列视图中揭开被遮挡的视图，揭开列表视图中的删除键，或者揭开peek视图中的动作。在iPad上四指操作时，作用是在app间切换。</p><p><b>Double tap.</b> Zooms in and centers content or an image, or zooms out if already zoomed in.<br/></p><p>双击。放大并且显示内容或者图像的中心，如果已经放大了，则缩小。</p><p><b>Pinch.</b> Zooms in when pinching outward, zooms out when pinching inward.<br/></p><p>捏。向外捏时放大，向内捏时缩小。</p><p><b>Touch and hold.</b> When performed in editable or selectable text, displays a magnified view for cursor positioning. When performed in certain views, such as a collection view, enters a mode that allows items to be rearranged.<br/></p><p>点击并长按。当在可编辑或者可选择的文本中使用时，显示放大的光标位置。当在某种视图中使用时，比如集合试图，进入允许项目重新排列的模式。</p><p><b>Shake.</b> Initiates undo or redo.<br/></p><p>摇晃。触发撤销操作或者重做操作。</p><p><b>As a general rule, use standard gestures.</b> People are familiar with the standard gestures and don’t appreciate being forced to learn different ways to do the same thing. In games and other immersive apps, custom gestures can be a fun part of the experience. In other apps, it’s best to use standard gestures so extra effort isn’t needed to discover or remember them.<br/></p><p>总纲领是，使用标准手势。人们对标准手势很熟悉，不想学习用不同方式做同一件事。在游戏中或者其他沉浸式app，最好使用标准手势，这样就不用为了发现或者记住手势付出多余努力。</p><p><b>Don’t block systemwide gestures.</b> In addition to the standard gestures, some additional gestures invoke systemwide actions, such as revealing Control Center or Notification Center. People rely on these gestures to work in every app.</p><p>不要屏蔽系统手势。除了标准手势，有些手势引发系统内的动作，比如拉出控制中心或者通知中心。人们在每个app中都需要这些手势。</p><p><b>Avoid using standard gestures to perform nonstandard actions.</b> Unless your app is a game in active gameplay, redefining the meaning of standard gestures leads to confusion and complexity.</p><p>避免用标准手势实现非标准动作。除非app是游戏，重新定义标准手势的意义会导致困惑和复杂感。</p><p><b>Offer shortcut gestures to supplement, not replace, interface-based navigation and actions.</b> Whenever possible, offer a simple, visible way to navigate or perform an action, even if it means an extra tap or two. Many system apps include a navigation bar that provides a clear, tappable button back to the previous screen. But users can also navigate back by swiping from the side of the screen. On iPad, people can exit to the Home screen by pressing the Home button, or by using a four-finger pinching gesture.</p><p>提供快捷手势来补充，而非替代，界面导航和动作。可能的情况下，提供简洁、可视化的方式来导航或者实行动作，即使这意味着要多点击几下。很多系统app包含提供清晰、可点击的返回键的导航条。但是用户也可以通过从屏幕一段滑动到另一端来返回上一屏。在iPad上，人们可以通过按Home键回到主屏，或者用四指内收的手势。</p><p><b>Use multifinger gestures to enhance the experience of some apps.</b> Although gestures involving multiple fingers at once aren’t appropriate for every app, they can enrich the experience in some apps, such as games and drawing apps. For example, a game might include multiple onscreen controls, such as a joystick and firing buttons, that can be operated simultaneously.</p><p>用多指手势提高某些app的体验。尽管目前多指手势不适合所有app，他们还是可以丰富某些app的体验，比如游戏和绘画app。例如，游戏可能包含好几个屏幕上的控件，比如同时操作的摇杆和射击按钮。</p><p><b>Loading加载</b><br/></p><p>When content is loading, a blank or static screen can make it seem like your app is frozen, resulting in confusion and frustration, and potentially causing people to leave your app.</p><p>当加载内容时，空白屏或者静态屏可能让app看起来卡住了，导致用户感到困惑沮丧，并且很可能让人们退出app。</p><p><b>Make it clear when loading is occurring.</b> At minimum, show an activity spinner that denotes something is happening. Even better, display explicit progress so the user can gauge how long they’ll be waiting.<br/></p><p>当加载进行时，清楚地显示出来。至少显示一个活动加载菊花，表示事情正在发生。好一点的方式，清楚地显示进程，这样用户就能估计他们还要等多久。</p><p><b>Educate or entertain people to mask loading time.</b> Consider showing hints about gameplay, entertaining video sequences, or interesting placeholder graphics.</p><p>通过教点东西或者娱乐大家来伪装加载时间。考虑显示关于游戏的提示，娱乐视频或者有趣的替代图片。</p><p><b>Customize loading screens.</b> Although standard progress indicators are usually OK, they can sometimes feel out of context. Consider designing a more immersive experience through custom animations and elements that match the style of your app or game.<br/></p><p>个性化加载屏。尽管标准的进程显示器通常都是可以的，有时候他们可能看起来不符合情景。考虑通过定制与app或者游戏风格搭配的动画和元素设计完整的沉浸式体验。</p><p><b>Show content as soon as possible.</b> Don’t make people wait for content to load before seeing the screen they&#39;re expecting. Show the screen immediately, and use placeholder text, graphics, or animations to identify where content isn&#39;t available yet. Replace these placeholder elements as the content loads. Whenever possible, preload upcoming content in the background, such as while an animation is playing or the user is navigating a level or menu.</p><p>For additional guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/progress-indicators/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Progress Indicators</a>.</p><p>尽快显示内容。不要在人们看到他们期待的屏之前让他们等待内容加载。立刻显示，用展位文字、图片或者动画说明还不能看到内容的地方。当内容加载完就把这些展位元素取而代之。尽可能在后台预加载将要出现的内容，比如当动画播放时或者用户在某曾某菜单浏览时。</p><p><b>Modality模态</b><br/></p><p>Modality creates focus by preventing people from doing other things until they complete a task or dismiss a message or view. Action sheets, alerts, and activity views provide modal experiences. When a modal view appears onscreen, the user must make a choice by tapping a button or otherwise exiting the modal experience. Some apps implement modal views, such as while editing an event in Calendar or choosing a bookmark in Safari. A modal view can occupy the entire screen, an entire parent view, such as a popover, or a portion of the screen. A modal view typically includes completion and cancel buttons that exit the view.</p><p>模态通过阻止人们做其他事 直到他们完成任务，或者撤销一个消息或者视图来创造焦点。上拉菜单，警告，活动试图提供模态体验。当模态视图出现在屏幕上，用户必须通过点击按钮作出决定或者离开模态体验。某些app实践模态试图，例如当在日历中编辑事件或者在Safari中选择书签。模态视图可以占据整个屏幕，整个父视图，比如一个弹窗或者屏幕的一部分。模态试图通常包括完成和取消按钮来离开视图。</p><p><b>Minimize the use of modality.</b> Generally, people prefer to interact with apps in nonlinear ways. Consider creating a modal context only when it’s critical to get someone’s attention, when a task must be completed or abandoned to continue using the app, or to save important data.</p><p>尽量少用模态。通常人们更喜欢通过非线性的方式与app交互。只有在必须引人注意时创建模态文本，当为了继续使用app必须完成或者放弃一个任务，或者保存重要数据。</p><p><b>Provide an obvious and safe way to exit a modal task.</b> Make sure people always know the outcome of their action when they dismiss a modal view.<br/></p><p>提供显眼安全的方式以离开模态任务。当他们离开模态视图时，确认人们总是知道他们行动的结果。</p><p><b>Keep modal tasks simple, short, and narrowly focused.</b> Don’t create an app within your app. If a modal task is too complex, people can lose sight of the task they suspended when they entered the modal context. Be especially wary of creating modal tasks that involve a hierarchy of views because users can get lost and forget how to retrace their steps. If a modal task must contain subviews, provide a single path through the hierarchy and a clear path to completion. Avoid using Done buttons for things other than completing the task.</p><p>保持模态任务简单，简短，焦点集中。不要做成嵌套app。如果模态任务太复杂，在他们进入模态文本时，人们可能忽视他们暂停的任务。特别注意创建包含一系列层级视图的模态任务，因为用户可能会迷路并且忘记如何回溯步骤。如果模态任务必须包含子视图，在层级中提供单行线和清晰的完成路线。避免使用Done按钮，除非已经完成任务。</p><p><b>Display a title that identifies a task, if appropriate.</b> You might also provide text in other portions of the view that more fully describes the task or provides guidance.</p><p>如果合适，显示表示任务的标题。您也可以在视图的其他位置提供更完整描述任务或者提供指南的文本。</p><p><b>Reserve alerts for delivering essential—and ideally actionable—information.</b> An alert interrupts the experience and requires a tap to dismiss, so it’s important for people to feel that the intrusion is warranted. To learn more, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/alerts/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Alerts</a>.</p><p>为重要的，最好是可操作的信息保留警告。警报会打断体验，并且要求点击以离开，所以对人们来说，感到入侵是合理的是很重要的。详情请查看【Alerts】</p><p><b>Respect notification preferences.</b> In Settings, people specify how they want to receive notifications from your app. Abide by these preferences so they aren’t tempted to turn off your app’s notifications entirely.</p><p>尊重通知偏好。在设置中，人们指定了他们想以何种方式从您的app收到通知。按照这些偏好来做，这样他们就不会试图彻底关掉app的通知。</p><p><b>Don’t display a modal view above a popover.</b> With the possible exception of an alert, nothing should appear over a popover. In rare cases when you need to present a modal view after action is taken in a popover, close the popover before displaying the modal view.</p><p>不要在弹窗上显示模态试图。在可能的警报例外中，任何东西都不应该在弹窗上层出现。在少数情况下，当您需要在弹窗中采取行动之后呈现一个模态视图，在显示模态视图之前关掉弹窗。</p><p><b>Coordinate modal view appearance with your app.</b> A modal view may include a navigation bar, for example. When this is the case, use the same appearance as the navigation bar in your app.</p><p>让模态视图的外观跟app相协调。比如，模态视图可能包含导航条。在这种情况下，使用跟app中导航条一样的外观风格。</p><p><b>Choose an appropriate modal view style.</b><b>You can use any of these styles:</b><br/></p><p>选择恰当的模态视图。您可以使用任何风格：</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-55f7c1cb94f11bff25b7c8abe8111ee9_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"334\" data-rawheight=\"256\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"334\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;334&#39; height=&#39;256&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"334\" data-rawheight=\"256\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"334\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-55f7c1cb94f11bff25b7c8abe8111ee9_b.png\"/></figure><p><b>Full screen.</b> Covers the entire screen. Use for a potentially complex task that can be completed within the context of the modal view.</p><p>全屏。覆盖全屏。用于在模态视图情景中能完成的潜在的复杂任务。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a63f10d27c4021ee939bf6c1cfc0d795_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"334\" data-rawheight=\"256\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"334\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;334&#39; height=&#39;256&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"334\" data-rawheight=\"256\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"334\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic2.zhimg.com/v2-a63f10d27c4021ee939bf6c1cfc0d795_b.png\"/></figure><p><b>Page sheet.</b> Partially covers the underlying content on larger devices held in landscape orientation. All uncovered areas are dimmed to prevent interaction with them. Covers the entire screen on smaller devices and in portrait orientation. Use for a potentially complex task that can be completed within the context of the modal view.</p><p>页表。在横向视图的大设备上挡住一部分底层内容。所有没被覆盖的区域变暗以防止与之交互。在纵向视图的小设备覆盖整个屏幕。用于在模态视图情景中能完成的潜在的复杂任务。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d55bba4c46ce14437d89e7dd50934308_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"334\" data-rawheight=\"256\" class=\"content_image\" width=\"334\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;334&#39; height=&#39;256&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"334\" data-rawheight=\"256\" class=\"content_image lazy\" width=\"334\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-d55bba4c46ce14437d89e7dd50934308_b.png\"/></figure><p><b>Form sheet.</b> Appears centered on screen, but may be repositioned if a keyboard is visible. All uncovered areas are dimmed to prevent interaction with them. May cover the entire screen on smaller devices. Use for gathering information.<br/></p><p>格式表。在屏幕中心出现，但是当键盘出现时会重新安排位置。所有没被覆盖的区域变暗以防止与之交互。在小设备上可能覆盖整个屏幕。用于收集信息。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-65ade3a462ff0b6ad8f5473d3a7710fa_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"740\" data-rawheight=\"256\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"740\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-65ade3a462ff0b6ad8f5473d3a7710fa_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;740&#39; height=&#39;256&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"740\" data-rawheight=\"256\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"740\" data-original=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-65ade3a462ff0b6ad8f5473d3a7710fa_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic3.zhimg.com/v2-65ade3a462ff0b6ad8f5473d3a7710fa_b.png\"/></figure><p><b>Current context.</b> Appears at the same size as its parent view. Use for displaying modal content within a split view pane, popover, or other view that is not full-screen.</p><p>当前情景。和父视图一样大小。用于在spilt view中显示模态内容，或者其他不适全屏的内容。</p><p><b>Choose an appropriate transition style for revealing a modal view.</b> Use a transition style that coordinates with your app and enhances the awareness of the temporary context shift. The default transition vertically slides the modal view up from the bottom of the screen and back down once dismissed. The flip-style transition appears to flip a view horizontally to reveal the modal view. Visually, the modal view looks like the back of the current view. It flips back once dismissed. Use consistent modal transition styles throughout your app.</p><p>For modal view implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiviewcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIViewController</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uipresentationcontroller\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIPresentationController</a>.</p><p>为露出模态视图选择一个恰当的过渡方式。使用与app相协调的过渡风格，并且加强临时情景切换的意识。默认过渡方式是模态视图从屏幕底部垂直滑上来，当离开时再滑下去。翻转过渡方式看起来是水平方向翻转视图来露出模态视图。视觉上，这个模态视图看起来像在当前视图的背面。当离开时，它就翻转回去了。在整个app中使用一致的模态过渡方式。</p><p><b>Navigation导航</b><br/></p><p>People tend to be unaware of an app’s navigation until it doesn’t meet their expectations. Your job is to implement navigation in a way that supports the structure and purpose of your app without calling attention to itself. Navigation should feel natural and familiar, and shouldn’t dominate the interface or draw focus away from content. In iOS, there are three main styles of navigation.</p><p>人们倾向于直到不符合他们的预期时才注意到app导航。您的工作是不引人注意地，通过支持app结构和目的的方式实践导航。导航应该让人感觉自然而熟悉，不应该支配界面或者将焦点从内容拿走。在iOS中，有三种主要的导航方式。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-370438eff7ff4a9434afd531ea81ee6c_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"630\" data-rawheight=\"438\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"630\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-370438eff7ff4a9434afd531ea81ee6c_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;630&#39; height=&#39;438&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"630\" data-rawheight=\"438\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"630\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-370438eff7ff4a9434afd531ea81ee6c_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-370438eff7ff4a9434afd531ea81ee6c_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p><b>Hierarchical navigation.</b> Make one choice per screen until you reach a destination. To go to another destination, you must retrace your steps or start over from the beginning and make different choices. Settings and Mail use this navigation style.</p><p>分层导航。每屏做出一个选择，直到到达目的地。要去另一个目的地，您必须回溯步骤或者从头开始，做出不同的选择。设置和邮件使用了这种导航方式。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ac06815fba0e5dc99413dc9fcb0f0390_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"630\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"630\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ac06815fba0e5dc99413dc9fcb0f0390_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;630&#39; height=&#39;202&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"630\" data-rawheight=\"202\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"630\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ac06815fba0e5dc99413dc9fcb0f0390_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-ac06815fba0e5dc99413dc9fcb0f0390_b.png\"/></figure>Flat navigation.</b> Switch between multiple content categories. Music and App Store use this navigation style.</p><p>扁平导航。在不同的内容分类之间切换。音乐和app store使用了这种导航方式。</p><p><b><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9dba74999b80462fdce6c6d40d14bb1f_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9dba74999b80462fdce6c6d40d14bb1f_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1200&#39; height=&#39;300&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"1200\" data-rawheight=\"300\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1200\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9dba74999b80462fdce6c6d40d14bb1f_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-9dba74999b80462fdce6c6d40d14bb1f_b.png\"/></figure>Content-driven or experience-driven navigation.</b> Move freely through content, or the content itself defines the navigation. Games, books, and other immersive apps generally use this navigation style.</p><p>内容驱动或者体验驱动的导航。在内容之间自由移动，或者内容本身定义了导航。游戏，书，或者其他沉浸式app大多采用这种方式。</p><p> Some apps combine multiple navigation styles. For example, an app that uses flat navigation may implement hierarchical navigation within each category.</p><p>有些app结合了多种导航方式。例如，一个使用扁平导航的app可能在每个分类中采用了分层导航。</p><p><b>Always provide a clear path.</b> People should always know where they are in your app and how to get to their next destination. Regardless of navigation style, it’s essential that the path through content is logical, predictable, and easy to follow. In general, give people one path to each screen. If they need to see a screen in multiple contexts, consider using an action sheet, alert, popover, or modal view. To learn more, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/action-sheets/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Action Sheets</a>, <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/alerts/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Alerts</a>, <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/popovers/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Popovers</a>, and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/interaction/modality/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Modality</a>.</p><p>总是提供清晰的路线。人们应该一直知道他们在app的哪个位置并且如何到达下一个目的地。除了导航方式，内容之间的路径富有逻辑性，可预见，容易跟随是很重要的。总的来说，每屏都有一个路线。如果他们要在多种情景下看到一屏，考虑使用上拉菜单、警告、弹窗或者模态视图。</p><p><b>Design an information structure that makes it fast and easy to get to content.</b> Organize your information structure in a way that requires a minimum number of taps, swipes, and screens.</p><p>设计能快速建议到达内容的信息结构。用需要最少点击次数、滑动次数、屏数的方式组织信息结构。</p><p><b>Use touch gestures to create fluidity.</b> Make it easy to move through your interface with minimum friction. For example, you could let people swipe from the side of the screen to return to the previous screen.</p><p>使用触摸手势创造流畅体验。用最少的摩擦来视界面之间的移动更加容易。例如，您可以让人们从屏幕一端滑到另一端来返回上一屏。</p><p><b>Use standard navigation components.</b> Whenever possible, use standard navigation controls such as page controls, tab bars, segmented controls, table views, collection views, and split views. Users are already familiar with these controls, and will intuitively know how to get around your app.</p><p>使用标准导航组件。尽可能使用标准导航控件，例如页面控件，标签栏，分区控件，列表视图，集合视图，分栏视图。用户已经熟悉这些控件，直接就知道该如何在app中走动。</p><p><b>Use a navigation bar to traverse a hierarchy of data.</b> The navigation bar’s title can show the current position in the hierarchy, and the back button makes it easy to return to the previous location. For specific guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-bars/navigation-bars/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Navigation Bars</a>.</p><p>使用导航栏来遍历数据层级。导航条标题可以显示在层级中当前的位置，返回按钮让返回上一位置更容易。</p><p><b>Use a tab bar to present peer categories of content or functionality.</b> A tab bar lets people quickly and easily switch between categories, regardless of the current location. For specific guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-bars/tab-bars/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Tab Bars</a>.</p><p>使用标签栏来展示内容或功能的同级分类。标签栏让人们快速容易地在分类之间切换，不管现在位置是哪。</p><p><b>Use a page control when you have multiple pages of the same type of content.</b> A page control clearly communicates the number of pages available and which one is currently active. The Weather app uses a page control to show location-specific weather pages. For specific guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/page-controls/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Page Controls</a>.</p><p>当有多个同类内容的页面时，使用页面控件（就是好几个小点那种）。页面控件清晰地传达可达的页面数量以及哪一页是当前页面。天气app使用页面控件显示各地天气。</p><p><b>TIP</b></p><p>Segmented controls and toolbars don’t enable navigation. Use a segmented control to organize information into different categories. Use a toolbar to provide controls for interacting with the current context. For additional information on these types of elements, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/segmented-controls/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Segmented Controls</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-bars/toolbars/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Toolbars</a>.</p><p>分区控件和工具条不能导航。使用分区控件来组织不同分类的信息。使用工具条来提供与当前情景交互的控件。</p><p><b>Requesting Permission请求允许</b><br/></p><p>Users must grant permission for an app to access personal information, including the current location, calendar, contact information, reminders, and photos. Although people appreciate the convenience of using an app that has access to this information, they also expect to have control over their private data. For example, people like being able to automatically tag photos with their physical location or find nearby friends, but they also want the option to disable such features.</p><p>app必须经过用户允许才能获得个人信息，包括当前位置，日历，联系人信息，提醒，照片。尽管人们喜欢获取这类信息的app带来的便利，人们喜欢自动地理位置标签照片或者找到附近的朋友，但是他们也希望有选项能关掉这类功能。</p><p><b>Request personal data only when your app clearly needs it.</b> It’s natural to be suspicious of a request for personal information, especially if there’s no obvious need for it. Make sure permission requests occur only when people are using features that clearly need personal data. For example, an app might only request access to the current location when activating a location tracking feature.</p><p>只有在app明明白白需要个人信息时才发出请求。对于个人信息的请求表示怀疑是很自然的事，特别是没有显而易见的需求时。确认允许请求只发生在人们在使用明确需要个人数据的功能特性时。例如，app可能只会在启动位置追踪特性时发出获取当前位置的请求。</p><p><b>Explain why your app needs the information if it’s not obvious.</b> You can add custom text to the system-provided permission request alert. Make the text specific and polite, so people don’t feel pressured. Keep the text short, and use sentence case. There’s no need to include your app name. The system already identifies your app as the one making the request.</p><p>如果理由不那么明显，解释清楚为什么app需要这些信息。您可以添加定制文字给系统提供的许可请求警报。文字要具体而且礼貌，这样人们就不会感到压力。这段文字要短，而且使用句首字母大写。不必包含app的名字。系统已经标记了是这个app发出了请求。</p><p><b>Request permission at launch only when necessary for your app to function.</b> Users won’t be bothered by this request if it’s obvious that your app depends on their personal information to operate.</p><p>只在必要时为了app功能，在启动时就请求允许。如果这个app显然需要个人信息才能运行，用户不会觉得被这种请求打扰了。</p><p><b>Don’t request location information unnecessarily.</b> Before accessing location information, check the system to see whether Location Services is enabled. With this knowledge, you can delay the alert until a feature truly requires it, or perhaps avoid the alert altogether.</p><p>To learn how to implement location features, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/LocationAwarenessPG/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Location and Maps Programming Guide</a>.</p><p>不在不必要时要求位置信息。在获取位置信息之前，检查系统看看定位服务是否开启。知道这个情况之后，您可以推迟警告，直到某个功能真正需要时，或者也不要警告了。</p><p><b>Settings设置</b></p><p>Some apps may need to provide a way to make setup or configuration choices, but most apps can avoid or delay doing so. Successful apps work well for most people right away, while also offering some convenient ways to adjust the experience. When you design your app to function the way most people expect, you decrease the need for settings.</p><p>有些app可能需要提供设置或者配置选项的方式，但是大多数app可以避免或者推迟设置。成功的app在大多数人那都能立刻良好运行，同时也提供一些方便的方式来调整体验。当您为大多数人期待的那样设计app的工作方式，您就减少了设置的需求。</p><p><b>Infer what you can from the system.</b> If you need information about the user, device, or environment, query the system for it whenever possible instead of asking the user. For example, instead of asking someone to enter their zip code so you can present local options, ask permission to use their current location.<br/></p><p>从系统中推测您能获取什么。如果您需要关于用户、设备或者环境的信息，尽量向系统发出请求而不是问用户。例如，请求使用用户当前位置，而不是让他们输入邮编。</p><p><b>Thoughtfully prioritize configuration options within your app.</b> Your app’s main screen is a good place for options that are essential or that change frequently. Secondary screens are better for options that change only occasionally.</p><p>对app内的配置选项优先级深思熟虑。对于主要的选项或者经常改变的选项来说，app的首屏是个好位置。对于偶尔改变的选项来说二级屏更好些。</p><p><b>Provide shortcuts to Settings when appropriate.</b> If your app includes text that directs users to Settings, such as “Go to Settings &gt; MyApp &gt; Privacy &gt; Location Services,” provide a button that opens that location automatically. To learn how to implement this behavior, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiapplication/1658897-settings_launch_url\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Settings Launch URL</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/uikit/uiapplication\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">UIApplication</a>.<br/></p><p>适时提供到系统设置的捷径。如果app包括指引用户去系统设置的文本，例如 “Go to Settings &gt; MyApp &gt; Privacy &gt; Location Services”，提供一个能自动打开该位置的按钮。</p><p><b>Expose infrequently changed   configuration options in Settings.</b> The Settings app is a central location for making configuration changes throughout the system, but people must leave your app to get there. It’s far more convenient to adjust settings directly within your app. If you must provide settings that rarely require change, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/UserDefaults/Preferences/Preferences.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Implementing an iOS Settings Bundle</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/UserDefaults/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Preferences and Settings Programming Guide</a> for implementation details.<br/></p><p>在系统设置里显示不常用的配置选项。系统设置是整个系统中配置选项的中心，但是人们必须得离开app才能到那。还是直接在app内调整设置容易得多。如果您必须提供一些很少需要的设置，详情查看【<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/UserDefaults/Preferences/Preferences.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Implementing an iOS Settings Bundle</a> in <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/UserDefaults/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Preferences and Settings Programming Guide</a>】</p><p><b>Terminology术语</b><br/></p><p>Every word in your app is part of a conversation with your users. Use this conversation to help them feel comfortable in your app.</p><p>app中的每个字都是您和用户的对话。用好这种对话方式，帮助用户在app感觉舒适。</p><p><b>Use familiar, understandable words and phrases.</b> Technology can be intimidating. Avoid acronyms and technical jargon that people might not understand. Use what you know about your audience to determine whether certain words or phrases are appropriate. In general, apps that appeal to everyone should steer clear of highly technical language. Such language may be appropriate in apps that target a more advanced or technical crowd.</p><p>使用熟悉的，可理解的话语。科技可能看上去很吓人。避免使用人们可能不理解的缩写和科技行话。使用您对用户的了解，来决定某些话语是否恰当。总的来说，面向大众的app应该避免高科技词汇。此类语言可能在面向更先进更高科技的群体时比较合适。</p><p><b>Keep interface text clear and concise.</b> People absorb short, direct text quickly and easily and don’t appreciate being forced to read long passages to accomplish a task. Identify the most important information, express it succinctly, and present it prominently so people don’t have to read too much to find what they’re looking for or figure out what to do next.<br/></p><p>保持界面文本清晰准确。人们能快速容易地理解简短直接的文本，并且不喜欢为了完成任务被迫读一大段文字。辨认出最重要的信息，简要地解释，并且明显的展示出来，这样人们就不用读好多文字来找要找的东西或者找出接下来该做什么。</p><p><b>Avoid language that might sound patronizing.</b> Avoid <i>we</i>, <i>our</i>, <i>me</i>, and <i>my</i> (for example &#34;our tutorial&#34; and &#34;my workouts&#34;). They&#39;re sometimes interpreted as insulting or patronizing.<br/></p><p>避免听起来高人一等的话语。避免我们，我们的，我，我的（例如我们的教程或者我的作品）这些话有时候听起来高人一等或者有侮辱意味。</p><p><b>Strive for an informal, friendly tone.</b> An informal, approachable style echoes the way you speak with people over lunch. Use contractions occasionally, and <i>you</i> and <i>your</i> to address the user directly.</p><p>尽量使用非正式的友好的语气。非正式的、和蔼可亲的方式就是像您跟人吃午饭聊天一样。偶尔使用缩写，使用您和您的指代用户。</p><p><b>Be careful when using humor.</b> Remember that people are likely to read the text in your interface many times, and what might seem clever at first can become irritating over time. Also remember that humor in one culture doesn&#39;t necessarily translate well to other cultures.</p><p>表现幽默时要谨慎。要记得，人们可能要读很多遍界面上的文字，一开始看起来聪明有趣的内容，看多了可能就觉得有冒犯性。还要记得，一种文化中的幽默在其他文化中可能不会被转译得很好。</p><p><b>Use relevant and consistent language and imagery.</b> Always make sure guidance is appropriate for the current context. If someone’s using an iPad, for example, don’t show iPhone tips or graphics. Use language that’s consistent with the platform. You tap, flick, swipe, pinch, and drag content on the touchscreen. You press physical buttons and content that responds to 3D Touch. You rotate and shake the device.</p><p>使用相关的一致的语言和图像。一直确保指南对当前的情景是恰当的。例如，如果某人使用iPad，不要显示iPhone提示或者图片。使用与平台一致的语言。对于触摸屏上的内容的操作用“ tap, flick, swipe, pinch, and drag ”等词，对于物理按键和对于3D Touch有反应的内容用“press”，对于设备用“rotate和shake”</p><p><b>Refer to dates accurately.</b> It’s appropriate to use friendly terms like <i>today</i> and <i>tomorrow</i>, but these terms can be confusing or inaccurate if you don’t account for the current locale. Consider an event that starts just before midnight. In one time zone, the event may start today. In another time zone, the same event may have started yesterday. Generally, dates should reflect the time zone of the person viewing the event. However, in some cases, such as in a flight tracking app, it may be clearer to explicitly show the start date and time zone where the flight originates.<br/></p><p>准确描述日期。使用“今天”“明天”是恰当友好的，但是如果您不了解当前地点时，这些话听起来就是令人困惑、不准确的。请考虑一个事件正好在午夜之前开始。在一个时区，这个事件可能在今天开始。在另一个时区，同个事件可能昨天就开始了。总的来说，日期应该反映查看时间的人的时区。然而，在某些情况下，比如一个飞行追踪app，明确显示航班出发地的开始日期和时区会更清晰一些。</p><p><b>Identify interactive elements appropriately.</b> People should be able to tell at a glance what an element does. When labeling buttons and other interactive elements, use action verbs, such as Connect, Send, and Add.</p><p>恰当地辨识交互元素。人们应该一眼就认出一个元素是干嘛的。当给按钮及其他交互元素加文字标签时，使用动词，比如连接，发送和添加。</p><p><b>Undo and Redo撤销和重做</b><br/></p><p>Many apps allow people to shake the device to undo and redo certain operations, such as typing or deleting. When initiated in this manner, an alert asks the user to confirm or cancel the undo or redo operation.</p><p>许多app允许人们摇晃设备来撤销或者重做某个操作，例如输入或者删除。当触发这个动作时，应该有个警报问用户确认或者取消这个撤销\\重做操作。</p><p><b>Briefly and precisely describe the operation to be undone or redone.</b> The undo and redo alert title automatically includes a prefix of “Undo ” or “Redo ” (including the trailing space). You need to provide an additional word or two that describe what’s being undone or redone, to appear after this prefix. For example, you might create alert titles such as “Undo Name” or “Redo Address Change.”</p><p>简洁精确地描述这个撤销\\重做操作。撤销\\重做警报标题自动包括一个“撤销\\重做”前缀。您需要提供另外的短语来描述到底是撤销\\重做什么，放在这个前缀之后。例如，您可以创建警报标题，像“撤销名字”或者“重做地址修改”</p><p><b>If you use the shake gesture for undo and redo, don’t use it for other actions.</b> Although you can programmatically give multiple meanings to the shake gesture, you run the risk of confusing people and making your app unpredictable.</p><p>如果您给撤销\\重做操作使用摇晃手势，不要给其他的动作使用了。尽管在程序上您可以给摇晃手势不同的意义，但是您就运行了让人迷惑和让app不可以聊得风险。</p><p><b>Provide undo and redo buttons sparingly.</b> It’s confusing when apps provide multiple ways to perform the same task. If your app truly warrants dedicated undo and redo buttons, use the standard system-provided icons and put them in an expected location, such as a navigation bar.</p><p>保守慎重地提供撤销\\重做按钮。如果app提供多种方式实现同一任务是很令人迷惑的。如果app真的需要撤销\\重做按钮，使用系统提供的标准图标，把他们放在预定的位置，例如导航条那样。</p><p><b>Perform undo and redo operations in the current context only.</b> Undo and redo should have a clear and immediate effect on the current context, not an earlier one.</p><p>For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Cocoa/Conceptual/UndoArchitecture/UndoArchitecture.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Undo Architecture</a>.</p><p>只在当前情景下使用撤销\\重做操作。撤销\\重做操作应该针对当前情景清晰迅速反应，而不是对之前的。</p>",

            "content": "<h2><b>3D Touch</b></h2><p>3D Touch adds an additional dimension to\ntouch-based interaction. On supported devices, people can access additional\nfunctionality by applying varying levels of pressure to the touchscreen. Apps\ncan respond by displaying a menu, showing additional content, or playing an\nanimation. People don’t need to learn new gestures to interact with 3D Touch. They\nquickly discover the additional interactive dimension when they press lightly\non the screen and get a response.</p><p>3D Touch给基于触摸的交互增添了一个维度。在支持该技术的设备上，人们可以通过给触摸屏施加不同级别的压力来实现附加功能。App会用显示菜单、展示附加内容或者播放动画来做出反应。人们不必学习用3D Touch交互的新手势。当他们在屏幕上轻轻按压并且获得回应时，他们会很快发现这个额外的交互维度。</p><h3>Home Screen Interaction</h3><p>On the Home screen, pressing the icon\nof an app that supports 3D Touch displays an action view. This view lets you\nquickly perform common app-specific tasks and see interesting information.\nCalendar, for example, provides a shortcut for creating an event. It also shows\nthe next event on your schedule. For design guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/home-screen-actions/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Home Screen Actions</a>and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/widgets/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Widgets</a>.</p><p><b>主屏交互</b></p><p>在主屏上，按压一个支持3D Touch的app icon会显示一个action\nview。这个视图能令您很快实行常见的app特有任务并且看到有趣的信息。比如说，Calendar（日历），提供创建新事件的快捷方式。它也会展示时间表下一个事件。</p><h3>Peek and Pop</h3><p>A peek lets\npeople use 3D Touch to preview an item, such as a page, link, or file, in a\nview that appears temporarily above the current context. To peek\nat an item that supports this functionality, apply a little pressure to the\nitem with your finger. Simply lift your finger to exit the peek. To open the\nitem and see more detail, press a little harder until the item pops and fills\nthe screen. In some peek views, you can swipe up to reveal related action\nbuttons. For example, while peeking at a link in Safari, you can swipe up to\nreveal buttons for opening the link in the background, adding the link to your\nreading list, and copying the link.</p><p><b>Peek and Pop</b></p><p>人们用3D Touch在一个临时出现在当前语境上方的视图里，预览一个项目，例如一个页面，一个连接或者文件。戳一个支持该功能的项目时，指尖用点力气按压该项目。只要抬起手指就能结束动作。为了开启该项目查看更多细节，请更用力按压直到该项目弹出并且充满屏幕。在一些Peek视图中，您可以向上滑来露出相关的动作按钮。例如，当戳Safari中的一个链接时，您可以向上滑来露出用于在后台打开连接、将链接添加到阅读列表、拷贝链接的按钮。</p><p><strong>Use peeking to provide live, content-rich previews.</strong>Ideally, peeking gives enough information about an item to\naugment the current task, or helps you decide whether to fully engage the item.\nFor example, preview a link in a Mail message before deciding to open it in\nSafari or share it with friends. Peeking is often used in tables to view\ndetailed row information before the row is selected.</p><p><i>使用戳来提供生动的内容丰富的预览。</i>理想状态下，戳提供关于一个项目的足够信息来增强当前任务，或帮助您决定是否要彻底投入这个项目。例如，在邮件消息中预览链接，然后决定在Safari中打开它或与朋友分享。\n在选择行之前，经常在表中使用Peek查看详细的行信息。</p><p><b>Design big-enough peek views.</b> Design\na peek viewthat&#39;s large enough so that fingers don’t obscure its content. Make\nthe peek detailed enough for people to decide whether to press a little deeper\nto fully open (pop) the item.</p><p><i>设计足够大的</i><i>Peek</i><i>视图。</i>设计一个足够大的peek视图，这样手指就不会遮挡住内容。让peek视图足够详细，使人们决定是否要再用力按压来完全打开该项目。</p><p><b>Adopt Peek and Pop consistently.</b> If you support Peek and Pop in some places but not\nothers, people won’t know where they can use the feature and may think there’s\na problem with your app or their device.</p><p><i>使用</i><i>Peek</i><i>和</i><i>Pop</i><i>时注意一致性。</i>如果您有的地方地方支持PeekPop，有的地方又不支持，人们就不知道他们在哪能使用这个功能，会觉得您的app或者设备有问题。</p><p><b>Allow every peek to be popped.</b> Even\nthough peeking should give people most of the information they need, always let\nthem transition to the pop if they decide to switch away from the current task\nand focus on the item. Popping should show the same thing as tapping the item.</p><p><i>同时采用</i><i>Peek</i><i>和</i><i>Pop</i><i>。</i>即使Peek已经给人们大多数他们需要的信息，如果他们决定要从当前任务切换出来并且聚焦到这个项目时，还是要让他们过渡到pop。Pop应该给他们展现点击时一样的内容。</p><p><b>Avoid displaying button-like\nelements in a peek view.</b> If a user\nlifts a finger to tap an element that looks like a button, the peek disappears.</p><p><i>避免在</i><i>Peek</i><i>视图中显示按钮一类的元素。</i>如果用户抬起手指去点击按钮之类的元素，peek视图就消失了。</p><p><strong>Don’t enable peeking and an edit menu for the same item.</strong> It\ncan be confusing to users and hard for the system to detect intent when both\nfeatures are enabled for one item. For additional guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-controls/edit-menus/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Edit\nMenus</a>.</p><p><i>不要在同一个项目中使用编辑菜单和</i><i>peek</i><i>。</i>用户会困惑，当这两个功能在一个项目中时，系统会很难察觉意图。附加指南参见【Edit Menus】</p><p><b>Provide action buttons when appropriate.</b> Not every peek needs action buttons, but they’re a\ngreat way to offer shortcuts for common tasks. If your app already provides\ncustom touch-and-hold actions for items, it’s good practice to include the same\nactions during peeks.</p><p>适当时提供动作按钮。不是每一个peek都需要动作按钮，但是这是一个给常见任务提供捷径的好方式。如果您的app已经为项目提供了传统的长按动作，在peek中包括同样的动作是很好的。</p><p><b>Avoid providing an action button that opens a peeked item.</b> People generally press deeper to open an item they’re\npeeking. As a result, there’s typically no need to provide an explicit Open\nbutton.</p><p><i>避免提供一个动作按钮来打开一个被戳开的项目。</i>在peek视图中，人们通常更用力按压来打开项目。所以，不需要再提供一个明晃晃的打开按钮。</p><p><b>Don’t make peek the only way to perform item actions.</b> Not every device supports peek and pop, and some\npeople may turn off 3D Touch. Your app should provide other ways to trigger\nitem actions in situations like these. For example, your app could mirror a\npeek’s quick actions in a view that appears while touching and holding an item.</p><p><i>不要让</i><i>peek</i><i>成为运行动作的唯一方法。</i>不是每一台设备都支持peekpop，并且有些人还会关闭3D Touch。您的app应该提供在这些情境下其他触发动作的方式。例如，您的app可以镜像peek的快捷动作在一个长按就会出现的视图中。</p><h3>Live Photos</h3><p>Apps can incorporate pressure into the\nphoto viewing experience by supporting Live Photos. Live Photos come to life\nwhen you press them, using movement and sound to show the moments just before\nand after the photo was taken. For design guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/technologies/live-photos/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Live Photos</a>.</p><p><b>Live Photos</b></p><p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\nApp可以通过支持Live Photos将压力融入照片查看体验。当您按压Live Photos，他们就活过来了，用动作和声音来展示照片拍摄前后的瞬间。<br/></p><p><b>Accessibility无障碍</b><br/></p><p>iOS offers extensive accessibility features for users with vision loss, hearing loss, and other disabilities. Most UIKit-based apps can be made accessible with very little effort, allowing more people to use your app while providing an equally engaging experience for all.</p><p>iOS为视障、听障以及其他残疾人士提供广泛的无障碍特性。大多数基于UIKit设计的app可以通过很小的努力做到无障碍，使得更过人用上您的app，同时为所有人提供同样引人入胜的体验。</p><p><b>Provide alternative text labels for images, icons, and interface elements.</b> Alternative text labels aren’t visible onscreen, but they let VoiceOver audibly describe what&#39;s onscreen, making navigation easier for people with visual impairments.</p><p><i>为图片、图标和界面元素提供可替换的文字标签。</i>可替换的文字标签在屏幕上是看不到的，但是他们可以通过VoiceOver描述屏幕上有什么，为听障人士提供更便利的导航。</p><p><b>Respond to accessibility preferences.</b> If your app uses UIKit to implement its user interface, text and interface elements automatically adapt to certain accessibility preferences, such as bold and larger text. Your app should also check and respond to accessibility preferences when appropriate, such as when the option to reduce motion is enabled. Apps implementing custom fonts should attempt to match the accessibility behavior of the system fonts.</p><p><i>对无障碍偏好做出回应。</i>如果您的app使用UIKit构建用户界面，文字和界面元素会自动适配某种无障碍偏好，例如加粗、加大字号的文字。您的app应该也在恰当的时候适配无障碍偏好，例如当减少运动的选项被选中。使用个性化字体的app应该试着适配系统字体的无障碍行为。</p><p><b>Test your app with accessibility features.</b> In addition to text and motion changes, accessibility options can change contrast, invert colors, reduce transparency, and more. Enable these settings and observe how your app will look and behave for people who enable these features.</p><p><i>测试您app的无障碍偏好。</i>除了对于文字和运动的改变，无障碍选项还能改变对比度，反转颜色，减少透明度以及更多。打开这些设置并且观察您的app在开启这些选项时看上去怎么样，有什么行为。</p><p><b>Include closed captions and audio descriptions.</b> Closed captions allow the deaf and hard-of-hearing to perceive spoken dialogue and other audible content in videos. Audio descriptions provide spoken narration of important video content for the visually impaired.</p><p><i>包含隐藏字幕和音频描述。</i>隐藏字幕使失聪人士和听障人士感知到口语和其他视频中的音频内容。音频描述为视障人士提供重要的音频内容口语描述。</p><p>For more information, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//www.apple.com/accessibility/ios/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">iOS Accessibility</a> and <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/UserExperience/Conceptual/iPhoneAccessibility/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Accessibility Programming Guide for iOS</a>.</p><p><b>Audio（音频）</b><br/></p><p>Whether sound is a primary aspect of your app’s experience or an embellishment, you need to know how people expect sound to behave and meet those expectations.</p><p>无论声音是您app体验的基础方面还是一个点缀，您需要知道人们是如何期待声音行为并且符合他们的期望。</p><p>Users manipulate sound through the volume buttons, silence switch, headphone controls, and the onscreen volume slider. Many third-party accessories include sound controls too. Audio can be output through internal or external speakers, headphones, and even wirelessly through an AirPlay-enabled or Bluetooth device.</p><p>用户通过声音按钮、静音开关、线控以及屏幕上的声音滑动条来操控声音。声音可以通过内部或者外部扬声器、耳机甚至通过AirPlay或者蓝牙无线播放。</p><p><i>Silence.</i> People switch their device to silent to avoid being interrupted by unexpected sounds, such as ringtones and incoming message sounds. They also want nonessential sounds disabled, including keyboard sounds, sound effects, game soundtracks, and other audible feedback. When the device is set to silent, only explicitly initiated sounds should occur, such as audio during media playback, alarms, and audio/video messaging.</p><p><i>安静。</i>人们将设备调至静音模式，避免被意外的声音打扰，比如铃声或者来消息的提示音。他们也希望把不重要的声音都关掉，包括键盘音，音效，游戏背景音乐，以及其他音效反馈。当设备调至静音状态，只有明确启动的声音可以出现，比如媒体回放时的声音，闹钟以及音频\\视频消息。</p><p><i>Volume.</i> Whether using physical device buttons or an onscreen slider, people expect changes in volume to affect all sound systemwide, including music and in-app sound effects. The only exception is the ringer volume, which is always adjusted separately when audio isn’t actively playing.</p><p><i>音量。</i>无论使用物理按键还是屏幕滑条，人们希望声音变化是对整个声音系统有效，包括音乐和app内的音效。唯一的例外是来电铃声音量，总是在音频没有主动播放时独立调整。</p><p><i>Headphones.</i> People use headphones to hear sound privately and to free their hands. When plugging in headphones, users expect sound to reroute automatically without interruption. When unplugging headphones, they expect playback to pause immediately.</p><p><i>耳机。</i>人们使用耳机来私密地听声音，解放双手。当插入耳机时，用户期待声音可以立刻自动连接不被打断。当拔出耳机时，他们希望播放的音频立刻暂停。</p><p><b>Adjust levels automatically when necessary, but not the overall volume.</b> Your app can adjust relative, independent volume levels to achieve a great mix of audio. However, the final output should always be governed by the system volume.</p><p><i>必要时自动调整音量，但不是全局音量。</i>您的app可以相对调整，独立的音量来达成音频的美妙混合。然而，最终的输出音量必须一直被系统音量掌控。</p><p><b>Permit rerouting of audio when appropriate.</b> People often want to select a different audio output device. For example, they may want to listen to music through their living room stereo, car radio, or Apple TV. Support this capability unless there’s a compelling reason not to.</p><p><i>适当时候允许音频重新路由。</i>人们经常想选择一个不同的音频输出设备。例如，他们可能想通过他们的起居室音响、汽车广播或者Apple TV听音乐。请支持这项功能，除非您有很有说服力的理由不做这件事。</p><p><b>Use the system-provided volume view to allow audio adjustments.</b> The best way to provide interface controls for adjusting audio is to use a volume view. This view is customizable, includes a volume-level slider, and even includes a control for rerouting audio output. For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/mediaplayer/mpvolumeview\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">MPVolumeView</a>.</p><p><i>使用系统提供的音量视图来允许音频调整。</i>提供音频调整界面的最佳方式就是使用音量视图。这个视图是可以定制的，包括一个音量级别滑条，甚至包括一个控制条来重新路由音频输出。</p><p><b>Use the system’s sound services for short sounds and vibrations.</b> For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/audiotoolbox/1657326-system_sound_services\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">System Sound Services</a>.</p><p><i>短促的声音和振动请使用系统声音服务。</i></p><p><b>Categorize your audio if sound is essential to your app.</b> Different audio categories allow sounds to be silenced by the silence switch, to mix with other audio, or to play while your app is in the background. Pick a category based on its meaning and the current audio state of the device, and assign it to your audio sessions. For example, don’t make people stop listening to music from another app if you don’t need to. In general, it’s best to avoid changing the category while your app is running, with the exception of apps that record and playback audio at different times. For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/Audio/Conceptual/AudioSessionProgrammingGuide/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Audio Session Programming Guide</a>.</p><p><i>如果声音对您app很重要，请分类。</i>不同的音频分类允许声音被静音开关静音，与其他音频混合，或者当您的app在后台运行时播放。基于它的意义以及设备当前的音频状态，挑选一个类别，并将它分配到您的音频区域。例如，非必要时，不要让人停止从另一个app听音乐。总的来说，最好在您的app运行时避免改变类别，除了那些在不同场合下录音和播放的app。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-854b210df74c6f7cec6b87349570cbc4_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"1046\" data-rawheight=\"790\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"1046\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-854b210df74c6f7cec6b87349570cbc4_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;1046&#39; height=&#39;790&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"1046\" data-rawheight=\"790\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"1046\" data-original=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-854b210df74c6f7cec6b87349570cbc4_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic1.zhimg.com/v2-854b210df74c6f7cec6b87349570cbc4_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p><b>Resume audio playback when appropriate after an interruption occurs.</b> Sometimes, currently playing audio is interrupted by audio from a different app. Temporary interruptions such as incoming phone calls are considered resumable. Permanent interruptions, such as a music playlist initiated by Siri, are considered nonresumable. When a resumable interruption occurs, your app should resume playback when the interruption ends if audio was actively playing when the interruption started. For example, a game playing a soundtrack and a media app in the process of playing audio should both resume. An app not playing audio when an interruption occurs has nothing to resume.<br/></p><p><i>适当时，在被突然打断之后继续音频播放。</i>有时候，当前播放的音频被另一个app的声音打断。暂时的打断，比如呼入的电话，被视为可以继续的。永久的打断，比如一个Siri开启的音乐列表，被视为不可继续的。当一个可继续的打断发生时，如果在打断发生时您的音频在主动播放，那么当打断结束时，您的app应该继续播放。例如，一个游戏播放音轨和一个视频app在播放音频的过程中都应该继续。当打断发生时，一个不播放音频的app没有什么可以继续播放的。</p><p><b>Let other apps know when your app finishes playing temporary audio.</b> If your app might temporarily interrupt the audio of other apps, it should flag audio sessions appropriately so other apps get notified when it’s safe to resume. For implementation details, see the <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/avfoundation/avaudiosessionsetactiveoptions/avaudiosessionsetactiveoptionnotifyothersondeactivation\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">AVAudioSessionSetActiveOptionNotifyOthersOnDeactivation</a> constant in<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/reference/avfoundation\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">AVFoundation</a>.</p><p><i>当您的app结束播放暂时音频时，让其他app知道。</i>如果您的app可能暂时打断其他app的音频，它应该恰当地标记音频分类，这样其他app就能知道什么时候可以继续播放。</p><p><b>Respond to audio controls only when it makes sense.</b> People can control audio playback from outside of your app’s interface, such as in Control Center or with controls on their headphones, regardless of whether your app is in the foreground or background. If your app is actively playing audio, in a clear audio-related context, or connected to an AirPlay-enabeld device, it’s fine to respond to audio controls. Otherwise, your app shouldn&#39;t halt another app’s audio that may be playing when a control is activated.</p><p><i>只有当操作有意义时才回应音频控制。</i>人们可能在app界面之外的操控音频，例如控制中心或者线控，无论您的app在前台运行或者在后台。如果您的app正在主动播放音频，一个清晰的音频相关的语境，或者连接到能使用AirPlay的设备，回应音频控制是正确的。否则，当控制被激发，您的app不应该将另一个可能正在播放的app的音频暂停。</p><p><b>Don’t repurpose audio controls.</b> People expect audio controls to behave consistently in all apps. Never redefine the meaning of an audio control. If your app doesn’t support certain controls, then it simply shouldn’t respond to them.</p><p><i>不要重新规划音频控制。</i>人们期望所有app的音频控制行为一致。永远不要重新定义音频控制的意义。如果您的app不支持某种控制，那就只是不要回应那些操作好了。</p><br/><p><b>Authentication认证</b></p><p>Ask users to authenticate only in exchange for value, such as personalizing the experience, accessing additional features, purchasing content, or synchronizing data. If your app requires authentication, keep the sign-in process quick, easy, and unobtrusive, so it doesn’t detract from the enjoyment of your app.</p><p>只有在交换值时向用户要求认证，例如自定义体验，获取附加特性，购买内容或者同步数据。如果您的app要求认证，保持登陆流程快速、简单并且不显眼，这样它就不会减损您app的乐趣。</p><p><b>Delay sign-in as long as possible.</b> People often abandon apps when they are forced to sign in before doing anything useful. Give them a chance to fall in love with your app before making a commitment to it. In a shopping app, let people browse your merchandise immediately upon launch and require sign-in only when they&#39;re ready to make a purchase. In a media streaming app, let people explore your content and see what you have to offer before signing in to play something.</p><p><i>尽可能推迟登陆。</i>当人们在做任何有用的事之前就被强迫登陆时，人们经常会放弃使用该app。在让用户做出承诺之前，先给他们爱上您的app的机会。在一个购物app中，让人们在一启动时就能立刻浏览您的商品，然后只有在他们决定购物时要求登陆。在一个流媒体app中，让人们在为了播放某物而登陆之前浏览您的内容，看看您提供了什么。</p><p><b>Explain the benefits of authentication and how to sign up for your service.</b> If your app requires authentication, display a brief, friendly explanation on the login screen that describes the reasons for the requirement and its benefits. Also, remember that not everyone using your app has an account from the start. Make sure you explain how to get one, or provide a simple in-app way to sign up.</p><p><i>解释认证的好处以及如何登陆您的服务。</i>如果您的app要求认证，在登陆页上展示一个简洁友好的解释，描述这些要求的原因以及他的好处。同时，要记得并不是每一个人在刚开始用您的app时就有账户的。确认您解释了如何获得账户，或者提供一个app内的简单方式来注册。</p><p><b>Minimize data entry by showing appropriate keyboards.</b> When asking for an email address, for example, show the email keyboard screen, which includes helpful data entry shortcuts.</p><p><i>通过展示合适的键盘最小化数据输入。</i>例如，当要求一个电子邮箱地址时，展示包含有用的数据输入捷径的邮箱键盘。</p><p><b>Data Entry数据输入</b></p><p>Whether tapping interface elements or using the keyboard, inputting information can be a tedious process. When an app slows down the process by asking for lots of input before doing anything useful, people can get discouraged quickly, and may even abandon the app entirely.</p><p>无论是点击界面元素或者使用键盘，输入信息都是一个乏味的过程。当一个app在做任何有用的事情之前，就通过要求输入很多东西让使用流程放缓，人们可能很快感到灰心，甚至彻底放弃这个app。</p><p><b>When possible, present choices.</b> Make data entry as efficient as possible. Consider using a picker or table instead of a text field, for example, because it’s easier to choose from a list of predefined options than to type a response.</p><p><i>如果可能，展示选项。</i>让数据输入尽可能高效。例如，考虑使用选择器或者表格，而不是文本框。因为从一列预设的选项中挑选比打字输入回应要简单。</p><p><b>Get information from the system whenever possible.</b> Don’t force people to provide information that can be gathered automatically or with the user&#39;s permission, such as contact or calendar information.</p><p><i>尽可能从系统中获取信息。</i>不要强迫人们提供能自动收集或者需要用户允许的信息，例如通讯录或者日历信息。</p><p><b>Provide reasonable default values.</b> To the extent possible, prefill fields with the most likely values. Providing good defaults minimizes decision making and speeds up the process.</p><p><i>提供有道理的默认值。</i>尽可能用最可能的值预填充。提供好的默认值能最小化做决定所需时间而且加快流程。</p><p><b>Enable advancement only after collecting required values.</b> Before enabling a Next or Continue button, make sure all required fields have values. Use the enablement of the button as a visual cue that it’s time to proceed.</p><p><i>只有在收集好所有需要的值时允许继续。</i>在执行一个“下一个”或者“继续”按钮之前，确认所有需要的字段都有值。用按钮的可用性作为一个视觉提示，来表明可以继续。</p><p><b>Dynamically validate field values.</b> It’s frustrating when you have to go back and correct mistakes after filling out a lengthy form. Whenever possible, check field values immediately after entry so users can correct them right away.</p><p><i>动态验证字段值。</i>填完一个冗长的表单之后，您又不得不回头去改错，这是很让人沮丧的。尽可能在输入之后立刻检查字段值，这样用户可以马上修改。</p><p><b>Require field values only when necessary.</b> Use required fields only for information that is truly necessary to proceed.<br/></p><p><i>只在必要时要求字段值。</i>只在继续流程真正需要时才使用要求字段。</p><p><b>Ease navigation through value lists.</b> Especially in tables and pickers, it should be easy to pick a value. Consider sorting value lists alphabetically or in another logical manner that facilities speedy scanning and selection.</p><p><i>在值列表中轻松导航。</i>特别是在表格和挑选器中，应该很容易挑选值。考虑按照字母顺序或者其他逻辑顺序排列值，这有益于快速浏览挑选。</p><p><b>Show a hint in a text field to help communicate purpose.</b> A text field can contain placeholder text—such as &#34;Email&#34; or &#34;Password&#34;—when there’s no other text in the field. Don’t use a separate label to describe a text field when placeholder text is sufficient.</p><p><i>在文本域中显示提示以帮助沟通。</i>当域中没有其他文本时，文本域中可以包含当位文本，比如“Email”或者“Password”。当占位文本够用时，不要用单独的标签来描述文本域。</p><p><b>Feedback反馈</b><br/></p><p>Feedback helps people know what an app is doing, discover what they can do next, and understand the results of actions.</p><p>反馈帮助人们知道app在做什么，发现他们下一步可以做什么，理解动作的结果。</p><p><b>Unobtrusively integrate status and other types of feedback into your interface.</b> Ideally, users can get important information without taking action or being interrupted. Mail, for example, subtly displays status information in the toolbar while navigating through mailboxes of messages. This information doesn’t compete with the primary content onscreen, but can be checked at any time with a quick glance.</p><p>不引人注意地将状态和其他种类的反馈整合进您的界面。理想状态下，用户可以在不采取行动或者不被打扰的情况下获取重要信息。例如邮箱应用，当用户在邮箱邮件中浏览时，只是默默地将状态信息显示在工具栏。这个信息不会与屏幕上的基本信息争抢，但是可以在人数时候被一眼看到。</p><p><b>Avoid unnecessary alerts.</b> An alert is a powerful feedback mechanism, but should be used only to deliver important—and ideally actionable—information. If people see too many alerts that don’t contain essential information, they quickly learn to ignore future alerts. For additional guidance, see<a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/ui-views/alerts/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Alerts</a>.</p><p>避免不必要的警告。警告是一种很有力度的反馈机制，但是应该仅用在传达重要的，最好是可操作的信息。如果人们看到太多不包含重要信息的警告，他们很快会学会忽视以后的警告。</p><p><b>Haptic Feedback</b><b>触觉反馈</b><br/></p><p>On supported devices, haptics provide a way to physically engage users with tactile feedback that gets attention and reinforces actions. Some system-provided interface elements, such as pickers, switches, and sliders, automatically provide haptic feedback as users interact with them. Your app can also ask the system to generate different types of haptic feedback. iOS manages the strength and behavior of this feedback.</p><p>在支持的设备上，触觉提供一种方式，用触觉反馈在物理上吸引用户，获得警告，加强动作。一些系统提供的界面元素，在用户与之交互时自动提供触觉反馈，例如挑选器，开关，滑条。您的app也可以让系统触发不同种类的触觉反馈。iOS管理这种反馈的强度和行为。</p><figure><noscript><img src=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bac07a4f0b818043581d86d82f19b6d7_b.png\" data-rawwidth=\"597\" data-rawheight=\"415\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb\" width=\"597\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bac07a4f0b818043581d86d82f19b6d7_r.jpg\"/></noscript><img src=\"data:image/svg+xml;utf8,&lt;svg xmlns=&#39;http://www.w3.org/2000/svg&#39; width=&#39;597&#39; height=&#39;415&#39;&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;\" data-rawwidth=\"597\" data-rawheight=\"415\" class=\"origin_image zh-lightbox-thumb lazy\" width=\"597\" data-original=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bac07a4f0b818043581d86d82f19b6d7_r.jpg\" data-actualsrc=\"https://pic4.zhimg.com/v2-bac07a4f0b818043581d86d82f19b6d7_b.png\"/></figure><br/><p><b>Use haptic judiciously.</b> Overuse can cause confusion, diminish the significance of feedback, and even have a negative impact on battery life.</p><p>明智地使用触觉反馈。滥用会引起困惑，减少触觉反馈的意义，甚至给电池寿命带来副作用。</p><p><b>In general, provide haptic feedback in response to user-initiated actions.</b> It’s easy for people to correlate haptics with actions they initiated. Arbitrary feedback can feel disconnected and be misinterpreted.</p><p>总的来说，对用户发出的动作提供触觉反馈。人们很容易将他们发出的动作与触觉反馈联系起来。随意的反馈会让人觉得断开连接，不被理解。</p><p><b>Don’t redefine feedback types.</b> To ensure a consistent experience, use feedback types as intended. Don’t, for example, use &#34;impact&#34; feedback to notify the user that a task has succeeded. Instead, use the &#34;success&#34; variation of &#34;notification&#34; feedback.</p><p>不要重新定义反馈类型。为了确保一致的体验，使用原始的反馈类型。例如，不要用“impact”反馈来通知用户任务完成了。相反的，使用通知类型中的“success”变化来反馈。</p><p><b>Fine tune your visual experience for haptics.</b> Provide visual and haptic feedback together to create a deeper connection between actions and results. Make sure animations are sharp and precise, to visually match what the user feels.<br/></p><p>为触觉反馈微调您的视觉体验。为了在动作和结果之间创造更深的联系，同时提供视觉和触觉反馈。确认动画是清晰精准的，以在视觉上匹配用户感受到的东西。</p><p><b>Don’t rely on a single mode of communication.</b> Not all devices support the full range of haptic feedback, and people can disable the feature entirely in Settings if they choose. In addition, haptic feedback occurs only when the device is active and your app is frontmost. Supplement haptics with visual and audible cues to ensure that important information isn’t missed.</p><p>不要依赖单一的交流模式。不是所有的设备都支持所有的触觉反馈，而且人们可以选择在设置里完全关掉这个特性。另外，触觉反馈只在设备支持时出现，并且您的app是最新版的。用视觉和听觉补充触觉反馈，以保证重要信息不被错过。</p><p><b>Use haptic when visual feedback may be occluded.</b> Some interactions, such as dragging an object to a location onscreen, are hidden by the user’s finger. Consider generating feedback that lets the user know when they’ve reached a particular location or value.</p><p>当视觉反馈可能被关闭时使用触觉反馈。有些交互，例如在屏幕上拖拽物体到某处，会藏在用户手指后面。考虑触发触觉操作，让用户知道他们已经到了某个特定的地方或者值。</p><p><b>Prepare the system before initiating feedback.</b> Because there may be some latency involved when providing haptic feedback, it’s best to get the system ready shortly before requesting the feedback. Otherwise, the haptics might come too late and feel disconnected from the user&#39;s actions or what they’re seeing on the screen.</p><p>让系统触发反馈之前做好准备。因为在提供触觉反馈时可能会有一些等待时间，最好让系统在要求反馈之前不久就做好准备。否则，触觉反馈可能来的太迟，用户会感觉动作断开连接了或者与他们在屏幕上看到的失去联系。</p><p><b>Synchronize haptic with accompanying sound.</b> Haptics don’t automatically synchronize with sounds. If you want an accompanying sound, you’re responsible for synchronizing it.</p><p>同步触觉反馈和伴随的音效。触觉反馈不会自动与音效同步。如果您需要伴随的音效，您得同步它。</p><p><b>File Handling文件处理</b></p><p>People shouldn’t need to think about the file system while creating, viewing, and manipulating files. If your app works with files, downplay file handling as much as possible.</p><p>人们在创建文件、查看文件、操作文件时不应该为文件系统考虑过多。如果您的app与处理文件有关，尽可能淡化文件处理过程。</p><p><b>Instill confidence that work is always preserved unless canceled or deleted.</b> In general, don’t make people explicitly save files. Instead, save changes automatically at regular intervals, when opening and closing files, and when switching to another app. In some cases, such as while editing an existing file, save and cancel options may still make sense for the sake of confirming when the edits are actually captured.</p><p>跟用户灌输信息，他们的作品除非被取消或者删除，总是被保存的。总的来说，不要让人们特地保存文件。取而代之，当打开或者关闭文件，还有切换到另一个app时，有规律的自动保存改动。在某些情况下，例如编辑一个已存在的文件，保存和取消选项还是有意义的，用于确认编辑真的发生了。</p><p><b>Don&#39;t provide an option to create local-only files.</b> Users often expect all of their files to be available on all of their devices. Whenever possible, your app should support cloud-based file storage through a service such as iCloud.</p><p>不要提供只创造本地文件的选项。用户经常期望所有的文件在他们所有的设备上都能访问。任何可能的时候，您的app应该支持云文件，通过类似iCloud的服务。</p><p><b>Implement an intuitive and graphical file browsing interface.</b> Ideally, use the system’s familiar document picker for browsing. If you implement a custom file browser, make sure it’s intuitive and efficient. File browsers work best when they’re highly graphical, providing visual representations of files. To speed navigation, minimize gestures, and consider providing a new document button, so people don’t need to go elsewhere to create a new document.</p><p>使用直观的图形化的文件浏览界面。理想状况下，为浏览文件使用系统熟悉的文件挑选界面。如果您使用个性化的文件浏览器，确认它是直观高效的。文件浏览器在他们高度图形化，提供文件的视觉展示时最高效。为了提高浏览速度，少使用手势，考虑提供一个新建文件按钮，这样人们就不必去其他地方创建新文件了。</p><p><b>Let users preview files without leaving your app.</b> You can use Quick Look to let people view the contents of Keynote, Numbers, and Pages documents, PDFs, images, and certain other types of files, even if your app doesn’t actually open them. See <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/features/quick-look/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Quick Look</a>.<br/></p><p>让用户不必离开app就能预览文件。您可以用Quick Look让人们预览Keynote，Numbers，Pages，PDF，图片或者某种文件的文件内容，甚至您的app不需要真的打开他们。</p><p><b>When appropriate, share files with other apps.</b> If it makes sense, your app can share its files with other apps through a <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/extensions/document-providers/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">document provider extension</a>. Your app can also let people browse and open files from other apps. For implementation details, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/FileManagement/Conceptual/DocumentPickerProgrammingGuide/Introduction/Introduction.html\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Document Picker Programming Guide</a>.</p><p>适当时候，与其他app共享文件。如果有意义的话，您的app可以通过【document provider extension】与其他app共享文件。您的app可以让人们浏览、打开其他app的文件。</p><p><b>First Launch Experience初次启动体验</b><br/></p><p>Launch time is your first opportunity to onboard new users and reconnect with returning ones. Design a launch experience that’s fast, fun, and educational.</p><p>启动app时是您吸引新用户和联系回归用户的第一次机会。设计快速、有趣、带有教学意味的启动体验。</p><br/><p><b>Provide a launch screen.</b> A launch screen appears the moment your app starts, giving the impression that your app is fast and responsive, while allowing initial content to load. This screen is quickly replaced by the first screen of your app, so it is should closely resemble this screen with the exception of localizable text and interactive elements. To learn more, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/graphics/launch-screen/\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Launch Screen</a>.</p><p>提供启动页。启动页在app启动时出现，传达app快速响应的音响，当时允许初始内容加载。这一页很快就被app的第一屏取代，所以它应该酷似第一屏，除了本地文本和交互元素。</p><p><b>Launch in the appropriate orientation.</b> If your app supports both portrait and landscape modes, it should launch using the device’s current orientation. If your app only runs in one orientation, it should always launch in that orientation and let people rotate the device if necessary. Unless there’s a compelling reason not to, an app in landscape mode should orient itself correctly, regardless of whether the Home button is on the left or right. For additional guidance, see <a href=\"https://link.zhihu.com/?target=https%3A//developer.apple.com/ios/human-interface-guidelines/visual-design/layout\" class=\" wrap external\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"nofollow noreferrer\">Layout</a>.</p><p>在合适的方向启动。如果app同时支持纵向和横向模式，它应该用设备当前的方向启动。如果app只在一个方向运行，它就得一直在那个方向启动，并且必要时让人们旋转设备。除非有令人信服的理由，否则横向模式的app应该在正确方向启动，无论Home键在左边还是右边。</p><p><b>Get to the action quickly.</b> Avoid showing a splash screen, menus, and instructions that make it take longer to reach content and start using your app. Instead, let people dive right in. If your app needs tutorials or intro sequences, provide a way to skip them and don&#39;t show them to returning users.<br/></p><p>快速行动。避免显示要花更久时间以获得内容或者开始使用app的闪屏，菜单或者指导。取而代之的是，让人们直接沉浸其中。如果app需要教程或者介绍序列，提供跳过方式，并且不要显示给老用户。</p><p><b>Anticipate the need for help.</b> Proactively look for times when people might be stuck. A game, for example, could casually show useful tips when paused or when a character isn’t advancing. Let users replay tutorials in case they miss something the first time.<br/></p><p>预料帮助的需求。主动寻求人们可能卡住的时机。例如，游戏中可以在暂停时或者人物不前进时，时不时显示有用的提示。如果用户在第一次错过了一些东西，让他们重播教程。</p><p><b>Stick to the essentials in tutorials.</b> It’s fine to provide guidance for beginners, but education isn’t a substitute for great app design. First and foremost, make your app intuitive. If too much guidance is needed, revisit the design of your app.</p><p>教程中抓住重点。为初学者提供指南是好的，但是教育不是好的app设计的替代。首先，要让app直观。如果需要太多指南，重新查看app的设计吧。</p><p><b>Make learning fun and discoverable.</b> Learning by doing is a lot more fun and effective than reading a list of instructions. Use animation and interactivity to teach gradually and in context. Avoid displaying screenshots that appear interactive.<br/></p><p>让学习充满乐趣和探索性。在实践中学习比阅读一大堆指示更加有趣，更加高效。使用动画和交互在情境中逐渐教学。避免显示看上去可交互其实是截图的东西。</p><p><b>Avoid asking for setup information up front.</b> People expect apps to just work. Design your app for the majority and let the few that want a different configuration adjust settings to meet their needs. To the extent possible, derive setup information from device settings and defaults, or through a synchronization service, such as iCloud. If you must ask for setup information, prompt for it in-app the first time, and let users modify it later in your app’s settings.<br/></p><p>避免一开始就要求设置信息。人们希望app立刻就能用。为大多数人设计app并且让少数需要不同构造的人调整设置来满足需求。尽可能从设备设置和默认设置中派生设置信息，或者通过同步服务，例如iCloud。如果必须要求设置信息，首次启动时在app内提示一下，让用户稍后在app设置里设定。</p><p><b>Avoid showing in-app licensing agreements and disclaimers.</b> Let the App Store display agreements and disclaimers before your app is downloaded. If you must include these items within your app, integrate them in a balanced way that doesn’t disrupt the user experience.<br/></p><p>避免在app中显示许可协议和免责声明。在下载app之前就在App Store中显示许可协议和免责声明。如果必须在app内包括这些条款，用平衡的方式整合他们，不要打扰用户体验。</p><p><b>Restore the previous state when your app restarts.</b> Don&#39;t make people retrace steps to reach their previous location in your app. Preserve and restore your app’s state so they can continue where they left off.</p><p>当app重启时重新加载上一次的状态。不要让人们在app中沿原路找到他们之前的位置。保存并且加载app的状态，这样他们就能在离开的地方继续。</p><p><b>Don’t ask people to rate your app too quickly or too often.</b> Asking for a rating too soon or too frequently is annoying and decreases the amount of useful feedback you receive. To encourage well-considered feedback, give people time to form an opinion about your app before asking for a rating. Always provide a way to opt out of rating prompts and never force users to rate your app.</p><p>不要让用户太快太频繁地给app评分。太快或太频繁要求评分很烦人，而且会减少收到的有用反馈。为了鼓励深思熟虑的反馈，在要求评分之前，给人们点儿时间去形成关于app的意见。一直提供跳出评分要求的方式，千万不要强迫用户给app评分。</p><p><b>Don’t encourage rebooting.</b> Restarting takes time and makes your app seem unreliable and hard to use. If your app has memory or other issues that make it difficult to run unless the system has just booted, you need to address those issues.</p><p>不要让人重启。重启浪费时间而且让app看起来不靠谱又难用。除非系统重启了，如果app有内存问题或者其他问题让它难以运行，您得处理这些问题。</p>",
